
# Described Instance List
As of May 10, 2017

This is a list of Mastodon instances with descriptions and contact information. It also contains preview links, so that you can better decide which instance to join.

I have removed instances that aren't accepting open registrations. Some instances couldn't be reached, so they are left out as well. The list is sorted by server uptime percentage. This extra metadata comes from list.mastodon.xyz/instances.json, since I do not know how to query the federation myself.

You can download the full JSON database (soon) from which this report was generated.

To view stats about the instance (and visit its about page) click its name. To see a preview of toots at the instance, click "preview."

The search function of your browser might help you find the instance you're looking for.

Please note that some instances may contain offensive content!
## [social.bytesexual.net](https://social.bytesexual.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=social.bytesexual.net&view=local)
social.bytesexual.net is a Mastodon instance run by the Merry Men of bytesexual.net. All fun and no SLA since 2012. 
We run this instance for ourselves and our friends. Courteous lifeforms of all backgrounds are welcome to coexist with us.

Lead maintainer is @q3k, follow for service updates.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Bytesexual Networks is a transcontinental non-profit guerilla of {sys,net}ops specializing in shoestring budget infrastructure for Hackerspaces and other NGOs.

This instance is physically hosted in France by a hosting company registered in the same country. The maintainers of this instance are EU citizens.

We have not been served any secret court orders and are not under any gag orders.
</details>

Email: [q3k@q3k.org](mailto:q3k@q3k.org)

Admin: [@q3k@social.bytesexual.net](https://social.bytesexual.net/@q3k)

## [mastodon.link](https://mastodon.link/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.link&view=local)
Mastodon server hosted by iooner.
A+ HTTPS, hosted in France, IPv6 coming.
Trouble registering ? Send me a mail contact@mastodon.link.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>mastodon.link
Guidelines
The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of mastodon.link; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:

The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:

Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence


The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:

Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism


The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:

Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism


Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:

Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
More (in french)
Le serveur est fourni en "best effort", l'équipe d'administration fait donc de son mieux sans donner aucune garantie de service.
Nous nous réservons le droit de fermer les inscriptions au node à tout moment
Si le node venait à s'arrêter nous ferons le maximum afin de vous avertir le plus tôt possible.
</details>

Email: [contact@mastodon.link](mailto:contact@mastodon.link)

Admin: [@iooner@mastodon.link](https://mastodon.link/@iooner)

    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:

    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.

## [mastodon.notwebsite.com](https://mastodon.notwebsite.com/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.notwebsite.com&view=local)
Just another Mastodon instance. This one is run by exnilio, a software consultancy run by a goofball named Vinney Cavallo. Enjoy!

<details><summary>(more)</summary>We don't have too many rules here. As long as content isn't impeding the mechanical usage of the instance (say, excessive spam) or illegal relative to whatever local laws apply, then it's allowed. This is not a safe space. That said, we reserve the right to change this policy at any time.

I considered making every single user an admin, but that probably would break the site (I still sort of want to do it).
</details>

## [mstdn.syoriken.org](https://mstdn.syoriken.org/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.syoriken.org&view=local)
Syorikenインスタンスは、北見工業大学の情報系サークルである情報処理技術研究会内でのコミュニケーションツールとして運営されています。

会員同士のコミュニケーションは勿論のこと、OBOGの方との交流も視野に入れております。(現在非対応)

処理研の関係者であれば、誰でも利用することができます。

現在、北見工業大学のActive!mailのメールアドレスのみ登録が可能です。キャリアメールやGmail等のフリーメールアドレスは使用できません。

注意事項

現在試験運用中のため予告なく停止する場合があります
公序良俗に反する内容は書き込まないでください

お問い合わせ
何か連絡等ありましたら下記メールアドレスか連絡先まで。
syoriken@gmail.com

## [mastodon.elmit.com](https://mastodon.elmit.com/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.elmit.com&view=local)
The Twitter Killer

Welcome
Here some resources to understand Mastodon:


Welcome to Mastodon by @Gargron


Bye, Twitter. All the cool kids are migrating to Mastodon by Mashable


Rules


No illegal content. The server is hosted in France : racism, apology for terrorism, bullying, defamation, violations privacy rights and child pornograhy are illegal under French law.


No oppressive content (sexism, homophobia, etc).


No parody account.


No bot (for the moment).


Any graphical content have to contain a Content Warning.


No explicit sexual content in the public timeline without content warning (you can configure your toot privacy on "public but do not display on public timeline").


Mobile applications


Android : Tusky


iOS : Amaroq for Mastodon


Full list


Support Mastodon


The code source can be found here : Github


You can help the developer of Mastodon on Patreon


Support this instance mastodon.elmit.com

<details><summary>(more)</summary>...sponsored by Elmit
</details>

Email: [ronald+mastodon@elmit.com](mailto:ronald+mastodon@elmit.com)

## [forum.manga.tokyo](https://forum.manga.tokyo/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=forum.manga.tokyo&view=local)
A community for fans of Japanese culture, such as anime, manga, voice actors and more, operated by MANGA.TOKYO through a mastodon instance. Anybody can participate in talks about the hottest topics and the newest anime information as well as find new friends and talk to people who have the same interests.
How to make an account
To use forum.manga.tokyo you must create an account.
1. Fill in your username, e-mail address and password and click ‘Get Started’.
2. You will receive a confirmation e-mail, please confirm your account by clicking on the link in the e-mail. 
3. Log in via the Login page.
That completes your registration. 
Let's have fun!!
Forum Rules
Use hashtags when talking about specific anime/manga etc 
Use the spoiler tag ‘CW’ for spoilers 
Respect others to create a place that everybody likes to return to.
Note

Acts against the law are prohibited.
Do not infringe on the rights of others.
Do not copy or post the work of others without permission.
Do not act against public order or morals. 
Do not impersonate other people or imitate organizations etc.
Do not cause hurt or loss in any form to other people
Do not overload the server with material

※ Please note that anything you write in your toots (posts) here may be quoted on MANGA.TOKYO
Contact and Inquiries
Twitter: @manga_tokyo_
Mail: info.manga.tokyo@donika.co.jp
Terms of Use
Privacy Policy

@mangatokyo

</details>

## [cuttlefi.sh](https://cuttlefi.sh/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=cuttlefi.sh&view=local)

Cuttlefish


<details><summary>(more)</summary>By charging a small monthly amount, Cuttlefish can pay its costs and its development team a fair wage and distribute the rest back to its members.
Cuttlefish is in the early stages of formation. We have an idea of how we’d like it to operate, but are figuring out the details as we go. The answers below sketch our current thinking about the project and the direction we hope to go in the future.
Q&A
Why shouldn’t I sign up for a free social network?
You can, and if you prefer you should. Cuttlefish is an alternative that attempts to answer the question of how a social network can be run without showing you ads or selling your information. Since Cuttlefish runs inside a larger OStatus network, members can interact with a larger community of users.
Mastodon was written by volunteers, and other instances are run by volunteers as well. Why not donate your time instead of asking for money?
The progress that the maintainers and contributors to Mastodon and OStatus is impressive, and their dedication to the stewardship of these projects is admirable. Our focus is on creating a sustainable instance, and we think that means having a dedicated staff working on the project. That gives us time to devote to moderation, maintenance, and contributing back to the open source projects that are being used to run Cuttlefish. We don’t think that this would be possible if running Cuttlefish was treated as a side project.
Why not just accept donations?
Accepting donations leads to some members having undue influence in the community, because their donations are required to cover operating costs. We ask each user to contribute equally to the cost of running the service, with the hope of returning membership fees to active members.
What do you mean by active members?
At this point, just members in active standing. In the future, this might also include looking at who is posting good stuff within their local network. We realize that add more terms to unpack, and raises more questions than it resolves. Our goal is to promote a healthy community, and we will be looking at how different means of profit-sharing might help that being achieved.
How are membership fees redistributed?
Our intention is to do this on a quarterly basis, and initially by equally dividing profit between members. During the initial quarter of a membership, the amount returned will be based on the percentage of the quarter for which the membership was active.
How are the operating costs determined?
Currently we are basing our operating costs on having one developer, one community moderator, and a part-time operations manager work on the project. There are also legal issues that require counsel that will need to be addressed in the initial months of operation. We estimate operating costs for the first month to be around twelve thousand US dollars. We will be publishing our actual operating costs quarterly, and revising that estimate to account changes in staffing.
Who is running this instance?
Cuttlefish is currently solely sponsored by the team at Standard Library, a small development firm that works inside of the cultural sector. We have a strong experience in building and maintaining Rails applications.
</details>

Email: [cuttlefishcoop@gmail.com](mailto:cuttlefishcoop@gmail.com)

Admin: [@root@cuttlefi.sh](https://cuttlefi.sh/@root)

## [social.ponyfrance.net](https://social.ponyfrance.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=social.ponyfrance.net&view=local)
Une instance francophone ouverte aux fans de poneys !
N'oubliez pas de lire nos règles sur la page des détails.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>
	Bienvenue, ceci est l'instance Mastodon installée et maintenue par Pony France.


	Envie d'en savoir plus sur Mastodon ? Alda a écrit un très bon article, en français, sur son blog : "Welcome to Mastodon".
	Une FAQ en anglais est disponible sur mastoguide.info.


Cette instance et alternatives

	Ici, vous pourrez obtenir un compte au format "@PSEUDO@ponyfrance.net". Vous pouvez rejoindre n'importe quel instance ouverte et suivre les utilisateurs des autres sites. Une liste est disponible ici.



	On vous propose aussi d'autres instances francophone :



equestria.social
Un autre réseau pour les fans de poneys.
	

witches.town
Un endroit accueillant pour les personnes queers, féministes, anarchistes et compagnie ainsi qu'à leur sympathisant⋅e⋅s.
	

mstdn.paris
Pour les Parisien⋅ne⋅s.
	

social.bzh
Pour les Breton⋅ne⋅s.
	

mapicardie.fr
Vive les Picard⋅e⋅s.
	



Règles de base

	Il va bien falloir instaurer quelques règles pour s'assurer que tout le monde puisse s'entendre. Sachez que l'expression qui va bien est Don't be a d*ck.
	En cas de problèmes, signalez les messages et comptes avec la fonction "Signaler..." dans le menu du message.


Restez civil, respectez les autres personnes et leurs choix
Evitez le flood et le spam
Utilisez la fonction NSFW et les spoilers (bouton CW) si nécessaire, dans la limite des rềgles

		Il n'est pas permi de poster...
		
De la pornographie, y compris en dessin (la nuditée est permise, mais NSFW + CW)
Du contenu gore, vore, homophobe et xénophobe
Ce qui n'est pas légal en France (oui, les lolis aussi)





	Concernants les comptes permis sur cette instance...


Le comptes liés a des entitées à but lucratif ne sont pas autorisés
Les robots sont permis après demande et acceptation par l'équipe.

		Les comptes parodiques sont autorisés avec les conditions suivantes :
		
Le nom du compte doit avoir un point d'ironie, ؟
La description du compte doit faire mention qu'il s'agit d'un compte parodique

## [insoumis-es.net](https://insoumis-es.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=insoumis-es.net&view=local)
Bastion insoumis et libre dont l'objectif est de porter le programme "l'avenir en commun" de la France insoumise. Résistance!

Ce serveur est une initiative personnelle indépendante, bénévole et autonome de toute organisation ou parti.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Regles d'usage du serveur mastodon insoumis-es.net

Notre instance est bien sûr régie par des règles spécifiques. En la rejoignant l'utilisateur accepte expressément ces regles :

Premièrement aucun sexisme, racisme, homophobie validisme, âgisme, grossophobie ou psychophobie, etc n’est toléré. Tout message de haine est proscrit, les fascistes et leurs copains nazis sont directement bannis.
Toute provocation, tout propos ou contenu à caractère illicite et/ou pornographique est prohibé.
Tout sujet polémique à l'encontre d’un de nos membres, de notre serveur, de la France Insoumise ou de Jean-Luc Mélenchon est également prohibé.
insoumis-es.net prône la laïcité, il est donc autorisé de débattre à propos des religions tant que le respect des croyances (ou non) de chacune et chacun est respecté.
Cette instance Mastodon se veut inclusive et bienveillante, ainsi nous bannirons sans prévenir et sans regret. Les comptes bannis ne sont plus accessibles depuis notre instance, vous ne pouvez plus voir leur contenu ni les suivre.
Nous encourageons nos utilisateur-ice-s à utiliser la fonction de rapport (“Report”) pour nous faire part du contenu et/ou des comptes allant à l’encontre de nos règles. D'ailleurs si celles-ci ne vous conviennent pas, ne râlez pas, trouvez simplement un autre serveur.
Notre réseau social, et son réseau entier selon nous, est dédié à la réappropriation des moyens de communication et à la création de communautés meilleures pour le collectif.
La divulgation de données personnelles ou de messages privés est strictement interdite
Tout partage de contenu dans le but de le "disliker" est interdit.
Toute insulte ou manque de respect envers les autres membres de insoumis-es.net est prohibé.
Le flood peu importe sa nature est strictement interdit.
Tout comportement et propos à caractère violent ou insultant, physique ou vocal, est également prohibé, même sous le couvert de l’humour.
Veuillez faire un effort dans l'écriture : le langage sms est à éviter.
Veuillez faire un effort de tenue dans votre langage : un usage abusif de grossièretés sera sanctionné.
Les pseudos ne doivent pas contenir exclusivement de majuscules

Ces règles ont été inspirées par celles de unixcorn.xyz ainsi que de la charte du discord insoumis, merci à eux.
</details>

Email: [admin@insoumis-es.net](mailto:admin@insoumis-es.net)

Admin: Not Available

## [writing.exchange](https://writing.exchange/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=writing.exchange&view=local)
Writing Exchange is a small, focused community for poets, writers, bloggers, and anyone else who makes things. It was started by Matt from Write.as.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>We're an inclusive community that welcomes all, as long as you're kind and respectful to others. We aim to provide an environment where you feel comfortable enough to participate freely and authentically. If you're not interested in that, there are plenty of other great instances you can join.
Guidelines
We'll be more specific in the future, but in general, be good to each other. Enjoy talking to strangers (and friends!) on the internet, and give people the benefit of the doubt.
If problems arise, please use Mastodon's features to Block, Mute, or Report users that are causing problems. If you need more help, contact @matt.
Background
This is an experiment to see if we can create a small, purposeful community among the Mastodon fediverse, with the eventual goal being a sustainable, community-run instance. If you'd like to help make that happen, get in touch.

## [mstdn.tokyocameraclub.com](https://mstdn.tokyocameraclub.com/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.tokyocameraclub.com&view=local)
mstdn.tokyocameraclub.comは東京カメラ部が運営するMastodonのインスタンス（サーバー）です。 「カメラがある暮らし」をより楽しくすることを目的として、写真や動画などを投稿・閲覧するためのグループです。こちらの趣旨に賛同いただける方はどなたでも無料で参加いただけます。

運営方針

東京カメラ部の公式アカウントではMastodon、Facebook、Instagramなどから東京カメラ部とその分室に投稿いただいた作品の一部を適宜紹介させていただきます。

Mastodonでの東京カメラ部への投稿は投稿にハッシュタグ「#tokyocameraclub」を付けていただくだけで完了します。

その他運営方針はFacebookの東京カメラ部と同等となりますので、詳しくはそちらをご覧ください。

http://app.minpos.com/fb/willvii/camera_jpn/static/faq/

禁止行為

著作権違反など日本国の法律に違反するする行為
他者の人格、作品を誹謗中傷する行為
実在の組織、団体、人格などになりすます行為
公序良俗に反する行為
無闇にサーバーの負荷を高める行為
禁止行為を行う方はアカウントを停止させていただく場合があります

注意事項

確認メールが届くまで時間がかかるときがあります
1－2時間たっても確認メールが届かない場合は迷惑メールに分類されている可能性があります。お手数ですが迷惑メールフォルダーを確認なさってください。
本インスタンスは試験運用中です。予告なくメンテナンス実施、データリセット、サービス終了がなされる可能性はあります。

連絡先

camera.jpn@tokyocameraclub.com

Business e-mail:




</details>

## [social.bytestemplar.com](https://social.bytestemplar.com/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=social.bytestemplar.com&view=local)

social.bytestemplar.com


<details><summary>(more)</summary>We're open registration; free for all! Just be cool, or I'll stab you in the soul.
STOLEN FROM mastodon.social:
The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of mastodon.social; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Admin: [@Fortyseven@social.bytestemplar.com](https://social.bytestemplar.com/@Fortyseven)

## [mastodon.acc.umu.se](https://mastodon.acc.umu.se/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.acc.umu.se&view=local)
mastodon.acc.umu.se is run by the Academic Computer Club at Umeå University located in Umeå, Sweden. 

Currently registration is only open to users affiliated with Umeå University so please use your university email when signing up!


<details><summary>(more)</summary>WELCOME TO MASTODON@ACC!
ACC is actively involved in several open source projects and we provide mirrors for Debian, Ubuntu, Gnome and GIMP. We also host servers for the Gimpnet, Freenode, and OFTC IRC networks.
You can read more about our projects and our servers on the ACC website.
Please read over our general usage policy and code of conduct. We hope you'll be happy here, but if you feel it's too strict, there are many other instances to choose from.
General Usage
Accounts on mastodon.acc.umu.se are for personal use only; commercial use is not allowed. If you need Mastodon for your business, why not run your own? :)
We ask that you comply with the rules and usage policy of the Academic Computer Club (ACC):(in English) (i Svenska)
You may not post (or boost/repost):

material illegal under Swedish laws
material against the rules of SUNET
material in breach of the copyright act
material that may damage ACC's public image or its relations with authorities and other institutions
It's the final decision of ACC to judge what material may damage our public relations and take suitable action, which may include removal of the material and suspension of your account.
Code of Conduct
Please remember you're in a public area and what you say here may reach millions of people, many of whom have backgrounds and values that differ from yours; take a moment before posting and think about ways your message may be misunderstood.
You may not use services hosted by ACC to violate another person's integrity. This includes compiling and posting personal information about another person, posting personal communications from a person without their permission, or sending harassing or abusive messages.
Taking part in online interaction obliges the user to comply with the current rules and conventions for computer and net usage (see: netiquette). On Mastodon, this includes using CW and NSFW functions and choosing an appropriate level of public display for your posts.
If you see content which you believe is in breach of these rules, please report it for review.
Federation
mastodon.acc.umu.se federates freely with all other Mastodon and GNU social instances in the network. Federation is a network service and suspension of federation with another server will only be implemented as a last resort in cases of technical difficulties or hostile or malicious activity. If we need to suspend federation with another instance, it will be noted here.
Currently not federating with: none
Privacy
ACC will do its best to respect individual privacy, but please remember that nothing on the internet is really private and consider anything you say saved forever. Mastodon is not a secure channel for sensitive communication.
Staff may examine user accounts hosted on the association's equipment if they suspect activity that conflicts with the association's rules.

Last updated: 2017-04-28
</details>

Email: [mastodon@acc.umu.se](mailto:mastodon@acc.umu.se)

Admin: [@maswan@mastodon.acc.umu.se](https://mastodon.acc.umu.se/@maswan)

## [thepractice.space](https://thepractice.space/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=thepractice.space&view=local)
Welcome! The Practice Space is a Mastodon server dedicated to musicians of all stripes, nations, and genres. It's a social network focused on discussing all aspects of being a musician—theory, gigging, songwriting, you name it. You can also connect with people on most other Mastodon servers to expand your network even more!


<details><summary>(more)</summary>The Goals
The aim of The Practice Space is to be both a fun and a useful community for musicians. To do that, we (the admins/moderators) lean towards being positive and protecting those who have less opportunity to express themselves.
The Rules
When in doubt, report and/or ask us. We go with the mastodon.social rules as a guideline. We are not hesitant about banning bad actors for the health of the overall community.
The Practice Space follows the witches.town federation blocklist.
Make Use of Content Warnings
If it's sensitive, graphic, NSFW, or potentially distressing, put it behind a content warning. It's why we have them. That includes text and graphics; if you're not sure, use one.
No Hating On Genre/Style
The Practice Space is for all kinds of musicians. If something isn't your jam, there's no need to cause conflict over it. Just move along.
Be Kind to Newbies
Both new musicians and new members to the server. We were all new once! (That said, being new isn't an excuse to not learn.)
Be Sensible with Promotion
It's totally fine to promote your band, gigs, whatever! It's even encouraged. But if people are asking you to tone it down, take their advice. The rules are stricter when what's being promoted doesn't relate to music.
No Harassment
If someone says cut it out, cut it out. No debate.
Nazi Punks Fuck Off
Says it all.
Disclaimer
This server is an experiment. It might break, it might go away. Things may change, rapidly and/or dramatically. I'll do my best to keep things from getting crazy, and I'll always give warning when I can.
</details>

Email: [zoe@leporidaemedia.com](mailto:zoe@leporidaemedia.com)

Admin: [@hupfen@thepractice.space](https://thepractice.space/@hupfen)

## [masto.themimitoof.fr](https://masto.themimitoof.fr/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=masto.themimitoof.fr&view=local)
Masto.themimitoof.fr is an instance by themimitoof.fr. Join us on this great community!



Masto.themimitoof.fr est une instance par themimitoof.fr. Rejoignez-nous sur cette belle communauté !

<details><summary>(more)</summary>
    /* Yes I know.. It's so bad here but it's needed :/ */

    ul.li li { margin-bottom: 2px; }
    h3 { margin-top: 8px; }

(French) Bienvenue sur Mastodon !
🌎 Click here if you likely to scroll to the English version

Bienvenue sur cette instance gérée par themimitoof. Cette instance a pour but de contribuer à la création du réseau Mastodon.

Quelques règles pour bien vivre

Toutes les langues sont autorisées sur cette instance
Evitez le flood/spam
Merci d'utiliser la fonction NSFW lorsqu'il s'agit d'un contenu partiellement autorisé
Il est strictement interdit de parler/poster du contenu :
        
à caractère sexuel (ce qui est en revanche autorisée : l'art (par exemple : une femme ou un homme dénudé·e peint·e, une statue), pas d'organe génital apparent (privilégiez tout de même l'utilisation de la fonction NFSW).)
insulter, discriminer, violence verbale, menacer, chantage, harceler et tout ce qui a un lien avec la cyberviolence
parler de sujets sensibles (réligieux, terrorisme, etc...)


Comptes parodiques autorisés. Veuillez juste le signaler.
Aucun compte ne sera clos sans une bonne raison
Nous sommes bénévoles, merci de respecter notre engagement
Amusez-vous et faites-vous de nouveaux amis 🙂

Rétention des données
La loi demande à ce que les données de connexion soient conservées 1 an. Parmi, ces informations, nous stockons :

Votre adresse IP
Votre nom d'utilisateur
Les appels serveurs
La date de la requête



Ses données permettront en cas de problème, de retrouver toute piste en cas de litige.

Droit à l'oubli
Pour le moment, il est impossible de supprimer un compte d'une instance mais il est en revanche possible de suspendre son compte.
En attendant que cette fonctionnalité soit disponible, nous proposons aux utilisateurs de faire une demande de suspension de compte avec l'ajout de votre adresse e-mail dans notre liste d'utilisateurs à supprimer. La suspension du compte aura pour effet de dé-indexer le compte et les toots de l'utilisateur concerné. Ainsi, nous ferons le nécessaire (avec confirmation du propriétaire du compte), de supprimer le compte de l'utilisation ainsi que ses toots et médias lorsque que cette fonctionnalité sera disponible.
Support
En cas de nécessité, vous pourriez avoir besoin d'aide. Le serveur ainsi que l'instance est entièrement géré par @themimitoof (disponible sur Twitter). En cas de problème avec votre compte ou d'un problème technique, vous pouvez envoyez un e-mail à contact+mastodon[at]mvieira[dot]fr.
Liste des administrateurs :

@themimitoof


Contribution fiancière

    L'infrastructure coute à ce jour 40€. Après plusieurs demandes, nous vous proposons plusieurs moyens pour nous aider à financer l'infrastructure :
    
Patreon: https://www.patreon.com/themimitoof
Bitcoin: 1F2igjKPA5eDPAmUmAvUrW5qqXZHkU686
Ethereum: 0x259C9B4A0f477bb6a9ff49779e5A4adAF45B4627


(English) Welcome on Mastodon!
🌎 Cliquez ici pour voir la version française.
This part is is back soon!

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Amateur porn is some of the hottest out there. There's just something about seeing the sexual pictures of other users like yourself without all of that over-the-top porn production.

Rules

ABSOLUTELY NO ONE UNDER THE AGE OF 18! There is an absolute, zero tolerance policy for any sexual content depicting minors.

Flag NSFW content as such. At least, until there is a large enough community to support us not being federated.

Mastodon（マストドン）秋田インスタンス


2017年4月25日サービス開始


こちらのインスタンスは秋田県のインスタンスとして作成しました。基本的には秋田県民、秋田在住者、秋田出身、秋田が好きな方に入っていただきたいインスタンスなのですが、少しでも秋田に興味がある方でしたらウエルカムなのでどんどん入って頂きたいです。

※アカウント登録時、確認メールが届かない場合があります、このような時は「迷惑フォルダ」に入ってる可能性が高いので確認をして下さい




はじめてマストドンを使う方や使い方がわからない方は、当インスタンスでログイン後 #マストドンのトリセツ で検索していただくかリンクをクリック（タップ）していただくと簡単な説明が出てきます


#管理人からのお知らせ


詳細はこちら

<details><summary>(more)</summary>
ルール


ここのサーバーは「さくらのインターネット」のサーバーを使用していますので日本の法律に抵触すような行為はおやめ下さい、グレーもダメです。
宣伝行為を全くしてはいけませんとは言いませんが、過度な宣伝の方法（連投や専用アカウントなど）はしないで下さい。
自分の個人情報の管理徹底、他人の個人情報の流出は絶対にしないで下さい。
サーバーの運営は出来る限り続けていく予定ですが管理者の事情その他により存続ができなくなった場合、予告なく終了することもありますしメンテナンスや不具合等で突然利用できなくなる場合もございますのでご了承下さい。
現在、低価格サーバーを使用しております、サーバーに負荷をかける行為（連投、botでの大量トゥート）は極力お避けください。
誹謗中傷など他人を傷つける行為や恐ろしくネガティブな発言、公序良俗に反するおこないなどはしないで皆さん仲良くトゥートして下さい。
ここのインスタンスで起きた問題や不具合等は自己責任において解決して下さい、パスワードなどはメインで使用しているのは使わずマストドン用を作成するなどして対応願います。
インスタンスの中に事件性や危険性のあるトゥートがありましたら直ちに管理者のアカウントかメールまでご連絡下さい、相応の対処を致します。




管理人のツイッターはこちら




</details>

Email: [shun@0608.info](mailto:shun@0608.info)

Admin: [@SHUN@akitadon.info](https://akitadon.info/@SHUN)

## [mstdn.hanabi-life.net](https://mstdn.hanabi-life.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.hanabi-life.net&view=local)
花火に関連する話題などを交換するマストドン・インスタンスです

花火・花火鑑賞・花火鑑賞士などの話題を中心としたコミュニケーション用サービスです。
個人が建てたサーバーですのでサービスの永続的な保証はできません。
管理人は、大阪住みの花火鑑賞士(14期)です。

## [don.akashi.cloud](https://don.akashi.cloud/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=don.akashi.cloud&view=local)
兵庫県明石市のMastodon（マストドン）インスタンスです。

明石市民以外も歓迎します！基本的に明石周辺の情報でトゥートしていけたらと思っています。

<details><summary>(more)</summary>
インターネットは公共の場です。なんでもして良い場ではありません。他のユーザーを不快にさせるような言動、行動は謹んでください。
また、あまりに目に余るような言動、行動があった場合、アカウント凍結などの処置を行います。
また、このサーバーにおいては日本の法律を適用します。
日本の法律に反するような行為等が見られた場合もアカウント凍結等の措置を行います。
一般に18禁と呼ばれるような文章についてはContent Warningで隠してください。また、18禁のメディア（画像など）については不適切なコンテンツとしてマークしてください。(NSFWボタンでできます)
フォロ爆、ファボ爆、連投他過度にサーバーに負荷をかける行為は禁止です。
BOTについて

原則BOTを作るときは独自のインスタンスを作成してそこでやってください。
BOTによる自発フォローはしないようにしてください。
悪質だと判断した場合連絡なしに凍結などの処置を行うことがあります。




</details>

Email: [admin@akashi.cloud](mailto:admin@akashi.cloud)

Admin: [@kntmrkm@don.akashi.cloud](https://don.akashi.cloud/@kntmrkm)

## [dancingbanana.party](https://dancingbanana.party/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=dancingbanana.party&view=local)
La banane qui danse.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of mastodon.social; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Email: [david@dancingbanana.party](mailto:david@dancingbanana.party)

Admin: [@awea@dancingbanana.party](https://dancingbanana.party/@awea)

An open Mastodon instance in french and english for tech enthusiasts

<details><summary>(more)</summary>The following guidelines (thanks mastodon.social) are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of mastodon.dremtech.fr; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:


The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:

Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:

Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:

Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:

Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.




These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

## [mstdn-off.com](https://mstdn-off.com/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn-off.com&view=local)
オフ会どんって？
オフ会募集専用のマストドンインスタンスです。
突然できてしまった休日に、アフターファイブの余暇に、友達作りに
より気軽にオフを楽しめるサービスを目指しています。

マストドンって？
今話題のサイト毎に独自のtwitterのようなサービスを運営できる仕組みです。
よく参加するオフ会主さんのアカウントをフォローしたり、フォロワーさんの中のみでのオフ会の募集も可能です。
退会も自由ですのでまずは覗いてみませんか？
初めての方はとりあえず連合タイムラインを開いてみることをオススメします。

募集するには？
「新宿二人」などタイムラインに放流しておけばDMが飛んできますので各自連絡を取り合流してください。

参加するには？
タイムライン上の募集に対してツイート画面下の地球マークを押しダイレクトに設定、リプライを送り参加を表明してください。
ツイートの公開範囲設定に関してはこちらを参考にしてください。

無料なの？
無料です。

## [mastodon-nagano.info](https://mastodon-nagano.info/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon-nagano.info&view=local)
新型SNSマストドン初の長野専用インスタンスです。
長野が好きな人、長野に関心がある人ならどなたでも参加OK！オススメのお店やイベント情報の発信など情報交換の場など好きにつぶやいて下さい！ただし喧嘩はダメ！(´・ω・`)
長寿県であり移り住みたい県ランキング、魅力度ランキングでは常に上位の長野県専用インスタンスはこちらです( ﾟДﾟ)
弱小個人で運営しておりますので、大手に比べ信用少なめですが、頑張って運営して参ります|дﾟ)アングラな感じでどうぞ！
マストドンについてはこちら※@ITさんより引用

<details><summary>(more)</summary>☆アカウント作成手順☆
１．ユーザー名を半角英数で入力します
２．メールを受信できるメールアドレスを入力します
３．パスワードを8文字以上で入力します
４．正常にユーザーが作成された際には入力したメールアドレスへ確認用のメールが当サイトより届きます。※受信トレイではなく「迷惑メールフォルダ」に受信する場合がありますので注意してください。受信したメール内の本文から「メールアドレス確認」をクリックしてください
５．完了！
☆スマートフォンアプリについて☆
iphoneの方は「Amaroq for Mastodon」が有名です。
Androidの方は「Tusky」が有名です。
それぞれアプリ起動後に当インスタンス名「mastodon-nagano.info」を入力し、登録が完了したユーザー名およびパスワードを使用してご使用ください。
禁止行為
・公序良俗に反する行為
・日本国内の法律に違反する行為
・他者に中傷・脅迫・経済的もしくは精神的に損害や不利益を与える行為
・実在の人物・団体などになりすます行為
・他者の著作物を無断転載する行為
・サーバに極端な負荷をかける行為
免責事項
当インスタンスにおいて発生した損害については運営者は一切の責任を負わないものとします。
当インスタンスに投稿された内容について、その正確性を保証するものではありません。投稿された内容において発生するまたはした損害等については運営者は一切の責任を負わないものとします。
当インスタンスは予告なくサービスを停止する場合があります。

</details>

Email: [@jjnobless](mailto:@jjnobless)

Admin: [@jjnobless@mastodon-nagano.info](https://mastodon-nagano.info/@jjnobless)

An instance of the Mastodon social network for the tech/startup scene in Scotland.
The goal is to gather all the web/tech people in one place to make for an interesting local timeline.
You don't need to actually be Scottish or in Scotland! Friends, the curious, and all of good will are welcome!

<details><summary>(more)</summary>This is an open instance of the Mastodon social network, aimed at gathering the Scottish web/tech/startup scene in one local timeline.
You don't need to be Scottish or in Scotland to be welcome here! If you're interested in the tech scene, or friends with people here, you're more than welcome!
Code of Conduct
This will be fleshed out in more detail at a later date, but the summary is:
Show respect for people's personal space. If they don't want you in their mentions, leave.
Do not use this platform to harass, stalk, troll, spam, or otherwise be a dick.
No nazis.
If you are experiencing harassment or spamming, please report the offending account and I'll investigate. If you feel at risk or otherwise want to contact the admin directly, I can be reached at john@scotland.computer.
The mgmt reserve the right to refuse service to anyone for any reason, except as prohibited by law.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Infos pratiques :
Les comptes à suivre :

@alex73630 : Administrateur de cette instance
@admin : Essentiellement pour transmettre des informations concernant l'administration (nouveaux modérateurs, MaJ des règles...)
@status : Indique les futurs maintenances, rapport de mise à jour, nouvelles fonctionnalités et bugs temporaires connus
@support : Fourni une assistance aux utilisateurs (préférez contacter/consulter @support@mastodon.social, qui est le compte officiel d'assistance de Mastodon)


Nota : Pour le moment, il est difficile de gérer plusieurs comptes depuis Mastodon, ne vous attendez pas à une réponse rapide sur ces comptes, excepté pour @alex73630


Spécifications du serveur :

Le serveur est actuellement hébergé chez SoYouStart.com en France, dans leur datacenter de Roubaix.


Le modèle : SYS-IP-1S

Règles :

Pas de règles spécifiques, tout ce que je demande c'est le respect de chacun, pas d'insultes, de racisme, d'homophobie, contenu illégaux etc... Bref tout ce qui va du bon sens !


De même, les comptes parodiques/non officiels sont autorisés tant qu'il est indiqué dans la description la mention de compte parodique ou le username officiel de la personne.


Egalement, pour éviter tout incompréhension, merci de ne pas utiliser le ✅ (:white_check_mark:) à coté de votre pseudo pour vous signaler comme étant "verified"/compte actif. D'autres emoji peuvent être utilisé à cet effet.

## [mastdn.jp](https://mastdn.jp/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastdn.jp&view=local)
Mastdn.jpは、プロモーションを中心とした企画・制作・運営とか、なんやかんややっている合同会社WeAreが運営するMastodonのインスタンス（サーバー）です。
特に指針などは決めておらず、どなたでも幅広くご利用頂けます。まぁ楽しくトゥートしていただければ幸いです。
ただ現状サーバースペックはそんなに高くはないので（サーバーは日本のさくらクラウド。メモリは1GB　HDDは30GB）、ある程度のユーザー数に達したら、新規登録受付をストップするかもしれません。
ルール
・公序良俗に反する投稿や行為はご遠慮ください。
・法に抵触する投稿、犯罪行為はおやめください。
・他者の権利を侵害する投稿は禁止です。
・みんなが楽しいと思う空間にしましょう！
管理人の好きなもの

新しい技術（ハード/ソフト）/バンド/ギター（最近はスラム奏法を練習中）/ベース/漫画（最近読んでるのは東京グール/亜人/）/アニメ/ドラマ（今期は朝ドラ/フランケンシュタインの恋/貴族探偵/あなたのことはそれほどでも）/お笑い/料理　などなど
お問い合わせ（問題報告、他）

メールアドレス　nemoto(at)weare.co.jp　にお願いします。
注意事項

*このインスタンスは試験運用中です。
予告なくメンテナンスの実施、データのリセット、サービスの終了となることがあります。

## [mastodon.at](https://mastodon.at/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.at&view=local)

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Welcome to mastodon.at! This instance is open to all users and federates with all other instances with the exception of those with community values that are overwhelmingly incompatible with our Terms of Service below.
Please read the section Responsibility of Contributors below and report any content that you feel might be inappropriate.
Follow @Support for important updates!


🇩🇪 🇦🇹 🇨🇭 Willkommen auf mastodon.at! Diese Instanz ist offen für alle User und ist mit allen anderen Instanzen verbunden, mit der Ausnahme jener, deren Werte mit unseren Nutzungsbedingungen (siehe unten) überwiegend inkompatibel sind.
🇩🇪 🇦🇹 🇨🇭 Bitte lies den Punkt Responsibility of Contributors unten genau durch und melde Inhalte, die du für unangebracht hältst.
Folge @Support für wichtige Updates!


Terms of Service:
The following terms and conditions govern all use of the mastodon.at website and all content, services, and products available at or through the website. Our Services are offered subject to your acceptance without modification of all of the terms and conditions contained herein and all other operating rules, policies (including, without limitation, the Privacy Policy) and procedures that may be published from time to time by mastodon.at (collectively, the “Agreement”). You agree that we may automatically upgrade our Services, and these terms will apply to any upgrades.
Please read this Agreement carefully before accessing or using our Services. By accessing or using any part of our services, you agree to become bound by the terms and conditions of this agreement. If you do not agree to all the terms and conditions of this agreement, then you may not access or use any of our services. If these terms and conditions are considered an offer by mastodon.at, acceptance is expressly limited to these terms.
Use of our Services requires a mastodon.at account. You will be solely responsible and liable for any activity that occurs under your username. You are responsible for keeping your password secure.
1. Your mastodon.at Account
If you create an account on mastodon.at, you are responsible for maintaining the security of your account and blog, and you are fully responsible for all activities that occur under the account and any other actions taken in connection with your account. You must immediately notify mastodon.at of any unauthorized uses of your account or any other breaches of security. mastodon.at will not be liable for any acts or omissions by you, including any damages of any kind incurred as a result of such acts or omissions.
2. Responsibility of Contributors
If you post material to mastodon.at, post links on mastodon.at, or otherwise make (or allow any third party to make) material available (any such material, “Content”), you are entirely responsible for the content of, and any harm resulting from, that Content or your conduct. That is the case regardless of what form the Content takes, which includes, but is not limited to text, photo, video, audio, or code. By using mastodon.at, you represent and warrant that your Content and conduct do not violate the following terms:


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Austria and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



If you delete Content, mastodon.at will use reasonable efforts to remove it from mastodon.at, but you acknowledge that caching or references to the Content may not be made immediately unavailable. Without limiting any of those representations or warranties, mastodon.at has the right (though not the obligation) to, in mastodon.at’s sole discretion, (i) reclaim your username or website’s URL due to prolonged inactivity, (ii) refuse or remove any content that, in mastodon.at’s reasonable opinion, violates any mastodon.at policy or is in any way harmful or objectionable, or (iii) terminate or deny access to and use of mastodon.at to any individual or entity for any reason.
3. Responsibility of Visitors.
mastodon.at has not reviewed, and cannot review, all of the material, including computer software, posted to our Services, and cannot therefore be responsible for that material’s content, use or effects. By operating our Services, mastodon.at does not represent or imply that it endorses the material there posted, or that it believes such material to be accurate, useful, or non-harmful. You are responsible for taking precautions as necessary to protect yourself and your computer systems from viruses, worms, Trojan horses, and other harmful or destructive content. Our Services may contain content that is offensive, indecent, or otherwise objectionable, as well as content containing technical inaccuracies, typographical mistakes, and other errors. Our Services may also contain material that violates the privacy or publicity rights, or infringes the intellectual property and other proprietary rights, of third parties, or the downloading, copying or use of which is subject to additional terms and conditions, stated or unstated. mastodon.at disclaims any responsibility for any harm resulting from the use by visitors of our Services, or from any downloading by those visitors of content there posted. You’re encouraged to report any content that you feel is inappropriate or in violation of these terms.

If we make changes that are material, we will let you know by posting on one of our admin accounts, or by sending you an email or other communication before the changes take effect. ［名・形動］《(梵)mohaの訳。痴・無明とも訳す》仏語。三毒の一。心性が愚かで、一切の道理にくらいこと。心の迷い。また、そのさま。

## [mstdn.studio](https://mstdn.studio/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.studio&view=local)
スタジオ・マストドンはコスプレをメインテーマとする、できたばかり (4/23 に UP) の Mastodon コミュニティです。
コスプレイヤーやカメラマンはもちろん、それに関連する漫画・アニメ・ゲームなどの趣味、およびそれらに興味のある方に使っていただくことを想定しています。


登録されましたらまずは気になる方をフォローしてみましょう！

コスプレイヤー、カメラマンの方はぜひ写真を UP してみてください！

<details><summary>(more)</summary>お知らせ
----
概要

コスプレ (界隈) を主題としていますが、それ専門ということではありません。コミュニケーションツールとしてご利用いただければと思います。
成人向けまたは過激なコンテンツは CW および NSFW の設定をお願いします。
作品の披露や併せの募集なんかにもご利用いただけます。
この世界で活動されている方は、イベントの告知などにもご利用いただけます。

このインスタンスの属性
上のものほど強いテーマです。

コスプレ / 写真
イラスト / 造形 / ドール / カメラ / 漫画 / アニメ / ゲーム
ポートレート / ファッション / 映像 / ロケーション

禁止行為

日本国内の法律に違反する投稿や行為
誹謗中傷、脅迫、いやがらせ、その他精神的な不利益を与える行為
他者のプライバシーを侵害する行為
なりすまし行為
サーバーに極端な負担をかける行為

お問い合わせ先: @gipani または メール
思想 妄想

ここは Twitter よりも少しだけ狭く、少しだけ濃い世界です。

ローカルタイムラインを埋めるのは同じ世界に住む皆さんです。心置きなくトゥートしてください！

----
Mastodon は Twitter のように好き勝手気軽に投稿することができながらも、少しセンシティブな公開範囲を興味のある方までに制限し、起こりうる問題をやわらかく回避できるはずです。
この仕組みは現存するコミュニティの隙間にはまるのではと期待しています。


大々的に宣伝活動をするつもりはありませんが、少しずつ利用者が増えればと思います。

今後について (目標)

4/28 までにユーザー数 30 になってたらいいな (達成: 83)
5/6 までに 1 日あたり 20 ユーザーがトゥート (多分無理)
コスプレ界隈ユーザーにとって有益な機能拡張を実装する


実装するかもしれない: プロフィールページのカスタマイズ, デザインのカスタマイズ, キャラ/撮影者/場所タグ機能


いつかは欲しい: 画像管理, ギャラリー


実装しない: 特権化(コスプレイヤー/カメラマン/一般参加者 の差別化)

</details>

Email: [gipanidon@gmail.com](mailto:gipanidon@gmail.com)

Admin: [@gipani@mstdn.studio](https://mstdn.studio/@gipani)

Mastodon は自由でオープンソースなソーシャルネットワークです。商用プラットフォームの代替となる分散型を採用し、あなたのやりとりが一つの会社によって独占されるのを防ぎます。信頼できるインスタンスを選択してください — どのインスタンスを選んでも、誰とでもやりとりすることができます。 だれでも自分の Mastodon インスタンスを作ることができ、シームレスにソーシャルネットワークに参加できます。

## [mstdn.rche-iidx.jp](https://mstdn.rche-iidx.jp/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.rche-iidx.jp&view=local)
傲慢ちゃんはかわいい！

音ゲーマー向けのインスタンスです。リザルト投稿、キャラ談義、ディスカッションにどうぞ。

ドメインにiidxとついていますが、弐寺以外の話題も大歓迎です。

あくまで日本国内の法律に基づいて使用して下さい。

<details><summary>(more)</summary>特徴など
毎日午前4時に自動的にmasterに追従するようにしてみました。
その間はサービスを一旦停止しているため、502エラーなどが出る事があります。
さくらのVPS、東京第2ゾーンにて動かしています。
</details>

お１人様の寂しいパオラ―が集う村です。彼氏・彼女のいない同士でわちゃわちゃ交流します。自由にトゥートしてもらって構いませんが、ルールは守りましょう。せっかくの新しいサービスなので、同性同士で街コン仲間を探せたり、男女ペアのゲームオフ会を開催できたりと既存の枠に捕らわれない自由で楽しい場所を提供できたらいいなと思ったりしてます。タイムラインチラ見 → コチラ

ルール

犯罪目的・公序良俗に反する・それらを助長するような行為の禁止広告活動・過度な勧誘の禁止ルールを守れない人はBANされる場合があります (´・ω・`) 仲良く使ってね


その他
プロフはなるべく書きましょう楽しいトゥートを心掛けましょうトップの二次絵を募集しております管理人は交際中のため管理に徹します

## [animefun.jp](https://animefun.jp/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=animefun.jp&view=local)

animefun.jp


<details><summary>(more)</summary>animefun.jpはアニメ好きなみなさんのインスタンスです。ジャンル・カテゴリ・属性自由。お気軽にご登録ください(*'ω'*)日本国内の法人が運営しています。運営：株式会社 テルル種別：アニメ・総合
本インスタンスは日本国内の法律に従い運用されています。

プライバシーポリシー

本プライバシーポリシーは、株式会社テルル(以下、当社)が運営／管理する情報サービスを通じて、お客様に個人情報をご提供いただく場合に適用されます。


１.個人情報とは

個人情報とは、当社が運営／管理する情報サービスを通じてお客様からご提供頂く、氏名、住所、電話番号、電子メールアドレス等、お客様個人を識別できる情報あるいはお客様個人に固有の情報を意味します。

２.個人情報の取り扱いについて

当社は、お客様の個人情報を適切かつ安全に管理し、紛失、破壊、改ざん、及び漏洩等の防止策を講じます。当社は、個人情報の収集、管理、利用にあたり個人情報の保護に関する法律等の関連法令、政府などが公表する指針を遵守いたします。

３.個人情報の利用

お客様の個人情報は、当社の取扱うサービスをお客様へ提供するため、あるいはお客様が希望される事項の実現のためのお客様との連絡のため、当社において正当な事業遂行の範囲内で利用いたします。お客様がご自身の個人情報を当社に提供されるか否かは、お客様のご判断によります。ご提供されない場合には、当社のサービスが提供できない場合があります。

４.個人情報の第三者への提供

お客様の個人情報は、以下に掲げる場合に限って、第三者に提供させていただくことがあります。

(１) お客様の同意がある場合

(２) 統計的情報として、お客様個人を識別できない状態に加工した場合

(３) 法令に基づいた、適法な開示要求を受けた場合

５.本プライバシーポリシーの改定

当社は、個人情報の保護に関する法律等の関連法令、政府などが公表する指針等の変更に伴い、本プライバシーポリシーを改定することがあります。

2017年4月16日 株式会社テルル
</details>

Email: [anime_fun-mastdon@telulu.co.jp](mailto:anime_fun-mastdon@telulu.co.jp)

Admin: [@telulu@animefun.jp](https://animefun.jp/@telulu)

## [ablative.stream](https://ablative.stream/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=ablative.stream&view=local)
This Mastodon instance is managed by Ablative.Hosting and hosted by Brass Horn Communications.

As such it is crypto/Tor friendly and as censorship-free as UK law allows.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>We intend for this Mastodon instance to be for paying customers of Ablative Hosting Ltd however registrations are currently open.
Ablative Hosting is a Tor centric hosting company originally designed to help UK indie producers of adult content defend themselves against the UK Digital Economy bill.
Ablative Hosting Ltd does not believe in Internet censorship but also reserves the right to not be the host for certain material in accordance with XKCD #1357.


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Material in violation of UK law



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



</details>

Email: [gareth@brasshorncommunications.uk](mailto:gareth@brasshorncommunications.uk)

Admin: [@Gareth@ablative.stream](https://ablative.stream/@Gareth)

## [webcommunity.club](https://webcommunity.club/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=webcommunity.club&view=local)

webcommunity.club


<details><summary>(more)</summary>The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of mastodon.social; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Email: Not Available

Admin: [@davatron5000@webcommunity.club](https://webcommunity.club/@davatron5000)

## [toot.pm](https://toot.pm/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=toot.pm&view=local)
This Mastodon instance serves the community respecting private messaging via advanced technology as well as open and fearless communication in general. Worldwide.

When posting, let the core rules of Netiquette guide you.

Follow @status for updates.

Instance Location: Frankfurt, Germany.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Privacy is necessary for an open society in the electronic age. Privacy is not secrecy. A private matter is something one doesn't want the whole world to know, but a secret matter is something one doesn't want anybody to know. Privacy is the power to selectively reveal oneself to the world.

If two parties have some sort of dealings, then each has a memory of their interaction. Each party can speak about their own memory of this; how could anyone prevent it? One could pass laws against it, but the freedom of speech, even more than privacy, is fundamental to an open society; we seek not to restrict any speech at all. If many parties speak together in the same forum, each can speak to all the others and aggregate together knowledge about individuals and other parties. The power of electronic communications has enabled such group speech, and it will not go away merely because we might want it to.

Since we desire privacy, we must ensure that each party to a transaction have knowledge only of that which is directly necessary for that transaction. Since any information can be spoken of, we must ensure that we reveal as little as possible. In most cases personal identity is not salient. When I purchase a magazine at a store and hand cash to the clerk, there is no need to know who I am. When I ask my electronic mail provider to send and receive messages, my provider need not know to whom I am speaking or what I am saying or what others are saying to me;  my provider only need know how to get the message there and how much I owe them in fees. When my identity is revealed by the underlying mechanism of the transaction, I have no privacy. I cannot here selectively reveal myself; I must _always_ reveal myself.

Therefore, privacy in an open society requires anonymous transaction systems. Until now, cash has been the primary such system. An anonymous transaction system is not a secret transaction system. An anonymous system empowers individuals to reveal their identity when desired and only when desired; this is the essence of privacy.

Privacy in an open society also requires cryptography. If I say something, I want it heard only by those for whom I intend it. If the content of my speech is available to the world, I have no privacy. To encrypt is to indicate the desire for privacy, and to encrypt with weak cryptography is to indicate not too much desire for privacy. Furthermore, to reveal one's identity with assurance when the default is anonymity requires the cryptographic signature.

We cannot expect governments, corporations, or other large, faceless organizations to grant us privacy out of their beneficence. It is to their advantage to speak of us, and  we should expect that they will speak. To try to prevent their speech is to fight against the realities of information. Information does not just want to be free, it longs to be free. Information expands to fill the available storage space.  Information is Rumor's younger, stronger cousin; Information is fleeter of foot, has more eyes, knows more, and understands less than Rumor.

We must defend our own privacy if we expect to have any. We must come together and create systems which allow anonymous transactions to take place. People have been defending their own privacy for centuries with whispers, darkness, envelopes, closed doors, secret handshakes, and couriers. The technologies of the past did not allow for strong privacy, but electronic technologies do.

We the Cypherpunks are dedicated to building anonymous systems. We are defending our privacy with cryptography, with anonymous mail forwarding systems, with digital signatures, and with electronic money.

Cypherpunks write code. We know that someone has to write software to defend privacy, and since we can't get privacy unless we all do, we're going to write it. We publish our code so that our fellow Cypherpunks may practice and play with it. Our code is free for all to use, worldwide. We don't much care if you don't approve of the software we write. We know that software can't be destroyed and that a widely dispersed system can't be shut down.

Cypherpunks deplore regulations on cryptography, for encryption is fundamentally a private act. The act of encryption, in fact, removes information from the public realm. Even laws against cryptography reach only so far as a nation's border and the arm of its violence. Cryptography will ineluctably spread over the whole globe, and with it the anonymous transactions systems that it makes possible.

For privacy to be widespread it must be part of a social contract. People must come and together deploy these systems for the common good. Privacy only extends so far as the cooperation of one's fellows in society. We the Cypherpunks seek your questions and your concerns and hope we may engage you so that we do not deceive ourselves. We will not, however, be moved out of our course because some may disagree with our goals.

The Cypherpunks are actively engaged in making the networks safer for privacy. Let us proceed together apace.

Onward.

Eric Hughes
<hughes@soda.berkeley.edu>

9 March 1993
</details>

Email: [contact at toot dot pm](mailto:contact at toot dot pm)

Admin: [@status@toot.pm](https://toot.pm/@status)

## [burners.social](https://burners.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=burners.social&view=local)
An online community for burners and the people that love them )'( 🔥

<details><summary>(more)</summary>
Radical Inclusion
Anyone may be a part of Burners.social. We welcome and respect the stranger. No prerequisites exist for participation in our community.


Gifting
Burners.social is devoted to acts of gift giving. The value of a gift is unconditional. Gifting does not contemplate a return or an exchange for something of equal value.


Decommodification
In order to preserve the spirit of gifting, our community seeks to create social environments that are unmediated by commercial sponsorships, transactions, or advertising. We stand ready to protect our culture from such exploitation. We resist the substitution of consumption for participatory experience.


Radical Self-reliance
Burners.social encourages the individual to discover, exercise and rely on his or her inner resources.


Radical Self-expression
Radical self-expression arises from the unique gifts of the individual. No one other than the individual or a collaborating group can determine its content. It is offered as a gift to others. In this spirit, the giver should respect the rights and liberties of the recipient.


Communal Effort
Our community values creative cooperation and collaboration. We strive to produce, promote and protect social networks, public spaces, works of art, and methods of communication that support such interaction.


Civic Responsibility
We value civil society. Community members who organize events should assume responsibility for public welfare and endeavor to communicate civic responsibilities to participants. They must also assume responsibility for conducting events in accordance with local, state and federal laws.


Leaving No Trace
Our community respects the environment. We are committed to leaving no physical trace of our activities wherever we gather. We clean up after ourselves and endeavor, whenever possible, to leave such places in a better state than when we found them.


Participation
Our community is committed to a radically participatory ethic. We believe that transformative change, whether in the individual or in society, can occur only through the medium of deeply personal participation. We achieve being through doing. Everyone is invited to work. Everyone is invited to play. We make the world real through actions that open the heart.


Immediacy
Immediate experience is, in many ways, the most important touchstone of value in our culture. We seek to overcome barriers that stand between us and a recognition of our inner selves, the reality of those around us, participation in society, and contact with a natural world exceeding human powers. No idea can substitute for this experience.
</details>

Email: Not Available

Admin: [@muloka@burners.social](https://burners.social/@muloka)

## [truecolors.space](https://truecolors.space/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=truecolors.space&view=local)
Welcome to True Colors! Please take some time to look over the Code of Conduct.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>True Colors Space
The goal of True Colors is to create an open community of like minded individuals and to connect with instances that hold similar values.
Code of Conduct
The following is our Code of Conduct, which is not a legal document and is up to the moderators of truecolors.space for interpretation. We ask that you follow these guidelines as actions do have consequences.
Short Version / Summary

Harassment and/or Discrimination is strictly prohibited (no tolerance)
We all want to have fun, but don't do it at the expense of others.
We reserve the right to bar any person or instance that have been deemed toxic to the community or in violation of our CoC.
Report any violations or issues to our moderators, so they may look into it.

Animations / Gifs 
We ask that you keep flashing animations and strobing lights to a minimum, and to always keep them behind a content warning (CW) as it might cause issues for some users. While you might have the best intentions it could potentially through someone into a seizure, which is obviously not good. If we find your avatar or animation to be intentionally flashing we will have to take action to protect our users.
Under Construction

Under Construction please bare with us as we are still getting setup. In the meantime please note that any form of harassment is strictly prohibited and will result in suspension. Bigotry is not acceptable and will result in the same
This is a living document is is subject to change in the future. As a member of True Colors you are expected to look back here from time to time to make sure you are in compliance with the CoC. We will try our best to inform users of the instance via a Toot when these get updated drastically.

Based On / Prior Work

Toot.cafe Code of Conduct
Mastodon.social Guidelines

Moderators

ErdMutter
Jermayan

Jurisdiction / Hosting Info
We are hosted on a New York droplet at Digital Ocean within the United States of America
</details>

Email: Not Available

Admin: [@ErdMutter@truecolors.space](https://truecolors.space/@ErdMutter)

## [lovethe.wang](https://lovethe.wang/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=lovethe.wang&view=local)
Do you love the wang?

We're pretty lewd here, be warned.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>We're pretty lewd here, be warned.

Site rules:
Interaction with the community.

Remember, people will never forget how you made them feel. 
Tag content that people may not want to see using the content warning function.
Harassment and bullying of any kind will not be tolerated and will lead to a full suspension.

Content

Content illegal in the United Kingdom, France or the Netherlands is prohibited and will lead to a full suspension. 
Transphobic, homo/biphobic, racist, etc content is prohibited and will lead to a full suspension. 
Spam is prohibited.
Bots are allowed but must not interact with users without being explicitly requested to.

Network
Please be aware that due to the nature of federated platforms, we have very little control over the behaviors of users from other communities.

  Use the standard mute and block functions where needed.

  However, please report users that offend the CoC of this instance and the administration will take action if necessary.


Admin decisions are final and are not up for discussion.
The rules set out above are guidelines for acceptable content/behavior and may be changed any time without notice.

Please note the administration may take action in cases outside of the rules for the greater need of the community/federation at large.


Suspended and silenced instances

noagendasocial.com (Silenced)

This Mastodon-instance is hosted in The Netherlands and has Dutch as its primary language.


<details><summary>(more)</summary>
Moi eem! Wat barsten we van de ambitie in Stad en ommeland. Onze startups horen bij de snelst groeiende bedrijven in Nederland, onze fabrieken worden slimmer en we krijgen zowel een indrukwekkend Internet of Things-netwerk als een 5G-fieldlab. En oh ja: we proberen Tesla binnen te halen en willen de duurzaamste energieregio van het land worden.


Misschien is het dus wel handig dat we elkaar goed weten te vinden. Voor inspiratie, ideeën, vragen en antwoorden. Waar dan ook over.


Dat elkaar helpen, dat proberen we hier. Een Mastodon: een gezamenlijke plek, een soort interne Twitter. Een experiment, maar zo zijn we hier in Grunn: gewoon proberen en gáán.


Zeg ook moi! Het is gewoon gratis, gaaf en vast gezellig.*

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Code of Conduct
NOTE: these are initial and subject to change

Anyone is welcome to open an account either as your personal account, or to run a bot. Open as many bot accounts as you like.
If you run a bot here, please be kind to the servers. If the instance starts to bog down, bots that are making lots of API calls will get shut down.
Do not use bots to abuse users. Bots should punch up, not down.


If you have questions or concerns, feel free to contact me at muffinista@mastodon.social, @muffinista on twitter, or by emailing colin at muffinlabs.com
