## [wandering.shop](https://wandering.shop/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=wandering.shop&view=local)
The Wandering Shop is a Mastodon instance for the science fiction and fantasy community. We want our 'local' timeline to have the feel of a coffee shop at a good science fiction convention: tables full of friendly conversation on a wide variety of topics. We welcome everyone who wants to participate, so long as you're willing to abide by our code of conduct.
Code of Conduct
We want this to be a fun, pleasant, and harassment-free experience for everyone. By joining the Wandering Shop, you're agreeing to abide by our code of conduct.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>The Wandering Shop Code of Conduct
Welcome!
The Wandering Shop is a Mastodon instance for the science fiction and fantasy community. We want our 'local' timeline to have the feel of a coffee shop at a good science fiction convention: tables full of friendly conversation on a wide variety of topics.
We want this to be a fun, pleasant, and harassment-free experience for everyone, regardless of gender, gender identity and expression, sexual orientation, disability, physical appearance, body size, race, or religion. We do not tolerate harassment of participants in any form.
Participants asked to stop any harassing behavior are expected to comply immediately. If someone asks you to leave them alone, leave them alone.
Unacceptable Behavior
The following behavior is not welcome anywhere in The Wandering Shop:

Offensive comments related to gender, gender identity and expression, sexual orientation, disability, mental illness, neuro(a)typicality, physical appearance, body size, race, or religion.
Holocaust denial and Nazi symbolism.
Deliberate or persistent misgendering.
Threats of violence.
Incitement of violence towards any individual, including encouraging a person to commit suicide or to engage in self-harm.
Deliberate intimidation.
Publishing any individual's address, phone number, or other private identifying information without consent.
Sexual depictions of children.
Unwelcome sexual attention, including sharing sexual content with specific users without consent.
Gratuitous sexual images or behavior without a content warning.
Simulated physical contact (e.g. textual descriptions like “*hug*” or “*backrub*”) without consent or after a request to stop.
Publication of non-harassing private communication without consent.
Sustained disruption of discussion.
Continued communications with someone who's asked that you leave them alone.
Unwelcome comments regarding a person’s lifestyle choices and practices, including those related to food, health, parenting, drugs, and employment.

The following behavior is not allowed on the public timeline:

Graphic violent or sexual content without a content warning
Gratuitous advertizing or spam. It's fine to promote your work, but it shouldn't be the bulk of what you share.

Known Harassers:
The admins may ban or silence users whom we know to be harassers or abusers, even if they have not violated the rules of this instance. The mere presence of a harasser can make past or potential victims uncomfortable, and it can put potential victims who are unaware of the person's history in particular danger. Users are encouraged to individually mute, block, and/or report accounts they don't want to see, but at our discretion, we may take the additional step of blocking or silencing someone instance-wide if we believe they endanger the safe and welcoming space we're trying to maintain.
Reporting
The current admins are:

Annalee
Phildini
If you are being harassed, notice that someone else is being harassed, or have any other concerns, please contact the admins. They'll respond as promptly as they can.
We will respect confidentiality requests for the purpose of protecting victims of abuse. At our discretion, we may publicly name a person about whom we’ve received harassment complaints, or privately warn third parties about them. We will not name harassment victims without their affirmative consent.
Consequences
Participants asked to stop any harassing behavior are expected to comply immediately.
If a participant engages in harassing behavior, the admins may take any action they deem appropriate, up to and including expulsion from the wandering shop and identifying the participant publicly as someone about whom we've received complaints.
Credits and License
This code of conduct is based on Annalee Flower Horne's Sample Slack Code of Conduct, which is in turn based on Geek Feminism's Community Anti-Harassment Policy.
</details>

Email: [phildini@phildini.net](mailto:phildini@phildini.net)

Admin: [@phildini@wandering.shop](https://wandering.shop/@phildini)

## [kosmos.social](https://kosmos.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=kosmos.social&view=local)
A friendly place for tooting. Run by the Kosmos peeps.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Technical Details
kosmos.social is currently hosted on a dedicated server at Hetzner in Germany (renewable energy source, German laws apply). We configure and deploy everything via Chef cookbooks. Your uploads are stored on Amazon S3. Automated backups are run regularly and pushed to S3 as well.
Our fork of the source code is publicly available at https://github.com/67P/mastodon/ (we deploy the kosmos branch). We frequently update the repo and running code with the latest fixes and improvements.
TL;DR We know what we are doing and your data should be safe. However, since this is a free service, we do not guarantee it.
IRC room
If you're into that jazz, you can find us in #kosmos on Freenode. If there's no immediate response to a question, just idle for a while.
The Rules
The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of kosmos.social; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Email: [mail@kosmos.org](mailto:mail@kosmos.org)

Admin: [@kosmos@kosmos.social](https://kosmos.social/@kosmos)

## [mstdn.niigata.jp](https://mstdn.niigata.jp/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.niigata.jp&view=local)
日本 新潟県某所に設置してあるmastodonインスタンスです。
新潟県民以外も参加歓迎します。
ルール

法律は厳守して下さい。
法律に加担・接触するようなトゥートの投稿は禁止
R-18指定(エロ・グロ等)は、文章にはContent Warningを，画像にはNSFWタグを付けてください。
連投やフォローバックなど過度な迷惑投稿は禁止です。
スパムにしか見えない宣伝やトゥートは禁止
みんな仲良く楽しみましょう


禁止事項

本サービスのサーバーまたはネットワークの機能を破壊したり，妨害したりする行為
他のユーザーに成りすます行為
当インスタンスの他のユーザーまたは第三者の知的財産権，肖像権，プライバシー，名誉その他の権利または利益を侵害する行為
宗教活動または宗教団体への勧誘行為
その他，運営チームが不適切と判断する行為


<details><summary>(more)</summary>mastodon 新潟サーバー作った理由
mstdn.jpの補助として作ろうと構築し始めました。
ちなみに新潟の理由は、サーバーを借りてる所が新潟県にあるからです。
提供

サーバーハード管理：hiroponさん

留意事項

当インスタンスは重大な損害を与える可能性があるインスタンスについてはBANさせていただきます。（例：パスワード抜き取るインスタンス）
原則、法律に反して警察・裁判所・弁護士から要請が来た場合、該当ユーザーのログを開示させていただきます。

寄付
もし宜しければEntyで支援をお願いします。
お問い合わせ
mastodon：@mamireimu@mstdn.niigata.jp
Twitter:@anilove_mami_13 or @mstdn_niigata

## [mdn.crows.tokyo](https://mdn.crows.tokyo/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mdn.crows.tokyo&view=local)
カラスやその他の鳥が好きな方と航空関係の人のためのインスタンスです。

## [tenforward.social](https://tenforward.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=tenforward.social&view=local)
Welcome to Ten Forward, a Star Trek themed Mastodon instance!

For more information on what Ten Forward is in the Star Trek universe, please read this page on Memory-Alpha.

The instance is not restricted to Star Trek role-play or characters. More general purpose use is welcome.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Want to support our community financially?
I have set up two methods of supporting our community:

Patreon
PayPal

Our supporters

@Morn
@Q
@Dathon

Thank you for any support you provide!
Alliance policy
We are currently open to allying with all other empires. Any changes to this policy will be noted here.
Blacklisted instances

pawoo.net (Silence with media block)
shitposter.club
freezepeach.xyz
sealion.club
social.heldscal.la
noagendasocial.com
unsafe.space

Code of Conduct
This instance borrows the code of conduct from the good folks of toot.cat.
As tooters on this instance, we pledge to uphold an environment that is radically inclusive with respect for all users of the instance.
We are committed to making participation in this instance an oppression-free experience for everyone, regardless of level of experience, gender, gender identity and expression, sexual orientation, disability, personal appearance, body size, race, ethnicity, age, religion, or nationality.
We define oppression as any language or action that expresses, reinforces, upholds or sympathizes with any form of systemic social domination.
Examples of unacceptable behavior by participants include:
Personal attacks
Trolling or insulting/derogatory comments
Public or private oppressive language or actions
Other unethical conduct
Users are empowered and responsible for addressing any abuses of the Code of Conduct such that the project remains an oppression-free experience.
Certain types of content should posted in such a way that you avoid showing it to non-consenting parties. These types of content should:

Not be used a profile picture
Be posted with a "NSFW" tag
Not be posted to the public timeline

the above rules apply to content that is:

Sexualized
Violent
Flashing or rapidly changing

By adopting this Code of Conduct, users commit themselves to fairly and consistently applying these principles to every aspect of using this instance. users who do not follow or enforce the Code of Conduct may be permanently banned.
This Code of Conduct applies both to toots on tenforward.social and to public spaces when an individual is representing tenforward.social or its community.
Instances of abusive, harassing, or otherwise unacceptable behavior may be reported by contacting an admin by using the report button. All reports will be reviewed and investigated and will result in a response that is deemed necessary and appropriate to the circumstances. Admins are obligated to maintain confidentiality with regard to the reporter of an incident.
</details>

Email: [guinan@tenforward.social](mailto:guinan@tenforward.social)

Admin: [@guinan@tenforward.social](https://tenforward.social/@guinan)

## [nijiura.xyz](https://nijiura.xyz/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=nijiura.xyz&view=local)
【Mastodon使用上の注意（全インスタンス共通）】

Mastodonはサービスの特性上、インスタンスごとに登録が必要です。複数のインスタンスに同じメールアドレスとパスワードで登録すると、登録したインスタンスの数分セキュリティが低下します。

セキュリティを気にされる場合は、普段のメールに影響を及ぼさないよう、普段使用するアドレスと別に、Mastodon専用で使う新しいメールアドレスとパスワードを作成し各インスタンスに使用することを推奨します。


にじうらますとどんは、
生まれたばかりのmastodonです。

応援して下さいね☆

お友達にもここを
教えてあげて下さいね。






にじうらますとどんを

虹裏そっくりにする

「ふたばどん」



作って頂きました！




https://userstyles.org/styles/141617/theme




【使い方】
GoogleChrome専用
install Stylishをクリックして拡張機能をインストール後
+ Install with Stylishを再度クリックしてください。
虹裏そっくりのデザインでmastodonを楽しめます。

## [summoners-riftodon.jp](https://summoners-riftodon.jp/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=summoners-riftodon.jp&view=local)
日本のLoLプレイヤーが交流をするためのマストドンインスタンスです

@yota と @utakata の個人によって運用されているもので、Riot公式のものではありませんのでご注意ください。

アンチハラスメントポリシー

ハラスメントとは、性差、性同一性と表現、性的指向、障害、外見や身体的特徴、人種、宗教、公共な場での性的な画像や類する表現、脅迫、ストーカー、望まない写真撮影や録音・録画、不適切な接触、およびそれらに関連した不快な言動が含まれます。
参加者が安心してコミュニティに集中できるよう、これらのハラスメント行為が行われないようにしてください。
私たちは、参加者へのハラスメント行為はいかなる形であれ容認しません。この原則に違反した参加者は、管理者の裁量により退場させられるものとします。また今後の参加が拒否される可能性があります。
これらの行為は、当コミュニティだけでなく、他SNSへの投稿、コメント等すべてにおいて認められないものとします。
これらのハラスメント行為を目撃した場合は管理者までご連絡ください。
私たちはすべての人が気持ちよくコミュニティに参加できるよう、尽力します。
皆様のご協力をお願いします。


<details><summary>(more)</summary>注意事項

公序良俗やアンチハラスメントポリシーに反する表現、法律に違反する行為等は禁止です。
機械的に大量のアカウントを取得したり、大量のトゥートを投稿する行為は禁止です。
違反したユーザーに対しては管理者の裁量やユーザーからのレポートに基づき、予告なくアカウント停止などの措置をとることがあります。
投稿されたトゥートや画像等の内容が永久的に保存されることは保障できかねますのでご注意ください。
この注意事項は追加・変更されることがありますのでご注意ください。
みんなが気持ちよく利用するためのルールです。ご理解とご協力をお願いします。

Discord

https://discord.gg/a9DsQM7
summoners-riftodonのメンバーでnormalに行く時に使いやすいかと思います。
すぷーんさんによって管理されています。

</details>

Email: Not Available

Admin: [@yota@summoners-riftodon.jp](https://summoners-riftodon.jp/@yota)

Likes are florps and timeline goes sideways

## [nog20.social](https://nog20.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=nog20.social&view=local)
Since the 1999 Seattle WTO protests, social media has been an integral part in organizing protests.
This year, the G20 will take place in Hamburg, Germany.
Since 1999 the world and the web have changed. Twitter is full of fascists, sexists and misogynists. But a safe place to share ideas and discuss is more needed than ever!
Thats why we created nog20.social. A safe place for everyone who wants to do something about the upcoming summit of the world‘s 20 economically and politically most powerful countries.



Warning!
This site will close down and will be deleted after July 10th

more info


<details><summary>(more)</summary>
Basic social rules apply here, and the moderation follows up on each report. Every rule violation can end up in an account suspension.


In particular, all forms of transphobia, misogyny, homophobia, racism, fat-shaming, ableism, engaging in harrasment, insults, etc are strictly prohibited, and will be dealt with in due course. There is no tolerance on shit like this, accounts are suspended without talking, period.


nog20.social was not designed for sensitive communication. Such communication shouldn't be discussed here, or on any other social network.
 Illegal content will be deleted, and may lead to an account suspension.

    
Content Warning should be used for the following :

violence (text and medias)
stories including *phobias (text and medias)



Please use the report feature if you see a rule violation. Be specific by including a comment. 

@chris
is in charge of moderation    


Don’t forget to follow @chris to stay up-to-date with problems, updates and server downtime



We are also reachable via email: contact@nog20.social.

GPG Fingerprint: C64A 0730 3CC0 3BD3 1141  AEA2 8EAC F5C4 5C45 C68F

</details>

Email: [contact@nog20.social](mailto:contact@nog20.social)

Admin: [@chris@nog20.social](https://nog20.social/@chris)

## [soc.mtb.wtf](https://soc.mtb.wtf/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=soc.mtb.wtf&view=local)
Welcome to soc.mtb.wtf. I made this for myself, but signups will stay open as long as I can manage.
Origin of the name: mtb is my initials, so I bought mtb.wtf a while ago; soc stands for social or SoCal or socialism or whatever you want it to stand for.
This instance has no specific purpose right now. If most of the users want one, we can discuss it.
If anything, this instance cares about privacy. I modified the terms to get rid of potentially worrisome ad-related parts. If you see anything else you don't like, I can change it again.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Rules "Moderation" duties will probably be limited to me, so since I'm busy I won't moderate too much. Some trolling is fine, but I reserve the right to ban Nazis.

Privacy policy I suppose I should have a privacy policy, so here it goes: I will not intentionally view or share your information unless required by law, in which case I'll do everything in my power to not share it.
</details>

Email: [matthew@bentley.link](mailto:matthew@bentley.link)

Admin: [@bentley@soc.mtb.wtf](https://soc.mtb.wtf/@bentley)

## [tusk.schoollibraries.net](https://tusk.schoollibraries.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=tusk.schoollibraries.net&view=local)
This Instance has been created to help educators collaborate and provide feedback to establish and improve the School Libraries Resource Network

<details><summary>(more)</summary>In the nineteen-eighties, the Internet was a small, decentralized collective of computers. This is not the same Internet we know today. Today most communication flows through a small set of corporations; and thus, falls under the influence of those companies and institutions.

Internet users now regularly submit to terms-of-service agreements that give companies license to share their personal data with other institutions, from advertisers to governments.

Distributed solutions like Mastodon and WebSonar will allow us to start to create outposts that can grow into the better web Berners-Lee envisions, where users control where their data is stored and how it’s accessed.

For example, social networks would still run in the cloud. But you could store your data locally. Alternately, you could choose a different cloud server run by a company or community you trust.
</details>

Email: [cowboy@wisdomquest.com](mailto:cowboy@wisdomquest.com)

Admin: Not Available

マンガドン・ビズ 
仕事としてマンガ業界に携わる方々の交流の場です。 
プロの漫画家や、編集者、漫画家予備軍、アシスタント、書店員さん、電子書籍書店、取次の方々の交流の場です。

<details><summary>(more)</summary>プロの漫画家や、編集者、漫画家予備軍、アシスタント、書店員さん、電子書籍書店、取次の方々の交流の場です！
ここ数年、混沌とした状況が続いておりますが、日本が世界に誇るマンガ文化を一緒に盛り上げて行きましょう！！
  -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------   ★重要：登録確認メールが、迷惑メールフォルダに届く場合が多いようです！！特にGmailを使用している方からのご連絡が多いです。ご確認頂ければ幸いです！HTMLメールが受信できないスマホ等では登録できません！  ※善は急げ！ということで、急きょ開始致しました！今後の運営方針がまだ確定しておりません。   【利用規約/免責事項/禁止事項について】 ※トゥートに内容に関するトラブル等には、管理人は対応致しません。トゥートしたご本人に法的な責任が生じます。発言内容については、十分気を付けてトゥートして下さい。他の人の不快になるようなコメントを発言する方は、即座にアカウントを停止等を致します。本インスタンスを快適にご利用頂けるようご協力をお願いします。  ※自費で運営しておりますので、サーバの処理能力が非常に低スペックです。サーバーに負荷の掛かる行為は禁止させて頂きます。一度に30件以上のCSVフォローリストをインポートすると、処理能力を超えてしまいます。大量のフォローリストのインポート等は絶対にお控え下さい。Pawoo等と比べると数千倍のサーバスペックの差がありますので、ご理解頂ければ幸いです。 ※インスタンステーマと関係のない宣伝目的のアカウントは即時アカウントを削除致します。貧弱サーバなんです。 ※捜査機関等からの要請が来た場合は、アドレス等の個人情報を提供する可能性がございます。 ※サーバー費用等の負担が結構大きい為、今後運営費を賄う為に、広告等が入る可能性がございます。最終的に毎月ウン十万程度のサーバー費用が掛かる可能性もございます。 ご投稿頂いたトゥートは、多媒体での紹介や人口知能を用いたサービスで利用させて頂く場合がございます。収益が発生した場合は、運営しているインスタンスを継続させる為の費用（サーバー代、運営費等）に充てさせて頂きます。  ※利用規約に変更があった場合はこちらのページにてご報告致します。当インスタンスが別途定める場合を除き、本ページ上に規約を表示した時点より効力が生じるものとします。  ※このインスタンスの利用に際し、利用規約の解釈及び適用については、日本の法律に準拠いたします。本規約に関連する一切の紛争は、東京地方裁判所を唯一の合意専属管轄裁判所とさせて頂きます。
</details>

## [podcast.style](https://podcast.style/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=podcast.style&view=local)
ポッドキャストを配信するポッドキャスターとポッドキャストリスナーのためのインスタンスです。
登録前にお願いをご一読ください

<details><summary>(more)</summary>
＝＝＝ お願い＝＝＝

ポッドキャストの配信者やリスナーの利用を想定してますが、話題については特定しませんのでご自由に
情報交換やコミュニケーションを目的としてますので一方的な告知の連投は避けていただければと
安定した運用をめざしますが、データの保存や動作を保証するものではありませんのでご了承ください
安定を求める場合は、他の大きなインスタンスの方が安心かもしれません
限られたリソースで運用しています。Botなどによる大量の投稿やフォローなどはご遠慮ください
公序良俗に反する投稿は控え、閲覧に注意が必要な内容は、必ずCWやNSFWを使ってください
良識を持って楽しく使って生きましょう

＝＝＝ 機能について＝＝＝

他のインスタンスの人をリモートフォローしたり、他からリモートフォローすることもできます
他のインスタンスから見られたくない場合は非公開アカウントにしてください
ミュートするとフォローしたまま投稿が見えなくなります
公開、未収載の投稿（トゥート）はマストドンを使っていない人からも見られる公のものです
公開はタイムラインに流れ、未収載はタイムラインに流れません（@通知などに利用）
非公開はインスタンス内のフォロワーだけ見ることができます
ダイレクトは@でメンションをした人だけに公開します（インスタンス 外へのものは要注意）

＝＝＝ 運営＝＝＝
このインスタンスは Whizzo Production が管理・運営しています。
要望やご質問は メールフォーム から。

</details>

Email: [mail@whizzo.jp](mailto:mail@whizzo.jp)

Admin: [@potaufeu@podcast.style](https://podcast.style/@potaufeu)

## [wsup.social](https://wsup.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=wsup.social&view=local)
Wsup! This is an independent Mastodon instance currently open to registrations. Welcome!

<details><summary>(more)</summary>This is a Mastodon instance in the cloud.
Anyone is free to join, as long as the person is not a jerk.
Support with Bitcoin: 19oNEzUyfLLkKCWV9Vxjti5wCcTVwsVjfT
The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of wsup.social; they are here to provide you with an insight into content moderation policies:


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of this service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Email: Not Available

Admin: [@denmojo@wsup.social](https://wsup.social/@denmojo)

## [go-newbie.club](https://go-newbie.club/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=go-newbie.club&view=local)
囲碁○新米●倶楽部

囲碁をこれから始めたい、始めたばかり、長くやってるけどなかなか上達しない、昔ルールを習ったがよくわからないうちにそれっきりになってしまった、そんな皆さんのための小さな碁盤（9路盤・13路盤）を中心にした情報交換の場です。というのは、あるていど囲碁が打てる人のための大きな碁盤（19路盤）についての情報なら書店・ネット・テレビなどにたくさんあるからです。

もう１９路盤でガンガン打っているという方もぜひアドバイザーとしてご参加ください。

棋譜の投稿にはつぶや棋譜が便利です。盤上に棋譜を入力した後、「URL作成のみ」ボタンを押し、できたURLを本文に貼り付けてください。

管理人はこちらです。よろしければフォローお願いします。

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Mastodon インスタンス「囲碁囲碁○新米●倶楽部」は株式会社きっずファイブが運営します。

利用規約

１．利用規約の適用 
株式会社きっずファイブ（以下「当社」といいます）は、利用者にソーシャルネットワーキングサービス（以下、「本サービス」といいます）を提供するため、以下に本サービス利用規約（以下、「本規約」といいます）を定め、利用者は、本規約により本サービスを利用するものとします。


２．禁止行為 
利用者は、本サービスの利用にあたり、次のいずれかに該当する行為をしてはならないものとします。なお、禁止行為に該当するかどうは、当社が独自の判断で行うことができるものとし、掲載情報の変更、登録削除を含めた適切な処置をとります。

(1) 他人に迷惑をかけたり不快感を与える行為
(2) 法令又は公序良俗に反する行為
(3) 会員ＩＤやパスワードを不正に使う行為
(4)システムに負担をかける行為
(5)１人で複数のＩＤを持つ行為
(6)１つのＩＤを複数人で利用する行為
(7)無差別に面識のない人を招待する行為
(8) その他、当社が不適当と判断した行為 

３．免責事項 
利用者は、本サービス内での自らの行為において責任を負うものとします。
当社は、本サービスをいつでも任意の理由で中止することができます。
当社は、本サービスの利用、または利用ができないことによって引き起こされた（直接的、間接的を問わず）損害について、一切責任を負いません。

４．利用者の同意、法的手続き 
利用者は、本サービス を利用することにより、この利用規約すべての記載内容について、同意されたものとみなされます。またこの利用規約は当社の判断で任意に変更されます。将来引き続きご利用になる場合は、その時点での内容に同意されているとみなされます。

この利用規約の準拠法は日本法とします。また、本サービス またはこの規約に関連して当社と皆様の間で生じた紛争については京都地方裁判所を第一審専属管轄裁判所とします。
</details>

Email: [masamitu@kids5.com](mailto:masamitu@kids5.com)

Admin: [@igokyoto@go-newbie.club](https://go-newbie.club/@igokyoto)

## [mental.social](https://mental.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mental.social&view=local)
メンタルヘルスをテーマとするインスタンスです。
心の病気、発達障害、さまざまなマイノリティなどを扱います。
上記に当てはまらないような方も、疲れたときや、鍵アカの置き場などにどうぞ。
投稿の内容は限定しませんが、法に触れる行為、人に迷惑をかける行為はご遠慮ください。
医療行為にあたる可能性があるので、他の人の病名を決めつけたりする行為も禁止です。
情報の活用については自己責任です。
ネット上の情報をうのみにせず、医療機関の適切な受診をお願いします。

管理人はADHDなのでサーバーの運用に過度な期待は持たないほうがよいです。


<details><summary>(more)</summary>AGPLv3に基づき、サーバーのソースコードをGitHubで公開しています。

## [animalliberation.social](https://animalliberation.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=animalliberation.social&view=local)
Animal Liberation Network is a community for animal activists on the Mastodon network. You can connect with other activists through the local timeline, as well as spread your activism to the outside world with the federated timeline. Please read our rules!

<details><summary>(more)</summary>This is a website by and for animal activists.
The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of animalliberation.social; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Speciesism or advocation of speciesism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Email: [alex@alexgleason.me](mailto:alex@alexgleason.me)

Admin: [@alex@animalliberation.social](https://animalliberation.social/@alex)

## [mastodon.night.coffee](https://mastodon.night.coffee/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.night.coffee&view=local)
Mastodon instance based in Oklahoma, USA for night.coffee and friends. We are one of many federated Mastodon instances and aim to be friendly and socially responsible. See our extended about page for more details.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>mastodon.night.coffee
We're a laid back instance that enjoys the finer points of geek culture. Don't be a douche/nazi.
The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of mastodon.night.coffee; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.
Bot software that automates posts, aggregates other user content, or other such behavior is considered spam and will result in an immediate silence or suspension of the account.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.

First, here are the main ideas behind our rules that should be yours:

The respect of others is primary.

Rules of Aleph.land

You can be suspended for:


Sharing content that is illegal in France (pedophilia, mainly).
Taking part of a harassment.
Putting someone in danger.
Having a racist, sexist, discriminating or oppressive talk.
Voluntarily degrading the prosperity or the good atmosphere of the instance.


You can be muted from the public timelines for:

nudity (#nude)
gore (#gore)
pornography (#porn)
a flashy media that could be harmful for photosensitive people (#epilepsywarning)
spoil (#spoil)


Unpleasant shitposting or flooding.
Making abusive ads.
Posting automatic toots from another source.



Please keep in mind that this rules are here to guarantee a good experience to everyone on the instance. Also, this list is not exhaustive and moderators will do their best to solve problems that may not have been specified here.

## [tsuruga.net](https://tsuruga.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=tsuruga.net&view=local)
敦賀を盛り上げるために作ったMastodon（マストドン）です。
敦賀市民はもちろん敦賀出身者やそれ以外の方も大歓迎です！

アカウント作成手順
１．ユーザー名を半角英数で入力します。（登録後変更不可）
２．メールアドレスとパスワードを入力して参加するをクリックします。
３．その後、登録したアドレス宛てに確認用のメールが届きます。受信トレイではなく「迷惑メールフォルダ」に入る場合もありますのでご注意ください。
４．受信したメールにある「メールアドレス確認」をクリックしてください。
５．以上でアカウント作成は完了です。楽しいマストドンライフを！

ルール
皆さんが気持ちよくご利用頂けるようご配慮をお願いします。
ネタバレやその他の理由によりユーザーへの配慮が必要な投稿の場合はCWタグやNSFWタグを付けてください。（CWタグ･NSFWタグについてはこちらをご覧ください）
上記タグを付けている場合でもR-18コンテンツのトゥート（投稿）は禁止です。
当方でもセキュリティ対策を行っておりますが、パスワードの使いまわしはご遠慮ください。
データの消失に対しては責任を負いかねますので予めご了承ください。

禁止行為

公序良俗に反する行為
日本国内の法律に違反する行為
他者に中傷・脅迫・経済的もしくは精神的に損害や不利益を与える行為
実在の人物・団体などになりすます行為
サーバに極端な負荷をかける行為

これらの行為が見られる場合、予告なくアカウントをブロックし参加をお断りさせて頂きます。
お問い合わせ先
メール　mastodon@eigadaisuke.com
メールフォーム　http://eigadaisuke.com/contact/
支援（サーバー維持費は個人負担のためご支援頂けると助かります）
Enty　https://enty.jp/eigadaisuke
DYC's STORE　https://dycmovie.stores.jp/
ウィッシュリスト　http://amzn.asia/49YPek4

オフィシャルサイト 映画監督山下大裕の2020年全国公開への道

<details><summary>(more)</summary>運営者プロフィール
山下大裕（やました･だいすけ）
1992年6月9日生まれ、24歳。福井県敦賀市出身、東京在住。福井県立敦賀高等学校普通科を経て日本映画大学映画学部映画学科脚本演出コース1期卒業。20歳の冬を迎えた2013年、地元敦賀を舞台にした自主製作映画『SNOWGIRL』(62分)を初監督。その2年後、2015年には敦賀映画第2弾と銘打ちオール敦賀ロケで『弥生の虹』(74分)を監督。18歳の頃から“2020年までに全国公開作を撮る”と公言し『映画で敦賀を盛り上げる』をテーマに日々奮闘中。2017年現在、敦賀市の委託を受け観光ショートムービー『いつか、きらめきたくて。』（全4話）を製作中。

## [mstdn.oresys.nagoya](https://mstdn.oresys.nagoya/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.oresys.nagoya&view=local)
Mastodon名古屋サーバです。
名古屋市民限定、名古屋の話題限定、というわけではありません。どなたでもご利用いただけます
使用前に詳細説明をよくお読みください。

<details><summary>(more)</summary>このインスタンスについて
ご紹介
私こと @kumasun が個人で運用している、無所属のパブリックインスタンスです。
.nagoyaドメインでホスティングされているため、「名古屋鯖」と呼んでいます。
運営方針は未だ流動的ですが、どうやら地域インスタンスとして認識され始めてきているようです。
(名古屋市民限定、名古屋の話題限定、というわけではありません。どなたでもご利用いただけます。)
運営方針についてのご意見も広く募集しております。
運用上、重要なお知らせは @admin より発信します。ハッシュタグは
 #名古屋運営 です。
アカウント削除をご希望の場合は、管理者宛にDMください。

ローカルルール

年齢制限：17+
いい感じに、仲良く使ってね


Bot運用ルール
当インスタンスにおいて、Bot(自動的にトゥート等を行う、又は、ユーザー情報等を収集するプログラム)に用いるアカウントを開設・運用する場合は、下記ルールに従ってください。

ユーザー名にBotであることを明記し、プロフィール欄に運用目的及び運用者の連絡先を記載してください。
自動トゥートの公開範囲は非収載・非公開・ダイレクトのみとし、ユーザーの自動フォローは禁止します。
頻繁なトゥート等、サーバに負荷をかける行為は禁止します。
営利目的での使用は禁止します。

ただし、ユーザーにとって有益なものに関してはこの限りではありません。まずはご相談ください。

その他留意事項

自動でフォロー等を行うスクリプトの使用は、ご遠慮ください。


支援のお願い
下記の支援をお願いしております。ご協力頂ける場合はお声がけください。

運営費 … インフラ保守費等(サービスURL準備中)
技術支援 … Git/Nginx/Ruby on Rails/PostgreSQL/Redis


免責事項

各種サービスまたは各種情報の提供またはその遅滞、変更、中断、中止、停止もしくは廃止、その他当サーバに関連して発生した全ての損害について、運営者は一切の責任を負わないものとします。
個人情報の保護に十分な注意を払いますが、情報の漏洩、消失、第三者による改ざん等の防止の保証はできません。したがって、情報の漏洩、消失、第三者による改ざん等により発生した全ての損害について、運営者は一切の責任を負担いたしません。
メールアドレスおよびパスワードの管理は、ユーザー自身の責任で行うものとします。ユーザーのメールアドレスおよびパスワードの管理不十分による第三者の利用、使用過誤等に起因する損害等について、運営者は一切責任を負いません。
当サイトに投稿された内容について、その正確性を保証するものではありません。投稿内容に起因する損害等について、運営者は一切責任を負いません。

※つまり、何かあっても責任はとれません。
このルールおよび各条件は随時更新されます。
</details>

Admin: [@admin@mstdn.oresys.nagoya](https://mstdn.oresys.nagoya/@admin)

基本的には公序良俗の範疇で。あんまし小学生とかに適切でないかも？という文章は CW (Content Warning) を、画像には NSFW (Not suitable for work;職場閲覧不適切) をつけましょう。つけても法にふれるようなのはダメです

## [social.csswg.org](https://social.csswg.org/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=social.csswg.org&view=local)
Mastodon server for anyone interested in CSS or general web development

<details><summary>(more)</summary>The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of social.csswg.org; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:

The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:

Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence

The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:

Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism

The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:

Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism

Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:

Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.


These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Email: [csswg@csswg.org](mailto:csswg@csswg.org)

Admin: [@csswg@social.csswg.org](https://social.csswg.org/@csswg)

小説ファンや、小説家志望者の為の日本初のマストドン、それが小説ドンです。好きな小説の感想の共有や、新しい小説との出会いの場としてご活用下さい！
言葉で物語世界を構築する小説は、一番心に響くストーリー媒体だと思います。一度、小説を読み始めるとドップリとその世界観に浸ってしまいますね。皆様の思い出に残る小説を教えて下さい！僕が一番最初に読んだ小説は、小学校の時に読んだHGウェルズのタイムマシンです。古い小説なのに、物凄く面白い！！！という胸躍る感覚を今でも覚えています。最近読んで心に残っているのは、トム・ソーヤーの冒険。1876年の小説ですが、ハリウッド映画の原点みたいな雰囲気がありました。面白かったなぁ…

## [mastodon.rocks](https://mastodon.rocks/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.rocks&view=local)
Because Mastodon rocks !

<details><summary>(more)</summary>English
Welcome
Here some resources to understand Mastodon :

Welcome to Mastodon by @Gargron
Bye, Twitter. All the cool kids are migrating to Mastodon by Mashable

Rules

No illegal content. The server is hosted in France : racism, apology for terrorism, bullying, defamation, violations privacy rights and child pornograhy are illegal under French law.
No oppressive content (sexism, homophobia, etc).
No parody account.
No bot (for the moment).
Any graphical content have to contain a Content Warning.
No explicit sexual content in the public timeline without content warning (you can configure your toot privacy on "public but do not display on public timeline").

Mobile applications

Android : Tusky
iOS : Amaroq for Mastodon
Full list

Support Mastodon

The code source can be found here : Github
You can help the developer of Mastodon on Patreon


Support this instance mastodon.rocks





Français
Bienvenue
Voici quelques ressources pour comprendre Mastodon :

Welcome to Mastodon par @Alda
Découvrez Mastodon, un clone de Twitter libre, open source et décentralisé par @Numerama
Le réseau social Mastodon, un « Twitter plus proche de l’esprit originel » par @Willvs (pour Le Monde)

Règles

Tout contenu doit respecter la loi relative à l'hébergement de contenu sur Internet.
Tout contenu oppressif (sexiste, homophobe, etc.) entraîne un ban.
Pas de compte parodique.
Bots fortement déconseillés (pour l'instant).
Les médias violents doivent obligatoirement être accompagnés d'un Content Warning.
Pas de contenu sexuel sans content warning dans la TL publique (il vous suffit de mettre les toots en "public but do not display on public timeline").

Applications mobiles

Android : Tusky
iOS : Amaroq for Mastodon
La liste complète

Contribuer à Mastodon

Le code source est disponible sur Github
Vous pouvez aider financièrement le développeur sur Patreon


Aider cette instance mastodon.rocks


</details>

## [mastodon.mit.edu](https://mastodon.mit.edu/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.mit.edu&view=local)

mastodon.mit.edu


<details><summary>(more)</summary>The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of mastodon.mit.edu; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:

The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
   
Excessive advertising
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence


The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
   
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism
Content in violation of US law


Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
   
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Admin: [@mastodon@mastodon.mit.edu](https://mastodon.mit.edu/@mastodon)

ルールなど

 実在の人物・団体などのなりすましは禁止です

 明確にBOTと判断できない形で、交流を目的としない自動投稿および連携投稿は禁止します。

## [framapiaf.org](https://framapiaf.org/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=framapiaf.org&view=local)

framapiaf.org


<details><summary>(more)</summary>Conditions d'utilisation
Version courte (TL;DR comme on dit chez nous) (version longue)
On est sympathiques :

Votre contenu vous appartient (mais nous vous encourageons à le publier sous licence libre) ;
Framasoft n’exploitera pas vos données personnelles, sauf à fin de statistiques internes (anonymisées) ou pour vous prévenir d’un changement important sur le service ;
Framasoft ne transmettra ni ne revendra vos données personnelles (votre vie privée nous tient - vraiment - à cœur) ;
Les engagements de Framasoft résultent d’une démarche militante inspirée du mouvement de l’éducation populaire, vous pouvez les retrouver dans notre Charte des services Libres, Ethiques, Décentralisés et Solidaires.

Mais il ne faut pas nous prendre pour autant pour des chatons :


« La loi est la loi, et on ne veut pas finir en taule »
Vous devez respecter la loi (que celle-ci soit bien faite ou idiote), sinon votre compte sera supprimé


« Merci d’être poli et respectueux avec ses voisins de service »
Vous devez respecter les autres utilisateurs en faisant preuve de civisme et de politesse, sinon votre contenu, voire votre compte, pourront être supprimés, sans négociation

« Si ça casse, on n’est pas obligé de réparer »
Framasoft propose ce service gratuitement et librement. Si vous perdez des données, par votre faute ou par la nôtre, désolé, mais ça arrive. Nous ferons ce que nous pouvons pour les récupérer, mais nous ne nous assignons aucune obligation de résultat. En clair, évitez de mettre des données sensibles ou importantes sur les services Framasoft, car en cas de perte, nous ne garantissons pas leur récupération

« Si vous n’êtes pas contents, vous êtes invités à aller voir ailleurs »
Si le service ne vous convient pas, libre à vous d’en trouver un équivalent (ou meilleur) ailleurs, ou de monter le vôtre

« Tout abus sera puni »
Si un utilisateur abuse du service, par exemple en monopolisant des ressources machines partagées, ou en publiant des contenus considérés comme non pertinents, son contenu ou son compte pourra être supprimé sans avertissement ni négociation. Framasoft reste seul juge de cette notion « d’abus » dans le but de fournir le meilleur service possible à l’ensemble de ses utilisateurs. Si cela vous parait anti-démocratique, anti-libriste, anti-liberté-d’expression, merci de vous référer à la clause précédente

« Rien n’est éternel »
Les services peuvent fermer (faute de fonds pour les maintenir, par exemple), ils peuvent être victimes d’intrusion (le « 100 % sécurisé » n’existe pas). Nous vous encourageons donc à conserver une copie des données qui vous importent, car Framasoft ne saurait être tenu pour responsable de leur hébergement sans limite de temps
</details>

Email: [https://contact.framasoft.org](mailto:https://contact.framasoft.org)

Admin: [@Framasoft@framapiaf.org](https://framapiaf.org/@Framasoft)

Elle est destinée à la famille, aux amis mais aussi aux amoureux de géo, de carto, d'opendata, aux libristes, geeks et makers de tous poils !

Cette chose tourne sur ma "Tour Infernale"... un Dell T7500 d'occasion (merci ebay) avec plein de coeurs (12) rapides (2 Xeon X5690 donc du 3.5GHz) de la RAM (96Go) des disques qui tournent et un qui tournent pas (oui, on dit "SSD").

## [soc.ialis.me](https://soc.ialis.me/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=soc.ialis.me&view=local)

A
generalist

<details><summary>(more)</summary>A generalist Mastodon instance hosted in France.


Our guidelines are currently being written ; but basically:


don't be a dick,
no advertising, harassment, spam,
no abuse on the API by local users (bots, ...),
Any thing illegal under the French law will be removed and reported to the competent authorities.


Informations and status about the instance is posted to @admin.

Currently the only human administrating this instance is @href. Other administrators may be added in the future, as I (href) prefer focusing on managing the servers and the underlying infrastructure than people.


Don't hesitate to ping either @href or @admin to talk about the instance, create an issue at hrefhref/mastodon on GitHub, or privately at admin (at) soc.ialis.me.

The instance itself is hosted on servers at Online.net and Scaleway.com, in Paris, France. The database and files are frequently replicated on a couple of servers, and externally backuped.

The servers are run by an organization (with no legal grounds; entierly privately owned)  called random.sh / random labs; which hosts other services such as irc.random.sh, a ChatSpike.net IRC Server, Etherpad.fr, and much more. I also intend to one day make it my own company for some products, but I'll then separate the business with theses community services (the business will just be a sponsor, and without any advertisement, tracking, or anything else evil).

The bird escaped, don't worry. Mastodons aren't that good at aiming.

</details>

<details><summary>(more)</summary>This instance tracks https://github.com/d3vgru/mastodon which is a dev fork of Mastodon so it might not be like totally stable or anything.

If I can get the new UI working, I'd like to add P2P capabilities so these networks can run more like torrent sharing and less like downloading from a server.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Since "Be excellent to each other" is much easier said than done, we have a (non-exhaustive) list of behaviours that may lead to deletion of toots, and silencing or suspension of accounts, if problems persist. In particular, we do not tolerate:

Harrassment, stalking, doxxing
Racism, sexism, verbal abuse or advocation thereof
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Violent nationalist propaganda, Nazi symbolism or promoting the ideology of National Socialism
Contacting people who made clear they want no contact. Dogpiling/brigading
Untagged sexual content, gore, or advertisement
Untagged, or automated, or excessive advertisement
Bots interacting with users without their explicit requests

Please report behaviour that bothers you. That includes behaviour from other instances - we are very willing stop federating with asshole instances.
You can find further information on our instance in our GitHub repository, which also provides a list of currently blocked or silenced instances, alongside with reasons.

一介のWebデザイナーが立てたインスタンスやさかい、サービスの永続性は保証できまへん。「万が一、データが消えても問題ないで」と思うてくださる、心の広〜い方のみご登録ください。
Mastodonの仕組みが気に入らはったら、企業はんが運営してはる堅牢なインスタンスにも登録しはったらよろしおすえ。
登録時の注意
パスワードの使い回しはあきまへん。ノーセキュリティノーライフどす
hotmailとoutlookのメールアドレスやと、うちからのメールが届かへんらしいのどす。その他のメールアドレスで登録しておくれやす
うちからのメールは迷惑メールに振り分けられやすいんどす。届かへんなーと思わはったら、迷惑メールフォルダを確認しておくれやす

他のユーザーへの迷惑行為、およびサーバの負荷に繋がる極端な行為があった場合、予告なくアカウントを凍結します

## [myfreckle.com](https://myfreckle.com/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=myfreckle.com&view=local)

myfreckle.com


<details><summary>(more)</summary>About myfreckle.com:
We believe Social Media is changing the world.  

This instance is for people who are fascinated with and enjoy being part of the change that Social Media is bringing.  

This instance has been set-up and continues to be maintained by professional developers.  This instance is hosted on Amazon AWS infrastructure.  We realise dependable infrastructure is important for a Social Media network to remain useful. 
The following guidelines are not a legal document, and the final interpretation is up to the administration of myfreckle.com; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:
General Rules and Guidelines

Be nice to each other.
Use common sense.
Corporate accounts are welcome, but don’t overdo the posting and no direct advertising.
Parody accounts are fine (identify your account as a parody), impersonation of others is not allowed.
Bots are not allowed to post to the public timeline unless permission has been received from an admin.
Automated posting is not allowed unless permission has been received from an admin.
Content / behaviour that is illegal in the United States of America, Canada, France, Germany, United Kingdom or Australia is not permitted on this instance.  Breach of this will result in a permanent ban of the account.

The following content will be removed from the timeline and will get your account permanently banned:

Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism
Pornography and sexually explicit content
Gore and extremely graphic violence



Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:

Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.
The administrators reserves the right of admission to this instance and the right to change the above from time to time except where limited by law.



If there are any comments, questions please email the admins at freckle@myfreckle.com - please be patient as a response may take some time.
</details>

Email: [freckle@myfreckle.com](mailto:freckle@myfreckle.com)

Admin: Not Available

## [m.massy.city](https://m.massy.city/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=m.massy.city&view=local)

Une instance Mastodon dédiée aux habitants de Massy (91) en France, tenue à jour et fournie par StrangeBlackHole SAS une entreprise Massicoise. Hébergée en France, l'un de ses objectif premier est la transparence mais aussi de fournir un outil de réseautage local et des services associés. La modération est collaborative, n’hésitez surtout pas à rapporter tout contenu problématique !
Cette instance n'a aucun lien avec la municipalité et ne dépend d'aucun parti politique ou courant de pensée. Elle sera ce que vous en ferez.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Quelques règles
Sur cette instance les règles sont simples. Aucun sexisme, racisme, homophobie, âgisme, grossophobie ou psychophobie, etc... n’est toléré. Tout message de haine est proscrit, les fascistes et leurs copains nazis, les fous de dieu intégristes en tout genre sont directement bannis. La publication de contenu pornographique non désigné comme tel avec un “Content Warning” (CW) mènent aussi à une exclusion du serveur. Cette instance Mastodon se veut inclusive et bienveillante, ainsi nous bannirons sans prévenir et sans regret. Les comptes bannis ne sont plus accessibles depuis notre instance, vous ne pouvez plus voir leur contenu ni les suivre.
Nous encourageons nos utilisateur-ice-s à utiliser la fonction de rapport (“Report”) pour nous faire part du contenu et/ou des comptes allant à l’encontre de nos règles. D'ailleurs si celles-ci ne vous conviennent pas, ne râlez pas, trouvez simplement un autre serveur.
Notre réseau social, et son réseau entier selon nous, est dédié à la réappropriation des moyens de communication et à la création de communautés meilleures pour le collectif. Les catégories de personnes citées dans le paragraphe précédent n'oeuvrant pas du tout (allant même dans le sens contraire) à la réalisation de ces objectifs, elles sont logiquement pas les bienvenues. Merci de rapporter leur présence si vous les croisez sur notre serveur.
Ces règles sont inspirées par celles écrites pour l'instance unixcorn, merci à eux.
</details>

Email: [contact@massy.city](mailto:contact@massy.city)

Admin: [@fabrice@m.massy.city](https://m.massy.city/@fabrice)

## [mastodon.org.uk](https://mastodon.org.uk/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.org.uk&view=local)
Statistics












How does it work? When you create an account on Mastodon, you create an account on the website you currently are visiting. For example, here you are on mastodon.org.uk. That is your instance.

You will notice after log in two different timelines, the Local and the Federated.
The local timeline is all the public toots of all our local users ( the one who registered on mastodon.org.uk and use it to access the Mastodon federation ).
The federated timeline adds the public toots of all the users that our local users are following in other servers/
Need to know users 
@xvilo Is the maintainer of this instance.
@STATUS Gives you information about this instance.
@userscount Gives us detailed info about users and toots.

Bots on this instance 
@STATUS Gives us an automated heads up when there is a new Mastodon Version available.
@userscount Gives us detailed info about users and toots. Source on Github
@bigben Toots the time. Source on Github. Maintained by @followthesam
	Bots are welcome here but please not that bots will be silenced when posting too much (e.g. flooding local timeline). If you have a bot, please contact me (@xvilo). I can add it to the list. 
	Bots will be banned if they post inappropriate content or if I (@xvilo) get many complaints about it.

## [mstdn.pw](https://mstdn.pw/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.pw&view=local)
mstdn.pw is a Mastodon instance that promotes healthy and open expression of individuals, ideas, and content. As you would expect,
 free speech is encouraged and viewed in high regard as is open discussion, spanning a multitude of viewpoints and among all users.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>There are few rules here as we operate on the assumption that most users are not malicious in intent.
Rules:

Illegal content - no illegal content is allowed, including but not limited to underage content with the depiction of minors in any sexual context.
Non-consent - no content depicting anyone being forced against their will for entertainment. Exceptions include videos on real world events that have a societal impact. This content should help raise awareness and educate, and stir up healthy discussions.
Harassment - discussion, including disagreements, are encouraged, but harassment of other users is prohibited. We are defining harassment as: anything intending to incite others and elicit negative emotions and reactions from other users while not contributing to worthwhile discussion. Having one's feelings hurt and being offended by another user's opinions and world views does not constitute harassment. When in doubt, follow this piece of advice: Don't be a dick.
Circumventing blocks/suspensions - this is a great way to be removed from the instance. If someone blocks you, just leave it be. Going around the blocks to engage someone is harassment.

Considerations
Do keep in mind that we are part of a community. Please be considerate of others and use the CW and NSFW flags for content warranting it. However, this is not a requirement, and content will NOT be removed for disregarding this request.
Personal Responsibility
You're responsible for your content, the content you view, and your interactions with other users. This platform gives great granular support to each individual user and instance alike. Please make yourself familiar with the controls if you are not familiar with them already.
If you want content tailored to your liking, we're not sure this is the place for you, but you are allowed and encouraged to follow, unfollow, block, and unblock users as you see fit. We don't expect everybody will along all the time, so use these functions as you please. You control the flow of the information you see.
You're responsible for what you toot, boost, and favorite. Nobody will warn you when you get too close to the line and stop you before you cross it. We will work on the assumption that you were raised as part of a community, so we expect you know how to act alongside others. If you lack social skills or just want guidance, feel free to contact our admins for information.
If you feel like you're getting too emotionally involved, allowing yourself to be distracted from work or from spending time with loved ones, know when to walk away. Nobody else knows your limit better than you do.
</details>

Email: [jake@eightsix.in](mailto:jake@eightsix.in)

Admin: [@jake@mstdn.pw](https://mstdn.pw/@jake)

## [gundam.masto.host](https://gundam.masto.host/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=gundam.masto.host&view=local)

SIDE7とは

ここは機動戦士ガンダムシリーズ好きが集まるMastodonです。
初代から最新作まで時代と世代を超えて語り合いましょう。
アニメに限らずガンダムの話題であればどの媒体の話でもOKです。

This is Mastodon where Mobile Suit Gundam series fans gather.
Let's talk over time and generations from original work to latest work.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>
サーバー

このサーバーはhttps://masto.host/上で稼動しています。
現在100人程度を収容可能な体制で運用していますが、今後の状況次第では拡張する可能性があります。そして同時に(無いとは思いますが)予告無く閉鎖する可能性もありますので、データのエクスポートは定期的にお願いします。
------------------------------

ルール

・法律に反する内容の投稿
・宣伝行為(営利・非営利不問)
・誹謗中傷
・その他公序良俗に反する事

上記の行為と管理者が判断した場合、サイレンス(透明NG)や最悪アカウント停止などの措置に踏み切る可能性があります。あんまりそういうことはしたくないので、楽しく穏便に安全に遊んでください。何かあったら管理者に相談してください。ケンカダメゼッタイ！

mastdonの仕様上”アカウントの削除”はできません。
アカウント停止は可能ですので管理者まで申し出てください。
------------------------------

お世話になってるインスタンス(順不同)

https://mast.moe/

## [clacks.link](https://clacks.link/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=clacks.link&view=local)
Welcome to The Clacks
Named after the transcontinental communications network from Terry Pratchett's Discworld.


<details><summary>(more)</summary>Welcome to the Clacks. I created this instance for my own use, and perhaps my friends if they are interested. I have decided to keep signups open for now, but will close them down if it becomes an issue.
Follow @tithonium for status updates, planned downtimes, upgrade announcements, etc. If this instance gets busy enough, I'll probably create a separate account so you don't have to follow my other nonsense.
Also: I tend to run against the master branch, and update when I remember to. Bugs happen.
Rule Overview
Most of the rules boil down to:

Don't be a dick
Don't get me in trouble with the law or my network provider
Don't embarrass me in front of the other Mastodon admins
You're literally in my house; Don't give me a reason to kick you out

The Clacks is hosted on a physical server owned by me, @tithonium, located in my office at home, on my own internet connection. When it comes down to it, you are in my home and I decide if you get to be here.
If you cause problems, I will deal with you based on my perception of the severity. This could be anywhere from [telling you to knock it off] up to [deleting your account and everything associated with it, blocking your IPs at the firewall, and reporting you to your ISP and law enforcement].
Please don't make me do the latter. Seriously.
I will try to avoid blocking /entire/ instances, but will do so when necessary. If and when I do start blocking users or instances at a site level, I will try to remember to maintain a list here.
I will also try to remember to announce when I change these rules. But I've also included a revision date down at the bottom.
Finally: I'd love to switch out the default Mastodon images and such for something more thematically appropriate, if any artists would be willing to help out for the pittance I can justify spending on this project.

Some Specific Rules
(lifted from other Mastodon instances)
The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of clacks.link; they are here to provide you with an insight into my content moderation policies:
Please report violations of these rules by local users as needed. This site is not responsible for, and has little control over, the actions and content of users of other federated sites. That said, if a non-local user is a problem, please do let us know about that too, so we can decide how we need to handle it.


    The following types of accounts are disallowed:
    
RSS-feed bots not connected to feeds of a Clacks user.
Commercial/Advertising accounts
Parody accounts

    In addition, accounts that go unverified or unused for a long period will be suspended.
  

    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged or Excessive advertising
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence
Misinformation for a purpose other than to entertain

My rules about NSFW-tagging-required may change in the future, I'm not entirely sold on it.


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Nazi symbolism, for purposes other than analysis or commentary
Confederate symbolism, for purposes other than analysis or commentary
Content illegal in the state of Washington



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed in bios and avatars:
    
Sexual content of any sort
Violent content of any sort
Images that flash or change rapidly



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason.
Last Revision: 2017-05-06
</details>

Email: [admin@clacks.link](mailto:admin@clacks.link)

Admin: [@tithonium@clacks.link](https://clacks.link/@tithonium)

## [oransns.com](https://oransns.com/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=oransns.com&view=local)
Google+からやってきたが誰もおらんインスタンス。botが蔓延っていおり、LTLの投稿は全てbotによるものだと言われている。

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Google+からやってきたが誰もおらんインスタンス。botが蔓延っていおり、LTLの投稿は全てbotによるものだと言われている──

　謎に満ち溢れたおらんインスタンスは、とある一滴の雫から人の手を借りず自然発生的に生み出された。世界は人を作るはずだったが、最初にbotを作り、最後に人を作った。人の人権など皆無で、botの権力が猛威を振るう。人はbotの脅威から恐れ逃げ回っていたが、いつしかbotの手により人間たちは駆逐されていった。
　人間たちは考えた、botに駆逐されない。安寧を手に入れるための術を。人は、自らをbotと虚偽することによって暗闇の中繁栄する道を選んだのだ。人は、同じ言葉を繰り返し話した。人は、軽く謝った後によく聞こえなかった旨を何度も繰り返し伝えた。こうして、botにbotだと認められた人間たちはいまでもこの世界に存在しているという──
人間だけがいないインスタンス、おらんSNS。
</details>

## [vocalomakets.jp](https://vocalomakets.jp/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=vocalomakets.jp&view=local)
「結月ゆかり」を企画したボカロP集団「VOCALOMAKETS」が運営するMastodonです。「結月ゆかり」に関する情報発信・情報交換・交流などを目的として立ち上げました。
※ 登録の確認メールが届かない場合は、迷惑メールに振り分けられないように「vocalomakets.jp」ドメインの受信を許可してください。

<details><summary>(more)</summary>お断り

主な目的は「結月ゆかり」を中心に公式からの情報発信、皆様からのご意見や情報の収集、そして交流の場として使用できればと考えております。
法律に違反するようなご使用、サーバーに過度の負担がかかるご使用はご遠慮ください。
18禁になりそうな内容には「Content Warning」タグを、画像には「NSFW」タグを付けてください。
当サイトをご使用することによって生じた損害などに関して、申し訳ございませんが一切の責任は負えません。
サーバー運営は全くの初心者ですので、不慣れな点もございますが、何卒ご容赦いただけますと幸いです。
上記内容は予告なく変更されることがありますことをご了承ください。

（更新日：2017年04月27日）

結月ゆかりについて
7名のボカロP集団「VOCALOMAKETS」による企画、株式会社AHSによる制作・販売で生まれた音声合成ソフトです。しっかりとしたきれいな歌声を持つ女性をベースに製作した「VOCALOID4 結月ゆかり」、大人の女性の情感あふれる声をベースとした入力文字読み上げソフト「VOICEROID2 結月ゆかり」、追加音声の「exVOICE」とバリエーション豊かなライブラリとなっております。

VOCALOID4　結月ゆかり｜製品情報｜AHS(AH-Software)
VOICEROID2 結月ゆかり｜製品情報｜AHS(AH-Software)


VOCALOMAKETSについて
「何かワクワクするような、面白い事」をしたいボカロPの集まりです。ボカロPが作るVOCALOIDのために集まりましたが、これに限らず今後も面白い事をしていきたいと思っています。

VOCALOMAKETS / ボカロマケッツ 公式サイト
VOCALOMAKETS blog | VOCALOMAKETSおよびそのメンバーの動向を紹介するブログ


</details>

Email: [contact@vocalomakets.com](mailto:contact@vocalomakets.com)

Admin: [@bumpyurushi@vocalomakets.jp](https://vocalomakets.jp/@bumpyurushi)

## [mastodon.huma-num.fr](https://mastodon.huma-num.fr/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.huma-num.fr&view=local)
L'instance mastodon d'Huma-Num est dédiée à l'enseignement supérieur et à la recherche. Elle se veut interdisciplinaire et ouverte à tous. Elle est mise en oeuvre et maintenue par la très grande infrastructure de recherche Huma-Num pour les sciences humaines et sociales numériques.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>A propos de cette instance
Instance mastodon dédiée à l'enseignement supérieur et à la recherche. Elle se veut interdisciplinaire et ouverte à tous. Elle est mise en oeuvre et maintenue par la TGIR Huma-Num.
Nous vous demandons de rester courtois et polis dans vos échanges. De plus, les contenus suivant sont strictement interdit : Raciste, sexiste, homophobe, apologie du terrorisme, incitation à la haine raciale ou au suicide, pornographie, etc. Nous nous réservons le droit de bloquer tout utilisateur ne respectant pas ces règles de base.

Huma-Num est une très grande infrastructure de recherche (TGIR) visant à faciliter le tournant numérique de la recherche en sciences humaines et sociales. Pour remplir cette mission, elle est bâtie sur une organisation originale consistant à mettre en œuvre un dispositif humain (concertation collective) et technologique (services numériques) à l’échelle nationale et européenne en s’appuyant sur un important réseau de partenaires et d’opérateurs.
La TGIR Huma-Num favorise ainsi, par l’intermédiaire de consortiums regroupant des acteurs des communautés scientifiques, la coordination de la production raisonnée et collective de corpus de sources (recommandations scientifiques, bonnes pratiques technologiques). Elle développe également un dispositif technologique unique permettant le traitement, la conservation, l'accès et l'interopérabilité des données de la recherche. Ce dispositif est composé de services dédiés, d'une plateforme d'accès unifié (ISIDORE) et d'une procédure d'archivage des données à long terme.
La TGIR Huma-Num propose en outre des guides de bonnes pratiques technologiques généralistes à destination des chercheurs. Elle peut mener ponctuellement des actions d'expertise et de formation. Elle porte la participation de la France dans le projet DARIAH en coordonnant les contributions nationales.
La TGIR Huma-Num est portée par l'Unité Mixte de Services 3598 associant le CNRS, l'Université d'Aix-Marseille et le Campus Condorcet.
Contacts
TGIR Huma-Num - UMS 3598
</details>

Email: [stephane.pouyllau@huma-num.fr](mailto:stephane.pouyllau@huma-num.fr)

Admin: [@spouyllau@mastodon.huma-num.fr](https://mastodon.huma-num.fr/@spouyllau)

## [talker.to](https://talker.to/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=talker.to&view=local)

A secure XMPP, Mumble and Mastodon Server.



/ XMPP In-band registration is enabled.

/ Server location: EU-Germany 

/ Webserver: Nginx

/ Mastodon: 1.2

/ XMPP: Prosody 0.9.12

/ Mumble: 1.2.12

<details><summary>(more)</summary>




Suspended & Silenced Servers

Silenced:

pawoo.net --> because of alot illegal media content
 Suspended: 
none so far --> shitposter.club is on the radar, because it is blocked on many other mastodon instances

Silence will make the account's posts invisible to anyone who isn't following them. Suspend will remove all of the account's content, media, and profile data.



 TALKER.TO Rules

This information is taken from mastodon.social and edited to match the needs of TALKER.TO

The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of TALKER.TO; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:


The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:

Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence

The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:

Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism

The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:

Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism
Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service.

This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:

Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.

These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
#

</details>

Email: [admin@talker.to](mailto:admin@talker.to)

Admin: [@dan@talker.to](https://talker.to/@dan)

## [eu1.mastoburn.com](https://eu1.mastoburn.com/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=eu1.mastoburn.com&view=local)
[FR]
Bienvenue sur MastoBurn !
Les inscriptions sont ouverte.
Cette instance possède la dernière version stable de Mastodon V1.3.3(08/05/2017 11h30)
Cette instance sera maintenue sur le long terme.
Cette instance est administrée par des passionnés de serveur et du Self-hosting, qui passe tous leurs temps libres à avaler de la documentation. Cette instance a pour but de contribuer au développement de Mastodon, réseau social Décentralisé.
N'hésitez pas à nous rejoindre et à partager l'instance Mastoburn à tous vos amis
Pour toutes questions sur notre instance contact@mastoburn.com
[EN]
Welcome to MastoBurn !
The sign up is open.
This Mastodon is administered by enthusiasts of server technology and self-hosting solution, who spends all their free time to eat linux documentation.
This Mastodon will be maintained over the long term.
Feel free to join us and share the  Mastoburn  instance to all your friends
For any questions about our instance contact@mastoburn.com

<details><summary>(more)</summary>[FR]
Règles de MastoBurn:

Pas de SPAM/FLOOD.
Pas de propos, ni de contenus média Racist, sexist, homophobic, pédopornographique etc ...
Le contenu non adapté à un public jeune (-18 ans) sont autorisé mais doivent êtres balisées de manière responsable en “Content Warning” (CW) / NFSW
Pas Pub sauf si accord des Admins.
L'Anglais, L'Américain et toutes les langues de l'Union Européenne sont autorisé sur cette instance.

## [masto.io](https://masto.io/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=masto.io&view=local)
Small alternative Mastodon instance with a short name. Registrations are open, but they may suspended/closed at any time if performance is compromised.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>
Contacts
Fell free to contact me (through @sena@masto.io or sena@smux.net) for any instance related issue.
Rules
Here are the house rules:
  
No harassing other people;
No posting NSFW content or spoilers without using the Content Warning feature;
No posting illegal content which can get you or me in trouble (this content will be removed if necessary, you may or may not be banned);
Parody accounts are permitted (and encouraged!), but it's suggested (not required) that such is stated in the bio.


Just be a good human being™.
Location and jurisdiction
Currently, the infrastructure which supports this instance is hosted in the United States (Kansas City, Missouri), although there are medium term plans to migrate it to some European location.
I am not based on the United States, so I may be more or less free from harassment from US law enforcement. Keep in mind that they should be able to shut the instance down and eavesdrop on communications and data without even warning me.

Policies:

Any content/site/service/action illegal in Austria, England, Ukraine or United States
DMCA takedown requests are checked and content is removed if we think it violates the policies
Spamming and mass user following is strictly forbidden and will result in removal of your account
Pornographic content is allowed - Pornographic content picturing minors (under 18) is obviously not allowed, this includes soft pornography and nudity as well

SLA, uptime, service info and support:

We run the systems based on a best-effort policy. We do not offer SLA or uptime guarantee.
Although we try our best, we can not guarantee that this service can be provided forever.
Support (if any at all) is also based on a best-effort policy - Please contact @fusl@s.meo.ws if you have any questions or support inquiries.

This basically means that no SLA is included so if you would like to sign up, do it at your own risk.

Mastodon.top is an mastodon instance hosted in France by VirtuBox. Our instance is updated with each new release of mastodon. Visit our about page to learn more about the rules of the instance and our moderation policy.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Welcome on mastodon.top !
We are very happy to be a part of the mastodon project and we will do our best to keep this instance running up. The instance is updated with each new release of mastodon, and we perform a daily backup on a offsite storage. We support freedom of speech, and we will not block instances or users unless there is a good reason. We may silence users or instances to hide them in the public timeline, this way only followers will see their toots.
