UNSTABLE BUT FRIENDLY

BE WARNED this instance may actually be unstable at times. It will likely be used for experimenting with settings and tweaks to Mastodon. So the place may experience outages, not federate reliably with the rest of the world, have posts go missing, or other technical faults. As such it's meant to be a chill, maybe kinda playful place. Time to see what we can do with this thing! Time to ˥∀IƆOS HƆ⊥I˥⅁


This instance also has domain level blocks on numerous others, using the block list found here . 

followbots from other instances will be blocked. please report them

Some rules


Do not engage in harassment of any kind.
Racist, sexist and other oppressive slurs will get you suspended, even in non-public conversations.
You can post porn and nudity, but you must use the nsfw flag and do not post on the public timeline or you will be silenced (ask around how to make unlisted posts)
try to be kind
no non-sentient bots until further notice
no shit that's illegal in Canada
animated gifs should always be marked sensitive/NSFW and identified as animated gifs (for now let's say just putting 'gif' in the text of the toot is sufficient), because they can cause serious problems for people

some guidelines

stuff here is impermanent but i still want this to be as safe a space as we can reasonably make it. let's keep common triggers and angry/ranty/grumpy toots behind CWs
free speech maximalists can kindly fuck off. there are instances where that is a priority. this is not one of them.
all languages are welcome!

the privacy stuff in the 'terms' isn't what it should be, but no time to change it yet. this instance's data will not be sold or traded or whatever.

## [mastodon.opportunis.me](https://mastodon.opportunis.me/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.opportunis.me&view=local)
Une instance ouverte à tou.te.s, qui se veut un minimum inclusive :

serveur réservé aux personnes parlant français ou anglais, par souci de facilité de modération.
Sexisme, racisme, homophobie et toutes formes d'exclusion des minorités sont à proscrire pour le bien être de tou.te.s.
Respectez la vie privée des personnes.
Utilisez les tags et autres CW que vous jugez adaptés, en particulier pour le contenu NotSafeForWork (NSFW).
Essayez d'être prévénant.e.s et inclusif.ve.s.
Si l'un de vos propos est perçu comme excluant et que quelqu'un vous en informe, écoutez. Nous sortirons tou.te.s grandi.e.s d'un tel dialogue.

Sachez que nous préférerons toujours notre liberté d'être ensemble à votre liberté d'exclure.
J'ai décidé de ne pas modérer l'extérieur de l'instance (bloquer des instances et/ou utilisatrices/eurs d'autres instances), sauf exceptions qui seront signalées ici et annoncées publiquements si des cas graves se présentent. J'estime qu'il est à chacun.e de choisir ce qu'iel veut lire de l'extérieur.
Merci au POOP, dont je ne cesse de m'inspirer de leur code de conduite.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Cette instance est hébergée en France. Chez moi, un administrateur système lambda, mais plutôt engagé.

L'accès à Internet se fait via un VPN associatif d'Illyse sur une fibre optique chez une grand fournisseur d'accès à internet commercial français.

De ce fait, le service dépent directement d'un accès à Internet grand public, et de matériel grand public, je fais mon possible pour que tout fonctionne au mieux mais je ne peux pas vous garantir un service constant, ni de GTR, ni SLA.

For non-french people.
This instance is open to everyone, willing to have a modicum inclusivity:

Server only for french and english speaking, to facilitate the moderation.
Sexism, racism, homophobia and any other minority exclusion should be avoided.
Respect for privacy.
Use tags and CW when you consider them relevant, in particular for NotSafeForWork (NSFW) contents.
Try to be considerate and inclusive.
If you are saying things that could be perceived as excluding and someone informs you, listen. We will all come out enriched from the dialogue.


Be aware that we will always prefer our freedom to be united than your freedom to exclude.
I decided to not moderate outside the instance (blacklist other instances and/or users for other instances), with a few exceptions which will be publicly announced for serious cases. I consider that everyone should make his own choices regarding what he wants to read from outside.
Thanks to the POOP for their inspiring  code of conduct.

This instance is hosted in France by myself, an average system administrator but rather committed.

Internet access is directly done through a voluntary VPN of Illyse over a fiber provided by a major french ISP.

Hence, the service depends on general public Internet access and hardware. I do my best, but I can't guarantee continuous service, nor SLA, nor MTTR.

Silence (and reject media file) instance : 

pawoo.net : lolicon
awoo.space : lolicon

## [mimumedon.com](https://mimumedon.com/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mimumedon.com&view=local)
Mimumedonはグラブルの話題を中心としたマストドンインスタンスです。
グラブルが好きでマストドンで遊んでみたいという人が集まる場所となれば幸いです。
ミムメモ速報の中の人がつくりました。
現在、テスト運用中です。
お試し作成段階なので、サーバーアクセス、またはその他の状況によっては突然閉じたり閉じなかったりすると思います。
画像等のファイル消去のお知らせ
容量問題に対応するため、ストレージの移設を行います。その際、インスタンス内の全ての画像ファイルなどについては、一度全て消去を行います。
【作業予定日】
5月11日（木）15時～
利用者の方にはご不便をおかけいたしますが、ご理解の程をよろしくお願いします。
プロフィール画像、残しておきたい画像についてはバックアップをお願いします。
運営方針について

「グラブルを遊んでる人が楽しく過ごせる場所」を目指してやっていきたいと考えています。

ルール・注意事項
公序良俗に反する投稿はおやめください
BOTの類はおやめください
他者への誹謗中傷、罵倒、暴言、差別的発言はおやめください
グラブル以外のゲームをはじめ、グラブル外の内容も話してもらって大丈夫です。
テスト運用中につき、いきなり閉じたりデータ消したりするかもしれません。

## [myriad.social](https://myriad.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=myriad.social&view=local)
"a social network where i'm not blocked...yet" - @Dre2Dee2
myriad.social is a discrete node in the mastodon network and the gnu social-compliant fediverse.
myriad.social is hosted in bucharest, romania and operates as a 'free-speech friendly' instance with emphasis on low moderation, high security, and full transparency, and operates under the auspices of the myriad truths project.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>myriad.social has a 'low-moderation' policy to facilitate free speech on this instance. This is not a legally binding document and may be updated and changed at our discretion, but currently our policy is to only remove content if it:
 - depicts minors in a sexually explicit manner
 - is illegal in romania (the locale where our infastructure resides)
 - disrupts the stability of the instance for other users
please report any content which violates one of these directives. general security-related correspondence, such as vulnerability disclosures, are gladly received at security@myriad.social.
myriad.social is a venture of The Myriad Truths Project, which accepts financial contributions from individual supporters and backers.

## [mel.social](https://mel.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mel.social&view=local)
mel.social is a small mastodon instance aimed primarily at Melbourne and Victoria based people who want a safe digital space to communicate and be creative. members are encouraged to communication and share their work as long as it adheres to our Code of Conduct
Please make sure you've familiarised yourself with our Code of Conduct before signing up and if our rules aren't to your liking then there are many other instances that may be better suited to your needs.
Follow @status for status & maintenance updates. Instance admin is @ajfisher

<details><summary>(more)</summary>mel.social Code of Conduct
As a user of mel.social, you agree to uphold an environment of respect and empathy for all users.
Any conduct that is deemed oppressive is grounds for removal from mel.social. Any language or action that expresses, reinforces, upholds or sympathises with any form of systemic social domination is considered oppressive and is grounds for removal at any level deemed appropriate by the Admin.
Pornography, violence, and fast-blinking images/content should not be used as a profile photo and should always be posted with a "NSFW" tag/content warning.
The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in a ban from mel.social:

Unapproved bots (for approval, please contact @ajfisher)
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and graphic violence
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism

The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in a ban from mel.social:

Sexual depictions of children
Holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism
Promoting the oppression of any group based on gender, gender identity and expression, sexual orientation, disability, personal appearance, body size, race, ethnicity, age, religion, or nationality.

Any conduct intended to stalk, harass, or intimidate other users, or to impede other users from utilising the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions is forbidden and subject to punishment up to and including a ban from mel.social.
This can include, but is not limited to, the following behaviours:

Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment.
Posting and/or disseminating a person's posts ("toots"), including screen captures or any other content without express permission.
Intentionally posting or disseminating libel, slander, or other disinformation.
This Code of Conduct applies both to content on mel.social and to public spaces when an individual is representing mel.social or its community.
Reports of abusive, harassing, or otherwise unacceptable behaviour may be made by using the report button. All reports will be reviewed and dealt with as soon as possible. Admins are obligated to maintain confidentiality with regard to the reporter of an incident.
The Admin reserves the right to revoke any user's content on or access to mel.social, at any time, for any reason.
</details>

Email: Not Available

Admin: [@ajfisher@mel.social](https://mel.social/@ajfisher)

## [social.tchncs.de](https://social.tchncs.de/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=social.tchncs.de&view=local)
This might be one of the best pieces of software for microblogging you can get right now. We here at tchncs.de are proud to be one of the first instances of Mastodon! Quick updates ensured. Mastodon is compatible and connected to the GNUsocial network.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>





Above statistics are specific to this server.
Guidelines
On social.tchncs.de our primary directive is: → "Be nice to each other!"
Please remember there are real people on the other side of the screen, and those people may have different feelings and opinions and experiences than you do. Some of them may be tired or having a bad day. Or you might.
 You don't have to agree with someone to be civil to them. If you can't be civil to someone, leave them alone.
 If you don't wish to interact with someone, or see any of their posts, there are tools at your disposal including mute and block functions.
 If someone's posts make you angry or upset, take some time to calm down before you reply. You might also try simply excusing yourself from a conversation and ask them to untag you if you no longer wish to discuss a topic.
 When someone asks you to leave them alone, leave them alone. If you feel like you can't control your urge to respond to that person, use the block or mute feature so you won't see their posts and be tempted.
 Keep in mind that while you cannot control other people's behavior, you are still responsible for your own conduct, even if you feel someone was rude to you or someone else.
 We will not allow abusive or disruptive conduct by or toward users on social.tchncs.de. This includes continuing to engage in conversation with someone who has specifically requested you leave them alone, inciting other users to engage with that person on your behalf, aggregating and posting another person's personal information without their consent, and inciting others to engage with that person on other platforms. Blocking someone and then sitting on the other side of a block and continuing to talk about that person is also a provoking behavior.
 Before you post, think about whether this is the kind of thing you would like to see (or would like your mom or kids to see) in the public timeline. There are post visibility settings that give you some control over which timelines your post appears in, and also CW and NSFW buttons to hide specific text and images in your post. Be a good social media neighbor and use these functions when appropriate.

Content not allowed on social.tchncs.de


Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism

Content which will be removed from the public timeline:


Excessive advertising
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence

We will also remove from the public timeline any content we judge to be hateful toward specific individuals or groups, or intended to cause or incite harm. This guideline is intentionally vague because we do not intend to play "rules lawyer" on the subject of what it is and isn't okay to say about people. A good rule of thumb is, if you're about to say something you think might fall foul of this rule, you probably shouldn't say it. ☺

</details>

Email: [tchncs@vivaldi.net](mailto:tchncs@vivaldi.net)

Admin: [@milan@social.tchncs.de](https://social.tchncs.de/@milan)

## [mastodon.host](https://mastodon.host/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.host&view=local)
General, fast, stable and open instance.

Federate with everyone.

One of the most complete Federated timeline thanks to @federationbot
lightly moderated in general, common sense applied. That said, read the rules below :)

 What sets mastodon.host appart ?
As a general instance, we are not centered on a specific theme, or a specific language. Everyone is welcome as long as they follow the few rules we have.
We have a very good view of the federation ( our federated timeline gives you a more broad view of the Mastodon network than a 'normal' instance, there's a lot to read in a lot of languages ).
Although we are a medium+ sized instance, we'd like to keep the feeling that you are at home and safe here.
Never hesitate to contact the admin team if you have any questions !
Please read the FAQ below or at https://mastodon.host/about/more to get started.
What are the instance rules ?
No illegal stuff, harassment, discrimination, xenophobia, threats or any behavior that is not appropriate to a friend will be tolerated to our users. This is a safe place for everyone, respect your fellow users or silence/block if you don't want to see someone. We moderate on our users report
Erotic/Porn/Gore/Etc..  talks/pictures/videos.. must be  behind a CW. If you would not open that picture/video in front of your boss/wife/husband/kids => CW ( Content Warning ).
Anything that is illegal in Europe/USA shall not be posted on this server, Lolicons for example are illegal.
Globally common sense applied,
 don't do illegal stuff, don't discriminate, don't be a racist, etc...
Notify to an administrator or report if you have a doubt. Do not engage, if you don't want to see someone's contributions, you can block/silence that person and report to us, we'll deal with it.We try to post in english so everyone understands, but that rule is not enforced at all ;)
Most important have fun and be nice to each other !

Oh and nazis, racists  are banned on sight too, of course.

What is this instance privacy policy ?
We will never share your data with anyone, except if a valid legal request is received (Hopefully it will not happen).
Who are the admins ? Shoutouts section.
This instance is hosted by @gled

<details><summary>(more)</summary>How does it works ?
When you create an account on Mastodon, you create an account on the website you currently are visiting. For example, here you are on mastodon.host. That is your instance.

You will notice after log in two different timelines, the Local and the Federated.
The local timeline is all the public toots of all our local users ( the one who registered on mastodon.host and use it to access the Mastodon federation ).
The federated timeline adds the public toots of all the users that our local users are following in other servers.
That is here that mastodon.host is a bit different, with a bot that actively follow everyone it sees on the federated timeline, we'll have eventually a good view of the overall network on the federated timeline.


@federationbot code is available on Github

What app can I use on my phone ?
There's multiples apps that support Mastodon:
- Twidere now support both Twitter and Mastodon, allowing you to seamlessly using the two networks, available for both Android and iOS.
- Amaroq is a popular app for Iphones.
- Tooty Fruity, Tusky, 11t or Subway tooter are also an option for Android phones.
How do I get verified ? Who is who ?
Do it yourself ;) For now there is no verification on Mastodon, it's just an emoji that people add as a joke.Your identity on Mastodon and the fediverse ( the federation of all the Mastodon instances ) is yourusername@yourinstance, so when you register here, your identity is yourusername@mastodon.host . You can follow and communicate with anyone in the fediverse if you know his username@instance !
How do I follow a user from another instance ?
If you know his username and his instance, you can search for @username@instance and from there it should be pretty easy. It's pretty young so there's room for improvments, and I'm sure that we'll end up being able to search across instances. There is now also some sites that allows searching users. You can always look at the federated timeline and find some interesting contacts !
How do I mask X language from the timelines ? I can't read that
That's a feature being developped at the moment, but you can always head to Mastodon lang remover
to do it in your browser without waiting for the feature to be integrated.
Who is moderating the instance ?
For the moment, you by reporting the posts and users and the admin enforcing the rules. We are currently recruiting a moderator team ( look for the announces by @gled ).
How often do you update the service ?
Usually the day a new stable version is released. You can follow @gled for announces when this is happening.
How much does it cost ?
Mastodon is free for the users.
This instance is hosted by me,@gled, on my personal funds.
Your help is appreciated to maintain/make the platform evolve.
How can I help ?
You can get involved in multiple ways, you can welcome new users, animate the local timeline, promote our instance and invite new users here, report posts and users not respecting our rules...

You can also help with the costs of running the service by donating, any small amount is appreciated ! Donations are accepted on: 
Liberapay:   
Paypal: 






What if the administrator cannot keep the service running ?
If in the future, we are unable to continue maintaining the service, it'll be handed to another administrator team that the community trusts !
</details>

Email: [gled@remote-shell.net](mailto:gled@remote-shell.net)

Admin: [@gled@mastodon.host](https://mastodon.host/@gled)

## [mastodon.swordlogic.com](https://mastodon.swordlogic.com/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.swordlogic.com&view=local)


DMMオンラインゲーム「しんけん!!」ファンの皆様のためのインスタンスです。
公式ページはこちら

 @mastodon.swordlogic.com からのメールを受信できるように設定をご確認ください。


<details><summary>(more)</summary>ご利用にあたって
このインスタンスは「しんけん!!」ファンの楽しい交流の場としてお使いください。
ネタバレなど他のユーザーへの配慮が必要な投稿を行う際は、テキストなら「CW」（Contents Warning：内容についての警告〜表題は指定可能）、画像ならアップロード後に「NSFW」（Not Safe For Work：職場や公共の場所での閲覧には不向き）ボタンをお使いください。

禁止行為について

全般的には皆様の良識にお任せしますが、以下の事項については禁止いたします。

日本の法律で禁止されている行為
公序良俗に反する行為
実在する個人や団体になりすます行為
特定の個人や団体の名誉を棄損したり脅迫や損害を与える行為
他者の著作権を侵害する行為
サーバーに過度の負荷をかける行為やスパム行為



「しんけん!!」とは

プロローグ

ある日突如として飛来した隕石群『大天狗』によって甚大なる被害を受けた日本。
飛散した隕石のかけらから生まれた謎の生命体『憑喪』が残った都市を蹂躙、エネルギーと名のつく全てのものを食い荒らし、遂には人々の命にも手をかけ始めた。
憑喪に対して我々はまったくの無力だったが、とある神社に奉納されていた神刀が憑喪に有効だったという報告が反撃の糸口となる。
発掘された古文書から、特殊な鍛えられ方をした刀剣には憑喪に対抗しうる力が宿るのだとわかり、研究の結果、秘伝の鍛刀法の再現に至った。
人類の存亡を賭けよみがえる数々の名刀と、名刀に魅入られし真剣少女達の物語がいま始まる!!

## [babuu.club](https://babuu.club/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=babuu.club&view=local)





【Babuuについて】

Babuuは育児に関わる方々を対象としたMastodonのインスタンスです。
現在テスト運用中です。

父母はもちろん、祖父祖母おじおば、教育、医療、福祉関係者etc…育児に関わる方ならだれでもOK!


育児の合間の一息に、ママさんパパさん達のコミュニケーションに、ぜひご利用ください。


<details><summary>(more)</summary>
※重要なお知らせ
現在、ホーム・連合・ローカルの各タイムラインの自動更新ができなくなっています。ご迷惑をおかけしますがよろしくお願いします。

■最低限の利用ルール


たとえそれがかわいい赤ちゃんでも、局部の写り込んだ写真の投稿はNGです。
R18の投稿はお控えください。判断が難しい場合は積極的にCWやNSFWを投稿時にに活用しましょう。
その他公序良俗に反する投稿は禁止します。


■お知らせについて

Babuu内部向けアナウンスは以下のアカウントから行います。
Babuu(@Babuuclub)

■管理者とお問い合わせ先

管理者は@itacchiku(2児の母)です。
問い合わせは、
Babuu(@itacchiku)
Twitter(@itacchiku)
までご連絡ください。

■ちょっとしたQ&A;


・登録メールが届かない
登録時の返送メールがとどかない場合、迷惑メールフォルダに振り分けられていることがよくあるようです。ご確認ください。
・ログインしてみたら画面が真っ黒
マストドンは現在IE非対応となっています。IE以外のブラウザでログインするか、スマホアプリをご利用ください。
・外部インスタンスとの接続について
一部のR18系をメインとしたインスタンスとの接続を除き、自由に開放しています。R18または差別的なトゥートの多いインスタンス及びアカウントがあれば、管理人までお知らせください。



</details>

Admin: [@Babuuclub@babuu.club](https://babuu.club/@Babuuclub)

## [tootmusic.com](https://tootmusic.com/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=tootmusic.com&view=local)
🎧 This is a Mastodon server for Music.  Constructive mentoring & discussions are all welcome - don't post illegal stuff and try to play nice. 🎧

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Welcome
Here some resources to understand Mastodon :
Welcome to Mastodon by @Gargron
Bye, Twitter. All the cool kids are migrating to Mastodon by Mashable
How does it work?
When you create an account on Mastodon, you create an account on the website you currently are visiting. For example, here you are on tootmusic.com That is your instance. You will notice after log in two different timelines, the Local and the Federated.The local timeline is all the public toots of all our local users ( the one who registered on mastodon.org.uk and use it to access the Mastodon federation ).The federated timeline adds the public toots of all the users that our local users are following in other servers.
Mobile applications

Android : Tusky
iOS : Amaroq for Mastodon
Full list

Support Mastodon

The code source can be found here : Github 

Terms 
The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of tootmusic.com; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:

The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:

Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence


The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:

Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism


The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:

Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism


Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:

Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Email: [info@tootmusic.com](mailto:info@tootmusic.com)

Admin: [@lee@tootmusic.com](https://tootmusic.com/@lee)

Rules
The following guidelines, mostly adopted from mastodon.social, are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of social.etc-services.de.
They are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Excessive advertising
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.


These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.

## [off-the-clock.us](https://off-the-clock.us/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=off-the-clock.us&view=local)
Just your run of the mill Mastodon server. We use mail-gun for email notifications, check your spam folder and mark us as "not spam" please.
Status: http://status.off-the-clock.us/

<details><summary>(more)</summary>This server is operated by Nick Gerakines, please contact him @ngerakines@off-the-clock.us for questions or issues.
Rules and Guidelines

Don't be a jerk -- this goes both ways. Everyone has bad days, so if you are having a bad day then try not to take it out on anyone. If you see someone else having a bad day, try to uplift them.
This server is meant for personal, non-commercial use. Promoting your services, projects, and products is OK, but don't be excessive. Corporate accounts, organizations, and businesses don't jell with being "off the clock", and probably don't belong here.
Some content doesn't belong here. I'm generally pretty OK with NSFW content, but please know your audience and use content warnings. Any content that is considered illegal, graphic, or promotes/is hate speech will not be tolerated.
 This really boils down to rule #1, don't be a jerk.
This server should not be used to transmit sensitive information or secrets. Please do not jeopardize the network, the other accounts on this server, or the operator by having information on here that other people would be interested in.

If you object to or have a problem with these rules, then you probably don't belong here. They are pretty tame and flexible.
Blocked Servers
The full list of blocked servers can be found here: https://github.com/off-the-clock/blocked-servers
</details>

Email: [nick@gerakines.net](mailto:nick@gerakines.net)

Admin: [@ngerakines@off-the-clock.us](https://off-the-clock.us/@ngerakines)

## [social.wxcafe.net](https://social.wxcafe.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=social.wxcafe.net&view=local)

This is an open mastodon instance for social justice activists, LGBTQIA+ people, and people who are aware of such subjects and care about them.


See the Goals, rules, and technical details for more information


<details><summary>(more)</summary> Goals and Rules 

The instance has multiple goals, the most important of all being making everyone on here feel as safe as possible. Other goals include letting users manage their social life easily and securely, making this instance a nice community with a shared expression space, and making the fediverse better. 

As such, we have a few rules we'd like everyone on the instance to follow :


Acting in any of the following ways will get you immediately suspended

Posting illegal content is, well, illegal. This server is in France. As such, heinous content, nazi propaganda, underage porn, and all other content that is illegal according to french law is forbidden.
Posting LGBTQIA+-phobic, whorephobic, sexist, racist, antisemitic, and islamophobic content. You can still discuss such topics, by including a CW, quotes, and a context.
Making public, by screencapping or copying, private or direct messages that the author didn't want made public
Taking part in targetted harassment
Posting spam, advertisment for a commercial product, etc
Being a techbro or Richard Matthew Stallman

Acting in any of the following ways will get your post deleted and you'll get a warning. After three warnings, you'll be suspended.

Posting pornographic images/videos or nude pictures without marking them NSFW, or posting them on the public timeline
Being clearly disrespectful towards another user
Being an asshole



Right now, the only admin and moderator is @wxcafe. This might change in the future, and will be reflected on this page. Please report any content breaking the rules highlighted on this page using the report function. We don't hesitate to moderate posts, to silence and/or suspend users, local or remote, and instances. In France we like to think of this as "Censure Communautariste".

Technical Informations

This server is run on a server paid for by @wxcafe, hosted on Vultr. The server is a 4GB RAM, 2 vCores, 60G disk VPS. It costs $20/months, and is financed using Patreon  The bot @server_status posts information about the status of the server every once in a while, be it graphs about the ressources, number of users and toots, etc...

 More 

Feel free to contact me for more informations at the email address in the right sidebar, or directly on Mastodon :)

</details>

Email: [wxcafe@wxcafe.net](mailto:wxcafe@wxcafe.net)

Admin: [@wxcafe@social.wxcafe.net](https://social.wxcafe.net/@wxcafe)

## [oc.todon.fr](https://oc.todon.fr/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=oc.todon.fr&view=local)
oc.todon.fr est une instance Mastodon francophone et avec une modération active. oc.todon.fr is an actively-moderated French-speaking Mastodon instance. oc.todon.frは、積極的にモデレートされたフランス語圏のMastodonインスタンスです。

<details><summary>(more)</summary>oc.todon.fr est une instance Mastodon francophone et avec une modération active.
Règles : Aucun type de harcèlement ou de (micro-)agression n'est toléré, qu'elles soient personnelles ou relèvent d'un système oppressif (misogynie, racisme, LGBTphobies/queerphobie, validisme, etc.). De même pour la promotion de ces oppressions et des mouvements politiques associés (masculinisme, suprémacisme, etc.). La pornographie et la nudité sont tolérées pour le moment, mais doivent être obligatoirement indiquées comme NSFW. De même pour contenus sensibles/choquants, qui doivent avoir un Content Warning approprié. Sauf exception accordée par l'admin, les publicités sont bannies de cette instance. Enfin, vous devez respecter les lois françaises, y compris celles concernant les droits d'auteurs.
À propos de cette instance :
Cette instance est maintenue sur mon temps libre, et je ne souhaite pas me faire rémunérer pour cela. Cependant, je dois louer le matériel, et vous pouvez me donner un coup de main sur Liberapay si vous le souhaitez.
Pour suivre les mises à jour de l'instance, abonnez-vous au compte @admin. Vous pouvez aussi me contacter via ce compte, ou par email à l'adresse progval+octodon arobase progval point net.
Mentions légales
Ce site web est hébergé à titre non lucratif par Val Lorentz sur un serveur loué en France chez Online.net. Les contenus présents sur ce site sont uniquement la responsabilité de leur auteurice.

## [toot.cafe](https://toot.cafe/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=toot.cafe&view=local)
Toot Café is an online club for tooting in a fun, safe, mammoth-themed environment.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Toot Café is an instance that was seeded from the web development and design community, so topics may tend to be about JavaScript, CSS, etc. They're not limited to that, though; you can talk about anything you want as long as you follow the Code of Conduct.
Code of Conduct
Prior art


Mastodon.social guidelines
JSConf Code of Conduct


The short version

Don't harass anyone
If someone is harassing you, report it to a moderator
Have fun
Be excellent to each other

Moderators

@nolan
@ohhoe
@halkeye
@luisbg

Blocked instances
We block some other instances. The full list is on GitHub and you are free to dispute it, but note that our preference is to err on the side of caution.
Rules

No advertising or excessive promotion
No bots, unless they're cute, funny, or useful. Bots should avoid posting to the public timeline.
No pornography, nudity, or something that would be considered "NSFW" in a U.S. workplace, even behind a NSFW warning.
No gore or graphic violence
Content that is borderline NSFW or could be construed as NSFW at a glance should be put behind a CW (Content Warning)
No racism
No sexism
No discrimination based on gender, sexual minority, sexual orientation, disability, physical appearance, body size, race, ethnicity, religion (or lack thereof), or national origin
No xenophobia or violent nationalism
No sexual depictions of children
No holocaust denialism, Nazi symbolism, promotion of National Socialism, or anything that is illegal in the European Union
No stalking or harassment
No fake accounts, even celebrity joke accounts. Note this rule does not necessarily apply to remote accounts.
No "follow bots." We block these and our instance is on a "no bots" list.

Handling harassment
If you are being harassed, please report the user using the "…" button and then "Report." For urgent concerns, please DM a moderator.
If you engage in harassing behavior, the moderator may take any action they deem appropriate, such as a warning or an expulsion.
The above rules may change at any time, and you may be banned at any time based on the moderators' judgment.
Privacy policy
What will we do with your data? Nothing. How will you be influenced by advertisers? You won't; brands and non-humans (other than fun/useful bots) are banned. How will we aggregate your data in order to improve your service… none of that.
We will never share your data with anyone else, except in the case of valid legal requests if it comes to that. (Hopefully it won't come to that!)
More privacy measures on toot.cafe:

EXIF data (GPS location, date, camera type, etc.) is stripped from images and never stored.
All crawlers are blocked in robots.txt.
HTTPS is used everywhere thanks to Let's Encrypt.
No ads or trackers.
Links are direct URLs rather than tracking redirects.

Understand though that this instance is run by me and my friends, and (as is the case with all Mastodon servers) we potentially have access to your data, including DMs. The back-end is also not encrypted. If this is not okay with you, this might not be the instance for you.
Also, for truly private data sent between two people, Mastodon offers no E2E encryption. So use Signal or WhatsApp for the things you really want to be private.
Discussion and Feedback
For questions about policy, bots, design, theming, etc., please refer to our discussions GitHub repo.
About this server
Purple theme and custom icons by Maxime Le Conte des Floris.

This server is an Azure instance running Ubuntu 16.04.2 LTS in US West 2 (near Seattle). It's maintained by Nolan Lawson, who has a Patreon if you would like to pitch in.
</details>

Email: [nolan@nolanlawson.com](mailto:nolan@nolanlawson.com)

Admin: Not Available

## [todon.nl](https://todon.nl/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=todon.nl&view=local)
Todon.nl is a Mastodon instance for progressive people. Although we are located in the Netherlands, we like to welcome every progressive person from all over the world.
So if you are (among others) a leftist, socialist, anarchist, Marxist, ecologist, green, vegan, open-minded, anti-racist, pirate, social democrat or social liberal, please join us!
Todon.nl is een Mastodon-server voor progressieve mensen. Ondanks dat wij ons in Nederland bevinden, willen wij elk progressief persoon van over de hele wereld welkom heten.
Dus ben je (o.a.) links, socialist, anarchist, ecologisch, groen, vegan, ruimdenkend, antiracist, piraat, sociaaldemocraat of sociaalliberaal, meld je dan aan!

<details><summary>(more)</summary>(Nederlands onderaan)
These Terms of Service are only valid for Todon.nl. See also Mastodon's (more general) Terms of Service. However, the terms on this page are leading. If you can't agree with the conditions below, you can still use Mastodon, but you should use another instance with different conditions. Or you can deploy your own instance, where you can set your own terms.

We have to adhere to Dutch and European law. Leading for us however is the Universal Declaration of Human Rights.
You are personally fully responsible and accountable for what you publish on Todon.nl. Without any exception, whether you use a pseudonym/alias or not. In other words: we from Todon.nl and the Mastodon Project in general are completely not responsible and accountable for what you publish, in any form whatsoever.
We do not tolerate, among other things, racism, homophobia, transphobia and other forms of discrimination, no (sexual) abuse of minors and adults, no calls to and glorification of violence, no right wing and religious extremism, no harassment, and of course no spam. We always keep the right to silence or suspend your account. We are fortunately very tolerant, and freedom of speech and expression are highly valued by us, and therefore we will always think twice before we take these actions. Please use the report tool if you think someone on this instance did not comply with our guidelines.

Copyright

Everything you toot is yours and stays yours. You are free to release your toots under any kind of license. We advise you to use a Creative Commons license. You can put this in short in your bio. When you don't indicate a license, the Dutch copyright Law applies. Work from others is of course not your work and using that is completely your risk. So keep yourself well informed about the copyright of third party content. Usually more flexible conditions apply for embedded content.

Warranty

Todon.nl and the Mastodon project cannot, in any way be held liable for damages and harm. Todon.nl and the Mastodon Project work hard to prevent fatal server and software failures, but we can never ever guarantee this.



The text above can be modified by us. Check therefore regularly if you still agree with these terms.


Deze gebruikersvoorwaarden gelden alleen voor Todon.nl. Zie ook Mastodons (meer algemene) gebruikersvoorwaarden (Engels). De voorwaarden op deze pagina zijn echter leidend. Als je niet akkoord kan of wil gaan met onderstaande voorwaarden, dan kan je nog steeds gebruik maken van Mastodon, maar dan wel op een andere Mastodon-server met andere voorwaarden. Of je kan je eigen Mastodon-server installeren, waar jezelf de voorwaarden mag bepalen.

Wij moeten ons aan de Nederlandse en Europese wet houden. Leidend voor ons is echter de Universele verklaring van de rechten van de mens.
Jij persoonlijk bent volledig verantwoordelijk en aansprakelijk voor wat jij op Todon.nl plaatst. Zonder enkele uitzondering en of je nu een pseudoniem/alias gebruikt of niet. In andere woorden: wij van Todon.nl en van het Mastodon-project in zijn geheel zijn niet verantwoordelijk en aansprakelijk voor wat jij hier publiceert in welke vorm dan ook.
Wij tolereren onder andere geen racisme, seksisme, homofobie, transfobie, en andere vormen van discriminatie, geen (seksueel) misbruik van minder- en meerderjarigen, oproep tot en verheerlijking van geweld, geen rechts- en religieus extremisme, niet het lastig vallen van mensen, en uiteraard geen spam. Wij houden ten allen tijde het recht om jouw account het zwijgen op te leggen of te blokkeren. We zijn gelukkig heel tolerant en hebben de vrijheid van meningsuiting hoog in het vaandel staan, en denken daarom altijd twee keer na voordat we daartoe overgaan. Gebruik de rapporteerfunctie wanneer jij denkt dat iemand op deze Mastodon-server zich niet aan onze richtlijnen houdt.

Auteursrecht

Alles wat jij toot is van jou en blijft van jou. Je bent vrij om jouw toots onder elke soort licentie vrij te geven. Wij adviseren om een Creative Commons-licentie te gebruiken. Dit kan je dan het beste in het kort in jouw bio kenbaar maken. Wanneer je geen licentie kenbaar maakt dan geldt de Nederlandse auteurswet, wat inhoudt dat alle rechten bij jou liggen. Werk van anderen valt uiteraard niet onder jouw auteursrecht en het gebruik daarvan is volledig jouw risico. Stel je dus goed op de hoogte van het auteursrecht op werk van derden. Voor ingesloten inhoud (embedded content) gelden meestal soepelere voorwaarden.

Garantie
Todon.nl en het Mastodon-project kunnen op geen enkele manier aansprakelijk worden gesteld voor geleden schade. Todon.nl en het Mastodon-project doen hard hun best om fatale server- en software-problemen te voorkomen, maar we kunnen dit nooit ofte nimmer garanderen.



Bovenstaande tekst kan door ons aangepast worden. Controleer daarom regelmatig of je je nog in bovenstaande voorwaarden kunt vinden.

</details>

Email: [admin@todon.nl](mailto:admin@todon.nl)

Admin: [@admin@todon.nl](https://todon.nl/@admin)

## [mstdn.lalafell.org](https://mstdn.lalafell.org/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.lalafell.org&view=local)
光の戦士向けマストドンインスタンス。

A moderated Mastodon instance for the OSR RPG community. NSFW content is allowed, but public posts must use the Content Warning feature or be deleted. More information on Mastodon OSR and our Code of Conduct can be found here.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>This is a moderated server focused on the discussion of RPGs in general and the OSR subculture in particular, though we talk about other RPGs, game design, board games, and all of the other varied topics you can find on Mastodon instances as well.
Any moderation of content on this server is intended to foster better discourse. Disagreement and discord are fine, but being an asshole who drives out other voices is not.
And, to be clear, we're going to lean towards being SJW Cucks in this.
Code of Conduct
Behaviors that will get you kicked out of here, no exceptions:

Racism, sexism, transphobia, ultranationalism, or the advocation thereof
Sexual depictions of children
Any conduct intended or perceived to be stalking, harrassing, denial of service, or the incitement thereof
Aggregation, posting, and/or dissemination of a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission, or the advocation thereof
The following types of posts will be deleted from the public timeline. Unrepentant repeat offenders will be removed from the community:
Any untagged sexually-explicit content
Any untagged depictions of extreme violence or gore
Excessive advertising
Links or advocation for items, services, or behaviors considered illegal in the United States of America

These provisions notwithstanding the administation of this service reserve the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>This is a Mastodon Instance for BBQ lovers to share tips, recipes, and ask for help.
---Code Of Conduct---
As members of this instance we all hold a share of responsibility in maintaining the quality of discussion and the safety of our fellow members and the members in which out instance interacts with.
 With this in mind there are a few guidelines to posting in this community, repeated violations will result in a ban: + Nude or pornographic content should ideally not be posted here, but if you must put it behind a content warning and give other members a heads up. + Violent content should also be put behind a content warning if it is posted here with a heads up to other members that it is there.  + Any content with rapidly changing content (or content that might cause seizures should be placed behind a content warning with a heads up to the other members that it is there. + This instance is dedicated to the topics of barbeque/food, other content may be posted here but should be kept to a mininum  The following actions will end up with an immediate ban from this instance:  + Hate speech of any sort against any person. + Harassment of any person (even if that person is not on this instance). + Overly sexual or violent content with no content warnings. Please note that the administrator of this instance has final say on bans. Also, this Code of Conduct may be changed/updated at anytime, notification of such changes will come through @josh, with a quick description of the change

金沢市のマストドンです。

８番らーめん万歳

<details><summary>(more)</summary>
登録時の自動送信メールが迷惑メールフォルダに届くことがあるようです。
メールが届かない場合、お手数ですが一旦そちらもご確認ください。



運営している人：とり（@torii）
金沢ではたらく一般人です。
地方インスタンスも盛り上がってほしいと思い、立ち上げました。
居心地の良い空間をつくっていきましょう！


情報の取扱いについて：


インスタンスに登録いただく過程で収集した情報は、警察や司法機関から正式な開示命令が為された場合以外では一切使用いたしません。
気休めになるか分かりませんが、IPAの情報セキュリティ資格を取得していますので、バックエンド設定などは気を遣っているつもりです。。。
なお万が一、マストドン自体の脆弱性が報告された際、利用者への損害を防ぐ為にサーバを一時的に停止させていただく場合がありますので予めご了承ください。


運営について：
金銭的なご支援は必要ありません。
あくまで趣味なので、すべて私の器量内で運営しています。
代わりと言ってはなんですが、周りの人たちを誘ってみていただけませんか？
この空間を多くの人と共有できれば、それで十分です。




ソースコード公開について：
マストドンはAGPLライセンス（ソースコード公開が義務）なので、他インスタンスと同様に金沢インスタンスでも準備ができ次第公開します。

## [meow.social](https://meow.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=meow.social&view=local)
This instance is focused around the furry community, and is open to anyone interested in it. It was created by @Tiwy57 originally for a small group of furry friends, but thought it might as well be open to all fluffies and scalies !

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Welcome to meow.social! A mastodon instance.

NetData Monitoring












Admin members : @Tiwy57 and @Nomaxice
Official Accounts : @TransparencyReports and @meow

This instance is focused around the furry community, and is open to anyone interested in it. It was created by @Tiwy57 originally for a small group of furry friends, but thought it might as well be open to all fluffies and scalies !
Meow is federated to nearly all instances of mastodon, which means you can follow pretty much anyone you want, no matter what instance they are on!
While it is open publicly, mind this is just one instance in the fediverse, and we encourage you to look at other instances available to be sure it’s the one you like, and if none please you and you got some knowledge, why not come help mastodon by making your own instance too!
Ruleset


Stay legal.

Respect international laws.
Respect laws from the country the instance is hold in (Netherlands).
Respect laws from the admins' country (France).
Respect laws from your own country.


Be respectful.

Don’t go insult others, whether you say it straight to their face or not.
Contents that are racist, sexist, hateful, or discriminating in any way are forbidden.
Stalking and harassment is forbidden, if someone don’t want to have anything to do with you, leave them alone.


Tag your content.

Tag as NSFW content properly, hidden behind a CW button, and keep porn as private or unlisted for AD posts.
Tag gore and NSFL content and keep it behind a CW button.
Tag politics and the like, again with a CW button.


Accounts policy.

Do not impersonate someone, unless for parody purposes (so long as you stay respectful).
Parody accounts must be tagged as such clearly in their profile description.
Bots must be tagged as such, and bot owners must ensure they will have a minimal impact on the instance's performances.
If your handle has been taken or stolen, and have the means to prove it yours, we will reattribute it to you.
Do NOT use a "verified" status (with checkmark) : prove that you are someone official by all your means possible
You may not create another account on this instance if your previous account has been suspended.




Failure to respect any of those rules will lead to a warning, content removal, and/or suspension of your account.
The admins have the upmost right to decide to delete your account for any reason.
You may discuss with the admins if you feel you were unfairly sanctioned, so long as you don’t try to force your way after the final statement has been given by them.
If you require any help or need to contact us, please contact @Tiwy57, @Nomaxice, or send a mail at meow@meow.social
About this server
This server is hosted on Scaleway, with four dedicated CPU cores, 8GB RAM, and 50GB of storage on SSD. It can be updated any time.
Uptime will be kept at the highest possible, hopefully only going down for updates.
</details>

Email: [meow@meow.social](mailto:meow@meow.social)

Admin: [@Tiwy57@meow.social](https://meow.social/@Tiwy57)

## [freehold.earth](https://freehold.earth/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=freehold.earth&view=local)
Freehold.Earth is a free-speech centered community, extremely lightly moderated (we'll do what we can about spam and harassment, and possibly some management of the federated public timeline, that's about it...do as you please when communicating with followers!).

More info at https://freehold.earth/about/more

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Welcome!
The unifying theme of Freehold.Earth is free speech. We welcome people from all walks of life, even those we don’t particularly like, to have a voice in the world.  While the initial round of invites mostly went to folks from the infosec and free speech advocacy communities, registration is open whenever our capacity limitations permit.
However, if you are the sort of person who wants those you deem to be “bad people” or holders of “dangerous opinions” ejected from the community…this is not the place for you. I guarantee that no matter your ideological bent, there will be someone here you deem bad/dangerous.
What does this mean in terms of user experience?
The admins don’t want to hear about your problems with anyone you haven’t both muted and blocked.  It’s your job to step away from speech that is troubling to you.  We will take action to:

Try to mitigate spam problems.
Try to intervene in harrassment, defined specifically as a user persistently contacting another user who has already muted and blocked them. If you didn’t mute and block, they aren’t harrassing you, though they may be annoying.  Annoying is not on the list of things we care about.
Try to mitigate actual security issues.
Encourage a tolerant and open community where users can control which content they produce and engage with.

Note the use of “try” and “encourage”…there are things we simply do not control, and we will not sacrifice free speech for everyone in an attempt to make our community a safe haven from all the world’s ills. Earth is a chaotic place, and Freehold.Earth will likely be so as well.
What should users know?

A “post” (“tweet” elsewhere) is called a “toot” here. To repeat/amplify a toot is to “boost” that toot.
We favorite things we like, by clicking the star on the toot.
The Local Timeline is all public posts at the moment on Freehold.Earth
The Federated Timeline is every public post from anywhere that is seen by Freehold.Earth – the more remote users followed by our users, the more of a firehose this becomes.

Are there any tips for being loved and followed by many?
Generally, we’re not here to tell you what to do…but in case you were wondering what social conventions are popular, consider the following.  Observing these tips will also help keep other servers from blocking our traffic!

Please use the #NSFW tag for NSFW posts…this allows other users to filter their view in public places.
Please wrap content likely to annoy some of your audience (politics, rants, etc) in a CW (Content Warning).
Please don’t use an animated GIF for your avatar.
Please place the #bot tag in the profile of any non-human account.
Please be a bit kinder than is really called for, and disengage rather than escalate when you see drama starting.
When someone’s being an asshat, please assume it’s out of misunderstanding rather than malice, until they prove you wrong.

Meet the Freehold.Earth admin team:

HedgeMage …This is my server, but I’m more often active on my personal account, HedgeMage@maly.io than on Freehold.
Consentacles …I’m generally friendly…AFTER coffee has been applied.
KatamariChaos …I like to boost a good toot.

Nodes (instances) currently blocked by Freehold.Earth
**NONE**
A note on bot accounts:
We are currently experimenting with silencing followbot accounts to reduce noise in the Federated Timeline at Freehold.Earth.

Follow bot traffic should not appear in the Federated Timeline, if it does, feel free to report it so we can silence.
Follow bots are NOT under a suspension ban. You can still follow them (and they you) if desired, the traffic just won’t be in the Federated Timeline. Some followbots will not follow users with #nobot in their profile.
It is possible for bots that are not follow bots to get caught up in this ban. If you think you have seen this happening, please contact the admins.

A follow bot is a bot that indiscriminately follows most/all users it comes across, in an attempt to increase federation between small servers and the rest of the Fediverse. Because their follow choices are random (and some spew statistics as often as every twenty minutes), we’re hoping that removing this traffic will make Freehold.Earth’s Federated Timeline more relevant and interesting to our users.
This is currently an experiment and may change at any time.
</details>

Email: [admins@freehold.earth](mailto:admins@freehold.earth)

Admin: Not Available

## [himastdon.club](https://himastdon.club/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=himastdon.club&view=local)

himastdon.club(ひますとどん)は
ひまわりストリーム ( http://himast.in/ ) の名を借りた、
非公認Mastodonサーバーです。
(※ひまスト管理人さんに知られちゃいましたが、非公認です！)

基本的には、ひまわりストリームにて
配信・視聴を行っている方向けのインスタンスです。
名前一緒にする必要もないですし、
匿名勢だけど……といった方もウェルカム
また、過疎インスタンスへの興味があるというのも構いません(*´∀｀*)
規約等は詳細説明をどうぞ。


メールアドレスは捨てアド、
パスワードは使いまわしてないものをお勧めします。
(セキュリティ面での保証ができかねる為)
ものによっては届かないのもあるらしいです。
以下のだと届くそうですよ。
https://10minutemail.net/

ただ、上記だときっとパスワード再設定出来なくなるので、要注意♡

<details><summary>(more)</summary>もしも以下の条件に当てはまった場合、このサーバーは停止されます。

・ひまわりストリーム管理者より通告があった場合
・himastdon.club管理者( @wanwan@himastdon.club )の都合
・2017/04/22より一年経過後に、アクティブなアカウントが少ない場合


その他は概ね、他のインスタンスの一般的なルールに則ります。
エログロに関わる発言には、Content Warning
エロ画像は、NSFWタグを付けること。
通報に関しましては@wanwanへDMか、
ビジネスメールアドレス欄宛に、連絡をお願いいたします


業者、BOTはお断り♡


完全に趣味、技術的興味で立てているインスタンスなので
最悪の場合データ消滅も有り得ます。
その際は、ゆるして♡
</details>

Email: [wanwan@himastdon.club](mailto:wanwan@himastdon.club)

Admin: [@wanwan@himastdon.club](https://himastdon.club/@wanwan)

## [mastodon.papey.fr](https://mastodon.papey.fr/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.papey.fr&view=local)
Pouet !

 Bienvenue à tous et à toutes sur l'instance Mastodon de @papey@mastodon.papey.fr. Elle est hébergé chez Scaleway SAS, sur un serveur VC1S. C'est une machine avec 2 cœurs/2 GO de ram, en conséquence, le nombre maximal d'utilisateurs sera contrôlé et limité.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Accueil

Cette instance est ouverte tant que la quantité de ressources disponibles sur le serveur est suffisante pour permettre à tous une utilisation convenable de l'outil.

Je (@papey) suis le seul à administrer cette instance, je fais de mon mieux pour améliorer l'infrastructure (mises à jours, entretien, nouvelles fonctionnalités) sans pour autant y consacrer tout mon temps libre (oui je fais plein d'autres choses à côté).

N'hésitez pas à me contacter par mail sur Mastodon si vous avez des questions concernant cette instance.

Attention, Mastodon ne me fait pas vivre, je met à disposition cette instance avant tout pour moi même (bien qu'elle soit ouverte).


Règles

Malheuresement, je dois encore le rappeler :

Les propos à caractères discriminant sont strictement interdits. N'hésitez pas à utiliser la fonction d'alerte pour dénoncer des individus.


Spécifications et détails techniques

L'instance tourne sur un serveur VC1S de chez Scaleway (Scaleway) à mes frais.


Docker
Les Docker ragix : cassez-vous.

Cette instance est propulsée par Docker. J'utilise l'image officielle de Mastodon. Celle-ci provient d'un build automatique mis en place entre le repo Github et Docker Hub).

Je déploie l'instance via Ansible qui effectue les tâches listées dans le docker-compose du projet. J'ajoute à ces tâches des modifications personnelles (gestion des logs, mapping réseau, tunning, volumes). Les données (pg, assets, redis) sont bind mounté entre l'hôte et le conteneurs (volumes).

Les images postgres et redis sont des images vanilla non exposée sur les internets.


Caddy
Caddy est utilisé en frontal comme reverse proxy HTTP. Il génère et gère comme un grand les certificats Lets Encrypt.


Mailgun

J'ai pas encore eu le temps de mettre un place un système de mail dédié, en conséquence l'envoi de mail pour cette instance utilise le service Mailgun. Les mails de confirmations arrivent dans les spams, merci de les vérifier :)


Sauvegardes

Pour l'instant, les seules sauvegardes disponibles sont les snapshots Scaleway (qui entraîne une indisponibilité du serveur). Je travaille actuellement sur un système de sauvegardes plus complet. VOUS ÊTES PREVENU-E-S.


TODO LIST

Backup
Metrics (Grafana, InfluxDB, Telegraf)
S3, via Minio

Bon mastodonage

Merci pour votre confiance et bon mastodonage :)
</details>

Email: [wollivier@fdn.fr](mailto:wollivier@fdn.fr)

Admin: [@papey@mastodon.papey.fr](https://mastodon.papey.fr/@papey)

<details><summary>(more)</summary>ルール

みんな仲良く。

禁止行為

以下に挙げる行為を行った場合、タイムラインでのミュート、もしくはアカウントの停止処分となることがあります。


日本国内の法律に違法するコンテンツを投稿すること
ツールなどを使用して過度にサーバへ負荷をかけること
特定の人物に対しての嫌がらせ、誹謗中傷
他のユーザの迷惑になるような過度なスパム行為

## [mastodon.me.uk](https://mastodon.me.uk/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.me.uk&view=local)
A Mastodon/OSocial server for users in the UK. Originally intended for the tech community, but open to anyone! As this is a volunteer-run server maintained by @floppy, users are required to abide by the Contributor Covenant Code of Conduct - if you don't like it, there are plenty of other instances you can use.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Bot Policy

Bots are tentatively allowed on this server as long as they are useful, interesting, or amusing. Bots that post excessively, that simply boost or link other posts, that just follow other users, or that produce badly-formed output will be suspended. Contact the admins if you have a problem. Yes, we know it's vague.

Contributor Covenant Code of Conduct
Our Pledge
In the interest of fostering an open and welcoming environment, we as
contributors and maintainers pledge to making participation in our project and
our community a harassment-free experience for everyone, regardless of age, body
size, disability, ethnicity, gender identity and expression, level of experience,
nationality, personal appearance, race, religion, or sexual identity and
orientation.
Our Standards
Examples of behavior that contributes to creating a positive environment
include:

Using welcoming and inclusive language
Being respectful of differing viewpoints and experiences
Gracefully accepting constructive criticism
Focusing on what is best for the community
Showing empathy towards other community members

Examples of unacceptable behavior by participants include:

The use of sexualized language or imagery and unwelcome sexual attention or advances
Trolling, insulting/derogatory comments, and personal or political attacks
Public or private harassment
Publishing others' private information, such as a physical or electronic address, without explicit permission
Other conduct which could reasonably be considered inappropriate in a professional setting

Our Responsibilities
Server maintainers are responsible for clarifying the standards of acceptable
behavior and are expected to take appropriate and fair corrective action in
response to any instances of unacceptable behavior.
Server maintainers have the right and responsibility to remove, edit, or
reject comments, commits, code, wiki edits, issues, and other contributions
that are not aligned to this Code of Conduct, or to ban temporarily or
permanently any contributor for other behaviors that they deem inappropriate,
threatening, offensive, or harmful.
Scope
This Code of Conduct applies both within project spaces and in public spaces
when an individual is representing the project or its community. Examples of
representing a project or community include using an official project e-mail
address, posting via an official social media account, or acting as an appointed
representative at an online or offline event. Representation of a project may be
further defined and clarified by project maintainers.
Enforcement
Instances of abusive, harassing, or otherwise unacceptable behavior may be
reported by contacting the maintainer at @floppy. All
complaints will be reviewed and investigated and will result in a response that
is deemed necessary and appropriate to the circumstances. The project team is
obligated to maintain confidentiality with regard to the reporter of an incident.
Further details of specific enforcement policies may be posted separately.
Server maintainers who do not follow or enforce the Code of Conduct in good
faith may face temporary or permanent repercussions as determined by other
members of the project's leadership.
Attribution
This Code of Conduct is adapted from the Contributor Covenant, version 1.4,
available at http://contributor-covenant.org/version/1/4.
</details>

Admin: [@Floppy@mastodon.me.uk](https://mastodon.me.uk/@Floppy)

## [eletusk.club](https://eletusk.club/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=eletusk.club&view=local)
「えれたすく」と読みます、たぶん。
ファンタシースターオンライン2（PSO2）を中心としたファンタシースター関連の話題を楽しむMastodonインスタンスです。
ゆるーくロビーチャットのようなノリで雑談してます。夜の予告イベント前後だと人が多いっぽいです。
※ゲーム会社様とは関係の無い、ファンサイト的なコミュニティです。
トップ画像は、湯呑様（@yunomi@eletusk.club）から頂きました。ありがとうございます！

このインスタンスについて


普段は「ローカルタイムライン」という所で色んな雑談をしてます。
初めて来られた方はちょっと面食らうかもしれませんが、ここにいるほとんどの人がこのインスタンスで知り合った同士なので、気楽に参加してもらえれば。所属Shipもバラバラです。
雑談してる所に混ざるのもいいですし、ゲームについての質問やネタを投げれば高確率で誰かが反応してくれると思います。わりとみんな議論したりアドバイスしたりが好きなので、是非是非何かトゥートしてみて下さい。


登録確認メールについて


登録確認メールが届かない場合、迷惑メールに分類されている恐れがあります。お手数ですが一度ご確認ください。
それでも届かないようであれば、手動で対応致しますので、Twitter @pso2_emg_hourまで、登録に使用したメールアドレスを添えてご連絡ください。


<details><summary>(more)</summary>
このインスタンスに限らずMastodonを使うにあたって


Mastodonは世に出て日の浅く、今なお作り込みが進んでいるソフトウェアです。
運営者として最大限気を配りますが、未知のリスクがある可能性を完全には否定出来ません。
そのようなリスクに遭っても大丈夫なように自衛しつつ楽しく使って下さい。
最低限、他サイトとのパスワードの使い回しは絶対にダメです。


また、投稿は会員登録制ですが、TLの閲覧にはその制限はありません。
その上、他のインスタンスと繋がるMastodonの性質上、一度投稿した物はどこまで拡散されるか分かりません。
見られて困る場面があるかもしれない物は、投稿しないのが安全です。
逆に加害者にならない為に、『仲間内だけで通じる際どいジョーク』みたいなモノの扱いにも気を付けて下さい。


脅かすような事ばかり言ってて何ですが、Mastodonは適切に使えば便利なモノです。
当インスタンスでも皆様に楽しんで頂ければ幸いです。


このインスタンスについて もうちょっと


このインスタンスにおけるMastodonのバージョンは1.3.3です。


予想より多くの人に来て頂いたので、継続的な運営を目指して4/28にサーバー交換を行いました。
また同時に、メールサーバーも導入しました。以前登録しようとして確認メールが届かずあきらめた方も、今一度試して頂けるとありがたいです。


インスタンス維持の足場固めが一段落ついたので、ちょっと便利な機能の追加やカスタマイズに着手したいと思ってますが、何時完成するかは全然分かんないです。
あと、サイトの見た目を変えたいとも思ってるのですが、残念ながら絵心もデザインセンスも無いので、皆様にご助力を仰ぐことになるかも。
トップ画像ぐらいはとっとと変えたいのですが。


Eletusk（えれたすく）という名前について


海外版ファンタシースター２に出て来る敵"Mastodon"の色違い版の名前から来てます。
変に捻らず、素直にマルモスとかにしとけば良かったと後悔中。
日本版での名前は"デゾリアンマンモス"だったかな？


</details>

Email: Not Available

Admin: [@Admin_eletusk@eletusk.club](https://eletusk.club/@Admin_eletusk)

## [mstdn.awa.sfc.keio.ac.jp](https://mstdn.awa.sfc.keio.ac.jp/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.awa.sfc.keio.ac.jp&view=local)
このインスタンスについて / About this mastodon instance
keio.ac.jp か keio.jp なメールアドレスを持っている人が利用できるmastodonインスタンスです。教育・研究目的のため、研究室の垣根を超えたスタッフによって運営されています。慶應義塾が正式に設置したインスタンスではありません。
Anyone who has keio.ac.jp or keio.jp email address can signup this instance.
注意事項 / ToS
本インスタンスは本インスタンスは慶應義塾大学の資産並びに、SFC-CNS上で運用されています。SFC-CNS利用内規IIで定める禁止事項に該当する利用(例.商用、公序良俗に反する投稿など)は固く禁止します。
This instance is running on the assets of Keio University and network connectivity has provided by SFC-CNS. Activities prohibited by Internal Rules for Using SFC-CNS are also prohibited on this instance.
問い合わせ / Contact Us
本インスタンスについての問い合わせは、mstdn-ops@awa.sfc.keio.ac.jpまでお願いいたします
If you wish to contact us, please send a mail to mstdn-ops@awa.sfc.keio.ac.jp

## [pouet.yolops.net](https://pouet.yolops.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=pouet.yolops.net&view=local)
Ce service est fourni à titre de courtoisie et absolument sans garantie.
Je vous promets d'essayer de faire les choses bien et d'assurer une certaine stabilité du service (à laquelle j'ai tout intérêt, car je l'utilise), mais n'attendez pas un support pro, je fais ça juste pour le fun ;)
Les règles de la modération sont ici : https://pouet.yolops.net/about/more

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Cette instance est un endroit de libre-expression.

Comme celle-ci doit malheureusement connaître des limites, il est bon de les énoncer.
Voici ce que je n'admet pas en tant qu'administrateur de l'instance :

-le racisme
-le sexisme
-la LGBTphobie
-l'humiliation
-l'appel à la haine
-le harcèlement
-la volonté de nuire à l'autre
-la pédopornographie

Ça n'est pas exhaustif ni figé, mais c'est pour bien comprendre les valeurs en jeu ici.
La personne qui fait ça, de manière non équivoque, c'est un ban direct.

Pour le reste, vous pouvez poster du porn, de la religion ou du steak tartare, en CW ou pas, je m'en balance.
Ce sont vos valeurs morales, elles ne concernent que vous et vos interlocuteurs, s'ils veulent vous bloquer, qu'ils le fassent eux-mêmes. Si vous voulez vous censurer c'est pareil, je ne le ferai pas à votre place.

Enfin, Mastodon permet de bloquer au niveau de l'instance même, des utilisateurs d'autres instances, voire une instance entière.
Ce pouvoir est particulièrement lourd, voici donc la liste exhaustive des blocages en cours de manière globale à l'instance :
- utilisateur : @jpney@masto.themimitoof.fr
- instance : https://pawoo.net/ (silence + no media caching : les toots ne s'afficheront pas dans la federated timeline, mais vous pouvez suivre des utilisateurs de cette instance)

Ce service est hébergé en Allemagne, les règles s'appliquant en termes de contenu et de gestion des données privées sont donc celles de ce pays.
</details>

Email: [mastodon-dek@iono.me](mailto:mastodon-dek@iono.me)

Admin: [@dek@pouet.yolops.net](https://pouet.yolops.net/@dek)

駅メモファンによる、駅メモファン向けの非公式Mastodonインスタンスです。

## [ephemeral.glitch.social](https://ephemeral.glitch.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=ephemeral.glitch.social&view=local)
toots on this instance are ephemeral; they disappear after a while (between 5 minutes and an hour) depending on the current phase of the moon.
also a disclaimer: your toots will be deleted from this instance. other instances that federate with this one SHOULD delete your toots but unfortunately that's not something that can be guaranteed.
UNSTABLE BUT FRIENDLY

This instance also has domain level blocks on numerous others, using the block list found here . 

followbots from other instances will be blocked. please report them

Some rules


Do not engage in harassment of any kind.
Racist, sexist and other oppressive slurs will get you suspended, even in non-public conversations.
You can post porn and nudity, but you must use the nsfw flag and do not post on the public timeline or you will be silenced (ask around how to make unlisted posts)
try to be kind
no non-sentient bots until further notice
no shit that's illegal in Canada
animated gifs should always be marked sensitive/NSFW and identified as animated gifs (for now let's say just putting 'gif' in the text of the toot is sufficient), because they can cause serious problems for people
oh yeah, NO SCREENSHOTS or copying text of toots not belonging to you. it defeats the purpose

some guidelines

stuff here is impermanent but i still want this to be as safe a space as we can reasonably make it. let's keep common triggers and angry/ranty/grumpy toots behind CWs
free speech maximalists can kindly fuck off. there are instances where that is a priority. this is not one of them.
all languages are welcome!

the privacy stuff in the 'terms' isn't what it should be, but no time to change it yet. this instance's data will not be sold or traded or whatever.

BE WARNED this instance may actually be unstable at times. It will likely be used for experimenting with settings and tweaks to Mastodon. So the place may experience outages, not federate reliably with the rest of the world, have posts go missing, or other technical faults. As such it's meant to be a chill, maybe kinda playful place. Time to see what we can do with this thing! Time to ˥∀IƆOS HƆ⊥I˥⅁

こにゃにゃちは～
Mastodonカードキャプターさくら/CLAMPインスタンスにアクセスしていただきありがとうございます。
さくらインスタンスですが、特に話題は限定せずここをメインとして様々なことを発信していただければ本望です。
安定運用と長期提供を目指しますが4/15の立ち上げより日数がたっていないのと個人運営のため予期せぬトラブルに見舞われる可能性があります。
絶対、大丈夫だよ。

現状このインスタンスは6CPU/8GBRAMのクラウドサーバーで稼働しており、ストレージは200GBです。今のところリソースには余裕がありますがユーザーが増えて重くなるようであればまた検討します。

## [mastodon.cx](https://mastodon.cx/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.cx&view=local)
👉 Alternative Mastodon instance hosted in France by Netrix.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>🇫🇷 Bonjour à tous !
🌎  (English version below)
👔 Owner : @jordan — 👀 Admins : @andre & @Peter 

Afficher la liste des comptes d'organisations ou de marques vérifiés
Cacher la liste des comptes d'organisations ou de marques vérifiés


@Visov1
@Hardisk

Vous êtes une organisation, ou vous possédez une marque déposée et vous souhaitez être vérifiés ? Contactez @andre


Bienvenue sur cette instance (majoritairement) Française de Mastodon. Une question ? Nous sommes là pour vous répondre, publiez simplement en « local » ou à @support@mastodon.cx et nous vous aiderons.
— 🚫 Merci de ne pas publier du contenu :

Publicitaire (excessif)
Spam (non-désiré)
Extrêmement Violent (images gores, etc)
Raciste, sexiste, xénophobe, discriminant..
Incitant à la haine
Nazisme, extrémisme, propagande

— ⚠️ Sont autorisés sous « Content Warning » :

Le contenu sexuellement explicite (NSFW)
Les images pouvant heurter la sensibilité des plus jeunes


Tout harcèlement sera sanctionné. Les administrateurs se réservent le droit de supprimer les publications ne respectant pas les règles présentes sur cette page. En cas de manquement grave ou multiple, l’utilisateur se verra malheureusement banni. En cas de publication ne respectant pas les lois en vigueurs concernant la propriété intellectuelle, nous serons dans l’obligation de la supprimer.

Hello ! Welcome to this instance (mainly French) of Mastodon. Questions ? We are here to help you ! Just ask on local timeline or @support@mastodon.cx and we’ll help you.


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Email: Not Available

Admin: [@jordan@mastodon.cx](https://mastodon.cx/@jordan)

## [mastodon.medieval.jp](https://mastodon.medieval.jp/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.medieval.jp&view=local)
ここは中世人のためのマストドン。
おもにヨーロッパの、中世からルネサンスからバロックあたりのことでたのしみましょう。

ここの運営をしているのは、ヴィエール（中世フィドル）とかゴシック・ハープを奏でる中世都市楽師たちなのですが、中世絵師、中世調理人、中世裁縫師、騎士、写本師、錬金術師、魔術師など、みなさまで中世生活を満喫しましょう。

音楽、動画、画像などは歓迎したいのですが、YouTubeやSoundcloudのように著作権の処理は行えません。ですので、「著作権の問題がないことがわかっているもの」以外はアップロードしないでください。
18禁コンテンツ、十字軍的宗教弾圧、魔女狩りは禁止です。イヤな予感のする発言は消しちゃったりします。
サーバーは日本にありますので、日本国の法にしたがってください。

なお、サーバー運営は 中世クヲリティです。なにかあったら、ごめんヽ(ﾟ∀｡)ﾉ


<details><summary>(more)</summary>中世人のためのマストドンと謳っておりますが、髭男爵もバロッカーもまとめて大歓迎です。
ここの運営をしているのは、ヴィエール（中世フィドル）とかバロック・ヴァイオリンとかゴシック・ハープとかバロック・フルートを演奏したりする都市楽師たちなのですが、絵画や彫刻を愛でる方、料理や衣装を再現されている方、甲冑かぶって騎士道を邁進される方、写本師の方、錬金術や黒魔術を嗜む方、みなさまで中世生活を満喫しましょう。
ただし、十字軍的宗教弾圧（および宗教勧誘）や魔女狩りは禁止です。

なお、サーバー運営は 中世クヲリティです。なにかあったら、ごめんヽ(ﾟ∀｡)ﾉ

</details>

Email: [mastodon@medieval.jp](mailto:mastodon@medieval.jp)

Admin: [@hazakura@mastodon.medieval.jp](https://mastodon.medieval.jp/@hazakura)

## [infinimatix.net](https://infinimatix.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=infinimatix.net&view=local)
Infinimatix, coined by blending infinity and informatics, is a community of interest in informatics with a federated node in the Mastodon fediverse.

The topics of informatics that we are interested in are mainly big data, data science, machine learning, artificial intelligence, deep learning, data mining, information systems, cyber security, web design, web development, web performance optimization, human-computer interaction, user experience design, and so on.

Reach out to @derekcecillewis if you'd like to have an appropriate discipline added to the list.

## [mapicardie.fr](https://mapicardie.fr/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mapicardie.fr&view=local)
Ma Picardie repose sur  Mastodon. Mastodon est un logiciel libre de microblog et ressemblant à Twitter.
Sur Ma Picardie vous pouvez écrire des messages courts (maximum 500 caractères) et suivre les membres du réseau sans publicité ni pistage.
Avec Ma Picardie, vous êtes dans un lieu d'échange libre, décentralisé et fédéré

## [tusk.social](https://tusk.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=tusk.social&view=local)
PLEASE NOTE: There is no way yet to delete accounts or change usernames. So please bear that in mind before creating an account.
Just another Mastodon instance. But we like it here. Bad behavior is not rewarded. If your hobbies involve harassing people, the constant use of 'SJW' or 'cuck' as pejoratives, or just general shitposting, then find somewhere else to go. You own your freedom. I own the server. A longer, more-detailed policy for this instance is in the works.
Tusk.social uses the Witches.Town domain block list. 
Don't harass. Don't be a shitty person. Do that, and we'll get along just fine.
PS - Yo, please get an icon straight away so you don't look like a bot. Also, local accounts which haven't tooted after 45 days are subject to deletion/suspension. Also also, while it's not a rule, just a request... please don't use this instance for follow bots and the like. If it takes, rather than contributes, please do that somewhere else.
Extended About Page
