## [mastodon.network](https://mastodon.network/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.network&view=local)
A social network open to all users.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>This is a free and open Mastodon instance ran by @ian.

We're one of the largest and most active Mastodon instances around, and we're quickly growing as a community. We are also federating with many of the other major instances. If you have questions about how this works or how to create your own instance, feel free to reach out.

If you see any abusive behavior, please report it. Each report is reviewed personally. Please treat each other with respect.

This instance is hosted on three servers: Two load balanced web servers and database server. They each have the following specifications:
- 4 core Xeon 2.13GHz CPU
- 8GB RAM
- SSD storage

Hosting costs are being covered by myself currently. If we need to upgrade servers in the future, I may post a link to help cover costs.

If you have any questions, feel free to ask.

mastodon 日本語サーバです。
Mastodon サーバの立て方 書きました。

ルール

日本の法律に抵触するようなコンテンツは厳禁です。警察や裁判所等行政機関からログやデータの提出を求められた場合、開示をいたします。
エログロなど、他人が不快に思う可能性のあるトゥートをする場合は、CW/NSFWを必ず設定してください。
一般的にスパムと呼ばれるような行為は禁止します。

注意事項

あらゆるマイノリティの方が利用している・インターネット上の誰でも閲覧が出来ることを心がけてください。
このサーバは試験的運用をしています。データの保証・サービスの可用性の保証はいたしません。

ルール
日本国の法律に抵触するような公序良俗に反する投稿はyametene。

テスト的な面が強いので接続数によってはものっすごく重くなったり、最悪突然消えてなくなります。ご了承下さい。一応死ぬ前には断末魔の声上げます。

opencoconプロジェクトをはじめとした、Linux/BSD/Android(Custon ROM等)/Thin Client まわりの開発者・利用者が自由に議論できればと思い、IRC代わりのマイクロブログサーバとして設置してみました。

Mastodon 1.2.2をソース無修正で deploy しています。

## [mastodon.crypt.lol](https://mastodon.crypt.lol/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.crypt.lol&view=local)


<details><summary>(more)</summary>Bienvenu sur l'instance mastodon du domaine crypt.lol.



Les inscriptions sont actuellement ouvertes.


Nous n'imposons aucunes rêgles particulières en matière d'expression et demandons simplement de faire preuve de sens commun. Nous ne tolérons donc aucun message raciste, sexiste, xénophobe, ..., sur les timelines public ou local. Le non-respect de cette (simple) rêgle entraînera un ban et une suppression immédiate de votre compte. Libre à vous d'exprimer les idées les plus nauséabondes qui soient tant que celles-ci restent privées.
Nous décourageons toutefois cet usage et tenons à rappeler que vos messages, y compris privés, ne le sont absolument pas. 
Moi et d'autres administrateurs, que cela soit de cette instance ou d'une autre, sommes en mesure de lire ceux-ci et nous ne pouvons garantir la suppression de vos messages sur chaque instance. Voir ce lien pour plus d'informations.
Réfléchissez donc à deux fois avant de poster des choses qui pourraient être préjudiciables à vous ou à votre interlocuteur.trice.
Nous recommandons fortement l'usage d'autres plateformes et protocoles de chiffrement adaptés à cette fin.


Toute forme de menace, harcèlement, chantage, ..., envers un autre utilisateur.trice est également proscrit et sera sanctionnée *au minima* d'une suppression de votre compte.



Le serveur est hébergé en France sur le réseau d'Iliad. Nous accordons une grande importance au respect de la vie privée et les disques durs sont intégralement chiffrés. N'ayant pas un accès physique à la machine, nous ne pouvons toutefois garantir que modérément l'efficacité de cette méthode. Voir cette page.

Activistes/militants ? Utilisez tor.


Administrateurs.trices d'une instance ? En cas de problème, vous pouvez contacter le compte @Pachy ou utiliser l'addresse mail présente sur cette page.
Vous pouvez également contacter @Neph ou
@Diagamma si vous n'obtenez pas de réponses suffisamment rapidement.
</details>

Email: [pachyderme@crypt.lol](mailto:pachyderme@crypt.lol)

Admin: [@Pachy@mastodon.crypt.lol](https://mastodon.crypt.lol/@Pachy)

## [twingyeo.kr](https://twingyeo.kr/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=twingyeo.kr&view=local)
Twingyeo (트잉여)는 한국어 사용자를 위한 Mastodon 인스턴스입니다.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>인스턴스 규칙 및 기타 공지 사항
2017/04/26 16:31 갱신
규칙

이 인스턴스에서는 다음과 같은 행위를 금지하고 있으며 규칙을 위반할 시 예고 없이 계정이 정지될 수도 있습니다.
※ 여기서 컨텐츠는 사용자가 이 인스턴스에 업로드한 Toot나 미디어를 칭합니다.


성적・잔혹 등의 다른 사용자가 불쾌함을 느낄 수 있는 과격한 내용의 컨텐츠를 NSFW 표시 없이 Public Timeline에 투고하는 행위
다른 사용자를 모욕하거나 괴롭힘, 사칭, 명예 훼손의 목적으로 계정을 생성하거나 컨텐츠를 투고하는 행위 (사이버 불링・리벤지 포르노…)
스크립트 등의 자동화된 수단을 사용하여 계정을 다중 생성하거나 광고를 투고하는 행위

관리자 목록
현재 관리자 목록은 다음과 같습니다.

@cheesekun

관리자가 지켜야 할 규칙

모든 관리 사항은 최대한 투명하게 이루어져야 합니다.
신념, 입장의 차이, 개인적인 원한과 같은 이유로 사용자의 계정을 함부로 정지하지 않아야 합니다.

기타

이 인스턴스는 100% 자비로 운영되고 있지만 현재 후원은 받지 않습니다.
Twitter @twingyeo_kr 를 팔로우 하셔서 이 인스턴스와 관련된 소식을 받아 보세요!

</details>

Admin: [@cheesekun@twingyeo.kr](https://twingyeo.kr/@cheesekun)

## [freeradical.zone](https://freeradical.zone/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=freeradical.zone&view=local)
Free Radical is our social media haven. It's where we talk in an inviting, respectful setting where we can set our own boundaries. We'd love for you to join us!

Read about our adventures on the Free Radical Blog.


<details><summary>(more)</summary>Code of Conduct
Prior art

Mastodon.social guidelines
JSConf Code of Conduct
Toot Café guidelines

The short version

Don't harass anyone
If someone is harassing you, report it to a moderator
Have fun
Be excellent to each other

Moderators

@tek

Blocked instances
We block some other instances. The full list is on GitHub. Contact a moderator if you wish to dispute an entry.
Rules

No advertising or excessive promotion
No bots, unless they're cute, funny, or useful. Bots should avoid posting to the public timeline.
No pornography, nudity, or something that would be considered "NSFW" in a U.S. workplace, even behind a NSFW warning.
No gore or graphic violence
Content that is borderline NSFW or could be construed as NSFW at a glance should be put behind a CW (Content Warning)
No racism
No sexism
No discrimination based on gender, sexual minority, sexual orientation, disability, physical appearance, body size, race, ethnicity, religion (or lack thereof), or national origin
No xenophobia or violent nationalism
No sexual depictions of children
No holocaust denialism, Nazi symbolism, promotion of National Socialism, or anything that is illegal in the European Union
No stalking or harassment
No fake accounts, even celebrity joke accounts. Note this rule does not necessarily apply to remote accounts.

Handling harassment
If you are being harassed, please report the user using the "…" button and then "Report." For urgent concerns, please DM a moderator.
If you engage in harassing behavior, the moderator may take any action they deem appropriate, such as a warning or an expulsion.
The above rules may change at any time, and you may be banned at any time based on the moderators' judgment.
Privacy policy
What will we do with your data? Nothing. How will you be influenced by advertisers? You won't; brands and non-humans (other than fun/useful bots) are banned. How will we aggregate your data in order to improve your service… none of that.
We will never share your data with anyone else, except in the case of valid legal requests if it comes to that. (Hopefully it won't come to that!)
Understand though that this instance is run by me and my friends, and (as is the case with all Mastodon servers) we potentially have access to your data, including DMs. The back-end is also not encrypted. If this is not okay with you, this might not be the instance for you.
Also, for truly private data sent between two people, Mastodon offers no E2E encryption. So use Signal or WhatsApp for the things you really want to be private.
More privacy measures on Free Radical:

Our robots.txt file asks crawlers not to explore the site.
HTTPS is used everywhere thanks to Let's Encrypt.
No ads or trackers.
Links are direct URLs rather than tracking redirects.

Discussion and feedback
For questions about policy, bots, design, theming, etc., please open an issue.
About this server
Free Radical is a Digital Ocean droplet in San Francisco. It's maintained by Kirk Strauser. Thanks for visiting!
</details>

Email: [tek@freeradical.zone](mailto:tek@freeradical.zone)

Admin: [@tek@freeradical.zone](https://freeradical.zone/@tek)

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Siamo un gruppo di cinque persone con la passione per FOSS e self-hosting; e quando abbiamo sentito di Mastodon, beh - questo è il risultato.

## [mastodon-srv.gq](https://mastodon-srv.gq/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon-srv.gq&view=local)
Mastodon日本サーバ(鯖)です。
サーバについての情報
さくらのVPSで運営しています。
リージョン(DC)は石狩です。
投稿にあたって守ってほしいこと
他人の名誉を毀損する投稿など法律に違反するような内容は投稿しないでください。
未成年が閲覧しても問題がない内容を投稿してください。
投稿する場合は、投稿する種類ごとに以下のようにしてください
守れない場合はBAN(アカウント停止処分)を行う場合があります。
PCとスマートフォンなどのブラウザから投稿する場合
テキストに対して閲覧制限を設ける場合は、CWをクリックorタップすると、Content Waring又は閲覧注意と表示されます。
※CWを有効化していてもContent Waring又は閲覧注意に何も入力していない場合は、通常の投稿として扱われますので、ご注意ください。
画像に対して閲覧制限を設ける場合は、画像投稿後にNSFWをクリックorタップしてください。
Amaroqを使い投稿する場合
テキストに対して閲覧制限を設ける場合は、Hide text behind warningをONにします。
ONにすると、Content Waringが表示されます。
画像に対して制限を設ける場合は、Mark media as sensitiveをONにします。
・喧嘩(けんか)などはしないようにしてください(本サーバ内又はリアルを含め)。
・喧嘩(けんか)をした場合は当事者間の解決とし、運営人は一切関与しないものとします。
・極端な連続投稿などDoS攻撃と思われるような投稿又、DoS攻撃やDDoS攻撃などはサービス運営の妨げになるので行わないでください。
※故意な連続投稿であると当方が判断した場合該当IPアドレスからの接続拒否やユーザの活動の制限を行う場合があります。
お問い合わせ
お問い合わせはmastodon(at)ichigo-lab.netまでおねがいします。
送信時には(at)を@にかえてください。
寄付及びその他
※運営には私費がかかっています。
現在サーバーは最低ランクですが、寄付が多ければスペックアップの可能性もあります。
また、ドメイン名も短いものを簡単なものに変更できるかもしれません。
Enty
Amazonほしい物リスト
BitCoin

『157ottxpMaENVC8FJwXXgBWZryhZxq6Dv3』
ichigo-lab BLOGも支援よろしくお願い致します。
寄付を頂いた際には、明細書のコピー等を掲載し使途をはっきりさせます。
アカウントにログインできない場合
パスワードを忘れて、メールアドレスも変わってしまった場合は、私でも対処ができませんので、あきらめてアカウントの再作成を行ってください。
利用規約等
利用規約は以下のURLより閲覧してください。
http://ichigo-lab.net/rule.html


<details><summary>(more)</summary>ichigo-lab.netが設置するMastodonの日本語サーバー(鯖)です。
IT系のインスタンスを目指していますが、投稿する内容はIT以外でもOKです。
皆さんお気軽に登録してトゥートしてね

## [niigata.minnna.xyz](https://niigata.minnna.xyz/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=niigata.minnna.xyz&view=local)
Niigata Mastodonは株式会社muku.と+CREATIVEが共同で運営するMastodonのインスタンスです。「新潟」の事を中心に幅広くご利用いただけます。

<details><summary>(more)</summary>ご利用について

公序良俗を守り、法律の遵守をお願いします。犯罪行為になどによる、警察や裁判所の要請に応じログを開示することがあります。
R18になりそうな文章をトゥートする場合はCWをつけ、画像にはNSFWを付けてください。上項に触れるような文章や画像の投稿はNGとします。
連投やスパム配信など、迷惑ととらえられる投稿は禁止します。宣伝なども過度に行わないようにお願いします。
ユーザー同士のトラブルに関して、運営は一切責任を持ちません。お問い合わせ頂いても仲裁はできかねます。当事者同士でご解決ください。

</details>

Email: [mstdn@muku-corp.co.jp](mailto:mstdn@muku-corp.co.jp)

Admin: [@muku@niigata.minnna.xyz](https://niigata.minnna.xyz/@muku)

## [lgbt.io](https://lgbt.io/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=lgbt.io&view=local)
By signing up, you agree to abide by the Terms and the Rules for this instance as follows:-

Do not discriminate, harrass and/or insult members based on their religion, race, sex, political beliefs, or whether they are gay or straight.
Do not bully and/or pick on other members.
Do not flame other members.
Do not advertise. As of now, you are not permitted to make money using lgbt.io.
Do not publicly expose your real identity unless you're using "Direct" privacy and you're communicating with someone you can trust.
Do not post screenshots or history of toot conversations publicly without all participants' consent.
Do not post copyrighted, piracy, warez and leaked content.
Do not spam.
All NSFW/sexual content must be accompanied by NSFW (not safe for work) and/or CW (content warning) option when writing a toot.
..more rules will be added when needed.

Note: Make sure to report any toots that violate the rules. A staff member will evaluate the reported toots and take appropriate actions against the them.
Happy tooting! :)

## [masto.raildecake.fr](https://masto.raildecake.fr/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=masto.raildecake.fr&view=local)
Une instance publique de Mastodon, hébergé et administré avec amour sur notre machine perso chez tetaneutral.net dans le Sud de la France.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Informations pratiques
En cas de soucis, de questions, n'hésitez pas à écrire à masto@raildecake.fr ou à tooter @zoski.

Vous pourrez trouver un peu d'aide et des informations supplémentaires sur :

le compte officiel du support de Mastodon : @support.
Il y à aussi une FAQ non officielle.
Le très bon article de Alda.


Règles
Du bon sens et du respect d’autrui...
Comme dirait les anglais : Don't be a dick
Cette instance n'a pas vocation à accueillir des robots et autres bots. Hébergez votre propre instance ou rejoignez-en une qui les acceptent. Pareillement les follow bot ne sont pas bienvenu.
La propagande politique telle qu'elle à lieu sur Twitter est priée de rester sur... twitter. Pas de ça ici, c'est du spam et sera considéré comme tel.
Le contenu pouvant choquer (NSFW, politique et cie) doit être taggé proprement à l'aide du content warning (CW). Le but est de n'importuner personne. Votre avatar ne devra pas être obscène ni classé NSFW. En cas de doutes demandez à @zoski ou @shug0
Je souhaite respecter la liberté d'expression de tous mais les comportements déplacés seront sanctionnés.
Vous pensez qu'il est important de rajouter certaines règles ici ? Contactez moi par Mastodon ou par e-mail.
Gestion de vos données
L'administrateur système (moi zoski) je m'engage à protéger vos données au meilleur de mes compétences. Je ne vendrais pas, ni ne tirerais partie des informations que je peux être amener à voir dans l'exercice de mes fonctions.
Vos données, pouets (toots) et les média partagés sur masto.raildecake.fr se trouvent sur mon serveur hébergé chez tetaneutral.net à Toulouse. Un backup chiffré de ses données est effectué chaque nuit sur un disque dur à mon domicile.
Vous pouvez exporter vos information depuis votre profil dans le cas ou vous souhaitez changer d'instance.
Il n'est pas encore possible de supprimer votre compte
Fediverse et blocage
Voici la liste à jour des blocages émis par notre serveur ou à l'encontre de celui-ci par d'autres instances. Vous ne pourrez pas interagir avec ces domaines. Désolé pour la gène occasionné. Si vous pensez qu'une instance mérite de figurer ci-dessous faites signe.
Nous bloque


good-dragon.com suite à cette demande de unfollow de bot. Ce serveur semble être hors ligne actuellement


Que l'on bloque
Personne et pourvu que ça dure ;-)
Soutenir Mastodon
Si tu souhaites aider Gargron le développeur du projet voici son patreon.
Si tu souhaites aider notre instance de Mastodon, Je réfléchi à une méthode de dons en toutes transparence. En attendant tu peux donner à une association ou une œuvre de charité ça sera tout aussi utile.
Hébergement du serveur
Notre serveur, Mugen est hébergé chez tetaneutral.net un fournisseur d'accès à internet associatif respectant la neutralité du réseau. C'est un anciens portable Lenovo de récupération animé par un i5, 8Go DDR3, 250Go de SSD et 600Go de disque dur.
À bientôt dans le fediverse ! 
Gaël/Zoski
</details>

Email: [masto@raildecake.fr](mailto:masto@raildecake.fr)

Admin: [@zoski@masto.raildecake.fr](https://masto.raildecake.fr/@zoski)

サーバ（～2017/04/30）

日本国法に抵触する行為

## [ohai.su](https://ohai.su/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=ohai.su&view=local)

ohai.su


<details><summary>(more)</summary>Code of Conduct
As tooters on this instance, we pledge to uphold an environment that is radically inclusive with respect for all users of the instance.
We are committed to making participation in this instance an oppression-free experience for everyone, regardless of level of experience, gender, gender identity and expression, sexual orientation, disability, personal appearance, body size, race, ethnicity, age, religion, or nationality.
We define oppression as any language or action that expresses, reinforces, upholds or sympathizes with any form of systemic social domination.
Examples of unacceptable behavior by participants include:
The use of sexualized / violent language or imagery at non-consenting parties, on the public timeline, or without the nsfw filter
Personal attacks
Trolling or insulting/derogatory comments
Public or private oppressive language or actions
Other unethical conduct
Users are empowered and responsible for addressing any abuses of the Code of Conduct such that the project remains an oppression-free experience.
By adopting this Code of Conduct, users commit themselves to fairly and consistently applying these principles to every aspect of using this instance. users who do not follow or enforce the Code of Conduct may be permanently banned.
This Code of Conduct applies both to toots on ohai.su and to public spaces when an individual is representing ohai.su or its community.
Instances of abusive, harassing, or otherwise unacceptable behavior may be reported by contacting an admin by using the report button. All reports will be reviewed and investigated and will result in a response that is deemed necessary and appropriate to the circumstances. Admins are obligated to maintain confidentiality with regard to the reporter of an incident.
</details>

## [mastodon.gougere.fr](https://mastodon.gougere.fr/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.gougere.fr&view=local)
Vive les gougères ! mnt-by: @yapret @papaeng89

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Gougère ?
Vous vous trouvez sur l'instance Mastodon de Gougère, un réseau informatique géré sur notre temps libre. L'instance est maintenue par @papaeng89 et @yapret.
Le serveur se trouve dans le datacenter Auxerrois de Virtua Networks, et utilise la bande passante de SCANI.
Quelques règles
De manière générale, les utilisateurs de cette instance sont invités à respecter la Netiquette (telle que décrite dans la RFC 1855).
Les contenus NSFW sont autorisés seulement s'ils sont taggés comme tels et légaux en France, de même que les spoilers pouettés doivent l'être sous Content Warning explicite. Il est souhaitable que chacun tente, dans la mesure du possible, de ne pas flooder, notamment sur les timelines publiques.
La liberté des uns s'arrête là où commence celle des autres. Si quelqu'un empiète sur la vôtre, vous pouvez le bloquer et/ou le signaler aux administrateurs, qui se chargeront, avec l'avis de la communauté, de prendre les mesures nécessaires.
Nous aider
L'accès à l'instance est gratuit et le restera, mais le réseau Gougère a un coût. Pour nous aider à le supporter, c'est par là : https://www.patreon.com/yapret
</details>

Email: Not Available

Admin: [@gougerenet@mastodon.gougere.fr](https://mastodon.gougere.fr/@gougerenet)

## [mstdn.io](https://mstdn.io/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.io&view=local)


Fast and up-to-date instance, welcoming everyone around the world. Come join us!
Up since 04/04/2017.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Welcome on mstdn.io!
I'm @angristan, the admin, a french tech enthusiast and learning sysadmin. I run my french blog here : angristan.fr
This instance is IPv6 compatible, has good HTTPS parameters, is following good security practices, has good uptime is focused on speed and will be updated regularly.
Also, I try to be as transparent as possible.
If you have trouble with the instance, please send my an email or contact me on Twitter : @fuolpit

By @headlessideas (also made the favicon)
Rules :
• Don't flood
• Respect each other
• I (the admin) support freedom of speech, so I won't block accounts or instances unless there is a good reason (like a legal one)
• Use NSFW tags for NSFW content 🔞
• Use content warning for spoilers
• Any language is allowed 🌎
• Have fun 🎉
Feel free to block or mute whoever you want.
What's behind ?
This instance is hosted on a VPS at NiHost, in France. They provide a very good quality of service, and accepted to make a custom VPS for the needs of this instance. Thanks to them!
The VPS has the following specifications :
• 8 virtual cores of Intel Xeon E5-2650v3
• 16 GB of DDR4 RAM
• 100 GB of SSD in RAID 5
• 1 Gb/s unlimited bandwidth
• Debian 8
This server is backed up everyday on another one.
Here are some statistics. You can check all the graphs here.










Check out the live monitoring!
Donations
You can donate to help me maintain this instance in the long term.
Here is what I have to pay :
• Domaine name: 35€/year 
• Server: 16€/month (thanks to my partnership with NiHost)
• Backup server: 10€/month
I also run 4 Tor relays, so your money will alway be put to good use 😊
I also invested a lot of time for this, dozens of hours of installing, tweaking, debugging, optimizing, monitoring, explaining, etc. I love it, it's my passion, but I do this on my free time, so any thanks for my work, financial or not, is really appreciated.
Don't forget to toot me @angristan if you made a donation. 😉

Don't forget to donate to the main dev, he is the one making the hard work for Mastodon : Gargron's Patreon

## [mastodon.technology](https://mastodon.technology/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.technology&view=local)
This Mastodon instance is for people interested in technology. Discussions aren't limited to technology, because tech folks shouldn't be limited to technology either!
Don't be a jerk to anyone or we'll need to be a jerk to you. We adhere to the TootCat Code of Conduct and follow the Toot Café list of blocked instances.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Code of Conduct
As tooters on this instance, we pledge to uphold an environment that is radically inclusive with respect for all users of the instance.
We are committed to making participation in this instance an oppression-free experience for everyone, regardless of level of experience, gender, gender identity and expression, sexual orientation, disability, personal appearance, body size, race, ethnicity, age, religion, or nationality.
We define oppression as any language or action that expresses, reinforces, upholds or sympathizes with any form of systemic social domination.
Examples of unacceptable behavior by participants include:

Personal attacks
Trolling or insulting/derogatory comments
Public or private oppressive language or actions
Other unethical conduct
Users are empowered and responsible for addressing any abuses of the Code of Conduct such that the project remains an oppression-free experience.

Certain types of content should posted in such a way that you avoid showing it to non-consenting parties. These types of content should:

Not be used a profile picture
Be posted with a "NSFW" tag
Not be posted to the public timeline

the above rules apply to content that is:

Sexualized
Violent
Flashing or rapidly changing

By adopting this Code of Conduct, users commit themselves to fairly and consistently applying these principles to every aspect of using this instance. users who do not follow or enforce the Code of Conduct may be permanently banned.
This Code of Conduct applies both to toots on toot.cat and to public spaces when an individual is representing toot.cat or its community.
Instances of abusive, harassing, or otherwise unacceptable behavior may be reported by contacting an admin by using the report button. All reports will be reviewed and investigated and will result in a response that is deemed necessary and appropriate to the circumstances. Admins are obligated to maintain confidentiality with regard to the reporter of an incident.
</details>

Email: [ash@ashfurrow.com](mailto:ash@ashfurrow.com)

Admin: [@ashfurrow@mastodon.technology](https://mastodon.technology/@ashfurrow)

Mastodon in IAMAS -> IAMASTODON

注意点


・分散型といってもSNSの一つであるので、ネットの海に上がるということを意識して使いましょう。法律は守りましょう。


・大事なやりとりは、もっとちゃんとしたところでやりましょう。ここはやはりチラシの裏程度の存在です。


・個人のサーバで運営しているので、情報保持や運営・動作についての保証はできません。認証のパスワードは普段使っていないものにしてください。

Mastodon の　MySQL Fork を作った、まぁ、多分大きな問題はないとおもいます。

<details><summary>(more)</summary>どなたでも参加いただけます！
本インスタンスは、サーバ運用に関する知見の拡大を目的として管理者の私費で運営されます。そのため、国内法に反する行為や迷惑行為がある場合など管理者の判断で対処を行う場合があります。また、管理人の都合で予告なく停止やメンテナンス等すると思いますが、ゆるく長く続けられたらいいなと思っています。
標準プライバシーポリシーへの追記事項として、管理者は、本インスタンス上の個人情報の第三者提供など法令に反する取扱いを一切行わないことを宣言します。
万が一Mastodon自体にセキュリティリスクが発覚した時のため、本人特定が容易なトゥート等を行わないよう各自でご注意のうえご利用ください。ご自身の情報の削除対応や登録のやり直し等に関しては、本人からの問い合わせに限り技術的・時間的に可能な範囲で行いたいと思います。
</details>

## [pegelinux.ga](https://pegelinux.ga/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=pegelinux.ga&view=local)
Pegelinux

This is a community for people who are interested in Programming, Science, and Technology. Our goal is to share and discuss insightful ideas that gratify intellectual curiosity, exchange experience, and help each other to make awesome things.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>How does it works ?
When you create an account on Mastodon, you create an account on the website you currently are visiting. For example, here you are on pegelinux.ga. That is your instance. 

You will notice after log in two different timelines, the Local and the Federated.
The local timeline is all the public toots of all our local users ( the one who registered on pegelinux.ga and use it to access the Mastodon federation ).
The federated timeline adds the public toots of all the users that our local users are following in other servers.
How do I get verified ? Who is who ?
Do it yourself ;) For now there is no verification on Mastodon, it's just an emoji that people add as a joke.
Your identity on Mastodon and the fediverse ( the federation of all the Mastodon instances ) is [email protected]/* <![CDATA[ */!function(t,e,r,n,c,a,p){try{t=document.currentScript||function(){for(t=document.getElementsByTagName('script'),e=t.length;e--;)if(t[e].getAttribute('data-cfhash'))return t[e]}();if(t&&(c=t.previousSibling)){p=t.parentNode;if(a=c.getAttribute('data-cfemail')){for(e='',r='0x'+a.substr(0,2)|0,n=2;a.length-n;n+=2)e+='%'+('0'+('0x'+a.substr(n,2)^r).toString(16)).slice(-2);p.replaceChild(document.createTextNode(decodeURIComponent(e)),c)}p.removeChild(t)}}catch(u){}}()/* ]]> */, so when you register here, your identity is [email protected]/* <![CDATA[ */!function(t,e,r,n,c,a,p){try{t=document.currentScript||function(){for(t=document.getElementsByTagName('script'),e=t.length;e--;)if(t[e].getAttribute('data-cfhash'))return t[e]}();if(t&&(c=t.previousSibling)){p=t.parentNode;if(a=c.getAttribute('data-cfemail')){for(e='',r='0x'+a.substr(0,2)|0,n=2;a.length-n;n+=2)e+='%'+('0'+('0x'+a.substr(n,2)^r).toString(16)).slice(-2);p.replaceChild(document.createTextNode(decodeURIComponent(e)),c)}p.removeChild(t)}}catch(u){}}()/* ]]> */ . How do I follow a user from another instance ?
If you know his username and his instance, you can search for @[email protected]/* <![CDATA[ */!function(t,e,r,n,c,a,p){try{t=document.currentScript||function(){for(t=document.getElementsByTagName('script'),e=t.length;e--;)if(t[e].getAttribute('data-cfhash'))return t[e]}();if(t&&(c=t.previousSibling)){p=t.parentNode;if(a=c.getAttribute('data-cfemail')){for(e='',r='0x'+a.substr(0,2)|0,n=2;a.length-n;n+=2)e+='%'+('0'+('0x'+a.substr(n,2)^r).toString(16)).slice(-2);p.replaceChild(document.createTextNode(decodeURIComponent(e)),c)}p.removeChild(t)}}catch(u){}}()/* ]]> */ and from there it should be pretty easy. It's pretty young so there's room for improvements, and I'm sure that we'll end up being able to search across instances. There is now also some sites that allows searching users. You can always look at the federated timeline and find some interesting contacts !
How do I mask X language from the timelines ? I can't read that
That's a feature being developed at the moment, but you can always head to Mastodon lang remover to do it in your browser without waiting for the feature to be integrated.
Who is moderating the instance ?
For the moment, you, by reporting the posts and users and the admin enforcing the rules. (@kimiamania)
How often do you update the service ?
Usually the day a new stable version is released. You can follow @kimiamania for announces when this is happening.
How much does it cost ?
Mastodon is free for the users. This instance is hosted by me, @kimiamania, on my personal funds. Your help is appreciated to maintain/make the platform evolve.
How can I help ?
You can get involved in multiple ways, you can welcome new users, animate the local timeline, promote our instance and invite new users here, report posts and users not respecting our rules... 
You can also help with the costs of running the service by donating, any small amount is appreciated ! Donations are accepted on:

Paypal: https://paypal.me/RezhaJulio
Local Indonesian Bank: BCA, Mandiri, BTPN

</details>

## [mastodon.direct](https://mastodon.direct/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.direct&view=local)
Mastodon.direct is an open Mastodon instance welcoming people to discuss a broad range of topics. We strive to provide a high quality instance with reliability, speed, and a responsive moderation team.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of mastodon.social; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:


    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Excessive advertising
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
For abuse or copyright reports, please email abuse at this domain.
</details>

Email: [hello@mastodon.direct](mailto:hello@mastodon.direct)

Admin: [@djchen@mastodon.direct](https://mastodon.direct/@djchen)

## [sakaba.space](https://sakaba.space/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=sakaba.space&view=local)

よく来たな。ここはマストドン酒場だ。あんたも冒険者なんだろう？見れば分かる。
北の山にモンスターが住み着いてからというもの、ここに来るのはあんたみたいな連中ばかりさ。
ゆっくりしていくといい。各地方から色んな奴らが集まってるから、何かいい情報が聞き出せるかもしれないぜ。


一応ここのルールみたいなもんだ

酒場での話題には決まり事なんかない。好きに話せば誰かが聞いててくれるだろう。
もしモンスターを見かけたら、リプライ（返信）ってやつで何発か攻撃すれば倒せるはずだ。
亡霊や機械人形(bot)でも構わないが、酒場に迷惑をかけるやつは容赦なく叩き出す(BAN)からな。
あまり大きな店じゃないんで、もしかしたら満席（募集停止）になるときが来るかもしれないが勘弁してくれ。


<details><summary>(more)</summary>更新履歴

2017.5.8: BOSS召喚コマンドを実装しました
2017.4.29: ゾンビを実装しました
2017.4.28: 壊れかけた時計を実装しました


お問い合わせ

開発者Mastodon @midori44
開発者Twitter @midori44

</details>

Email: Not Available

Admin: [@master@sakaba.space](https://sakaba.space/@master)

## [oulipo.social](https://oulipo.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=oulipo.social&view=local)
A Dcntralizd and Fdratd Social Ntwork

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Oulipo.social is a lipogrammatic Mastodon for all.
FAQ

I saw a stray fifth symbol! Can you fix it?
 Look at our list of bugs on GitHub. It's probably known, and you shouldn't toot at @mus about it. If it's not known, add a bug or a PR on GitHub. 
Can I post links that contain taboo symbols?
Go for it. Validation skips links and it's not a faux pas at all.
What if I post symbols that look similar to that taboo glyph?
Don't. Mods will discard toots that do this, and if you don't stop, banning may follow.
No problm I'll writ lik this.
No. Stop. Don't do this.
But this is hard?
Practicing will bring you far.
What synonym should I sub in for [x]?
Try to stop looking for synonyms; if you try to swap out individual words, you'll find it tough going. Pull back and think abstractly about what you want to say and find words for that.

Social Contract
This social contract is an adaptation from Mastodon.social.
What follows is not a law contract, and final ruling is up to administrators of oulipo.social; it should function to clarify our community policy and standards:


    Posts similar to any of this will not stay up on our activity list:
    
Abundant ads
Bots that post spam
Pornography without a "CW" or "Tricky Topic" tag
Horrific or traumatic posts without a "CW" or "Tricky Topic" tag
That fifth symbol, or any variant of it, that is found in Latin script, including using "3" or homographic symbols in its spot.



    Posts similar to any of this will not stay up on our activity list, and is possibly grounds for banning:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Misogyny or advocation of misogyny
Discrimination against LGBT minority groups or individuals, or advocation of that
Jingoism or militant nationalism



    Posts similar to any of this will not stay up and is without doubt grounds for banning:
    
Child pornography
Nazism of any kind or any promoting of National Socialism



    Any conduct which could stalk or harass participants or individuals, or stop individuals from participating in this community, or to impact usability and functionality of this community, or to harass anybody, or advocations that accounts do such actions, is not okay, and is grounds for banning any violators. This is activity such as:
    
Continuing to talk to an individual that has said to stop, a platform's privacy tools notwithstanding.
Posting, and/or sharing an individual's data or information without that individual's approval (informally known as doxing or dropping dox).
Inciting accounts to post to an individual in additional discussion if that individual has said it should stop (informally known brigading or dogpiling).



All this notwithstanding, administrators of oulipo.social can ban any accounts, at any point, for any motivation, if not in violation of law.
</details>

Email: [mousereeve@riseup.net](mailto:mousereeve@riseup.net)

Admin: [@mus@oulipo.social](https://oulipo.social/@mus)

## [pao.moe](https://pao.moe/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=pao.moe&view=local)
English instance available! => en.pao.moe
 ご挨拶
pao.moeインスタンスのテーマは主に cat FOSS *nix です．ゆるくハードに語り合いましょう．
「エンジニアはコードで殴り合うべきだ」を標語に，長期間に渡り安定稼働するMastodonインスタンスを目指して，2017年4月14日より運用を開始しました．
ご要望等ございましたら， @nukosu までお気軽にお問い合わせください．
 守るべきこと

このサーバは日本国内に設置されており，日本の法律の影響下にあります．日本の法律に抵触するコンテンツの投稿を禁止します．
Mastodo 及び *.pao.moe は無法地帯の代わりになりうるものではありません，公序良俗を守りましょう．
仲良く（*´・ω・）人（・ω・`*）

## [mastodon.art](https://mastodon.art/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mastodon.art&view=local)
Mastodon.art — a place for your artwork of all types from visual, musical, peformance or ____. Also, fun banter, commentary & cited fair-use posts/art/reviews of others' art too. Welcome to y(our) free & open source decentralized life. Mastodon.art doesn't monetize or profit off of your personal information—your information is never for sale. Export & leave for another instance anytime. No Brand, name or famous trademark squatting. Zero tolerance for harrassment or bullying — your account will be deleted.  🎨 📸✏️🎥🎶💡💬 Powered by v1.3.3 of Mastodon
—
Users are Artists & people here. All content is ⓒ each artist & cannot be distributed or used without prior permission by the respective Mastodon.ART artist. Artists, by using this site you understand that it is not a backup or permanent repository for your information or files. You may leave and join another instance at any time by exporting your statuses & follow list. Your media was downsized on original upload & is not exportable at this time. Thank you for simply enjoying a creative community run by someone supporting the arts.
—
Federation serves as a link & not a perpetual copy - other instances may not disseminate others' work or toots without credit and licensing nor use Machine Learning or AI to analyze any derived text or work for publication or profit. Public toots are derived works that are still protected. This instance honors noindex/nofollow and search engines are not allowed to index.


<details><summary>(more)</summary>What is Mastodon.ART? & CoC
Mastodon.art — a place for your artwork of all types from visual, musical, peformance or ____. Also, fun banter, commentary & cited fair-use posts/art/reviews of others' art too. Welcome to y(our) free & open source decentralized life. Mastodon.art doesn't monetize or profit off of your personal information—your information is never for sale. Export & leave for another instance anytime. No Brand, name or famous trademark squatting. Zero tolerance for harrassment or bullying — your account will be deleted. Your Original Content Only No PornNo LoliArtistic Form No Bots Respect Others

Our instance has a CoC similar to Mastodon.social's and follow its principles while administrating OUR instance
You understand that your users are subject to Mastodon.ART's CoC while interacting with our users
You're not federating with instances whose administration has a history of ignoring or encouraging abuse of Mastodon users on their platform. The instances we're currently particularly concerned about are:
    
shitposter.club
sealion.club
freezepeach.xyz
rainbowdash.net
social.heldscal.la
unsafe.space



Administration

  The current administrators of this instance are:
  
@Curator


Moderators here take on a different role than other places- they do not have the power to directly silence or ban your account, and are instead are volunteers whom the administration trusts with a direct line of commmunication with the admin to help facilitate the respect of boundaries and keep discussion and education civil so that Mastodon.ART is a safe place for folks.
We are interested in more moderators, but are not currently actively searching for new ones.  If you are interested, please contact the administrator.  We are trying to build a diverse team for this place and if you feel you fit into that and don't mind volunteering then please let us know!
Guidelines
The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of Mastodon.ART; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:


    All users, local and remote, are expected to adhere to the following interaction principles:
    
Posting work of others must be cited (or say artist/author unknown) after searching. Fair Use of copyright applies here.
Respect boundaries as placed by others
Be respectful/apologize if someone tells you that you cross a boundary accidentally
Give people space if you accidentally push past a boundary
If you are on either side of this and are worried about the situation escalating, contact the admin or a mod
Tag potentially upsetting content such as violence/blood, politics, and other such topics



    All users, local and remote, will be considered in the wrong in a conversation that goes sour if they participate in the following:
    
Microaggressions ("not all men", white/man/cis-splaining, using the wrong pronouns to address someone after being corrected, etc)
Demanding education on problematic behavior from a non-admin/moderator
Skirting the lines of being a troll
Not tagging potentially sensitive replies

    This is not an exhaustive list.  If any of these don't make sense, please speak with an admin or moderator- we are more than happy to help you understand the problems with these kinds of behavior.
  

    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:
    
Advertising
News bots that do not tag upsetting content
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence



    The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:
    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism



    The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:
    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism



    Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:
    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Email: [—](mailto:—)

Admin: [@Curator@mastodon.art](https://mastodon.art/@Curator)

## [octodon.social](https://octodon.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=octodon.social&view=local)

octodon.social


<details><summary>(more)</summary>Octodon:





no rules in particular, be nice be reasonable call me mommy stuff like that



Seriously though: It should be similar to mastodon.social.
NSFW/any legal porn is allowed, but tag it as NSFW or make it unlisted or less. Trolls are only allowed if they're quiet; you can shitpost but not harass someone, and my threshold is pretty low.
I'm not Twitter, I'll fuck up nazis and bullies for fun, and get an AI to do it if I get bored.
I'm your nice cyberpunk queen and I intend to keep this place decent and safe for everyone.

You should choose an instance based on shared values; here I believe everyone deserve freedom, but also to be safe from harassment and hate. Freedom will not be given a higher priority.

I'll always try to solve problems in the most rational and safe way possible for users, and try to discuss any issue with the people concerned if I think it's worth it. If you at least try to be good and comprehensive, so will I.
I understand and accept mistakes, but not being bad on purpose.


Advertising: Probably never, if any it will not be integrated into content or intrusive, at most I'm thinking about the Wikipedia way of asking for donation when needed.


Federation & Politics: It federates with nearly everything, I'll block whatever instance isn't compatible with this site's rules as needed. For example if a remote user harass a local user and their instance admin endorses it. See list at the end of this page.

Reminder: that's a private place and your free speech means very little to me and most of my users. If your instance gets blocked it's because you endorse hate and/or harassment; then why be pathetic now and bitch about it? You can't force people to like you and being an asshole won't get you friends. Go run your little world.


CW: On public toots (not unlisted, private, or direct), content warnings are required for
any kind of (explicit enough) violence (with or without pics, including gore, *phobia, abuse, sexual or not) and referring to it;
sexual content (pics must already be tagged as NSFW, use a CW if you have text or want to warn about specific content).
This is not about what is culturally or religiously accepted, but about common sources of trauma
that deeply hurt people for very real reasons. Consider yourself lucky if you don't need any of it, but it's not about you.
They are also appreciated but not mandatory on:
politics, spoilers, anything depressing or too negative. Use them in an opportunistic way.


Enforcement:
On this instance, a toot that doesn't follow these rules may be deleted.
On repeated offences or if disturbing public timelines,
the account may get silenced (only their followers will see toots).
If silencing is not enough (harassment, ...), the account may get
completely suspended.
If the account is on another instance, it may get silenced and suspended from here, and I will not hesitate to share reports
with other instance admins.
Instance admins, feel free to contact me about this instance's users' behavior.




Support / Servers:
You can support me/this server through a Patreon here and you can get a VPN here or send bitcoins to 1F3TeADq25W471a1G5W5gJJ1BWbQYn6Di5.



Anyway if you're wondering, it's hosted on Scaleway in France, and it should be pretty stable since I'm a competent sysadmin.
There are full backups done every 12 hours, and sent fully encrypted to an append-only remote server.
Feel free to report it to me directly if it's slow or anything doesn't work.

Server stats:
main, 
app01, 
app02, 
sidekiq01.



Instance blocks:

NameReason

noagendasocial.comAdam is a fucking idiot who enjoys harassing people himself if they report someone. You're breaking the federation Adam.
pawoo.netToo much child porn in public timelines. (silenced)


Also: sealion.club, heldscal.la, freezepeach.xyz, shitposter.club, unsafe.space, gs.smuglo.li, are blocked or silenced as they did allow hate speech and harassment.
</details>

Admin: [@CobaltVelvet@octodon.social](https://octodon.social/@CobaltVelvet)

"Powered by the mighty elephants of Mastodon, binbou box is a humble micro-blogging server for the folks who feel very micro in life."


Really, Angelo? Is that all you can write for the introduction?


Well, yes, inner monologue. It's 2 a.m. and I still have stuff to do in the morning.

Then why don't you go to slee--hmm. Wait a minute...


What is it, other me?

Mmm. Burritos.

You know, maybe you should revis--


Zzzzzzz...

自動化された大量フォロー、大量ポストなどのサーバに負荷がかかる行為

注意事項など

基本的に人の活動に対応するアカウントを想定しています。
宣伝ほかについては迷惑になりそうな場合何らかの対処をする可能性はあります。
無人っぽいアカウントも消す可能性があります。
サーバのメンテナンスについては随時行なう可能性があります。できるだけ起こらないようにしますがメンテナンスの結果データが消える可能性は当然あります。
負荷増大の結果家鯖で処理出来無くなった場合サービスを止めるなどをする可能性はあります。
家鯖の回線の不調、家鯖の不調、家鯖の構成変更ほかによりサービスの可用性に問題が発生する可能性があります。
サーバ内の比較的古い過去の画像などのデータに関しては消していく可能性が高いです。
その他想定外の事象に対しては常識的に考えられる方向にベストエフォートで対応されます。


<details><summary>(more)</summary>
連絡先




神楽坂しえる
@Clworld



ビジネスメールアドレス:
clworld@ggtea.org



</details>

Email: [clworld@ggtea.org](mailto:clworld@ggtea.org)

Admin: [@Clworld@md.ggtea.org](https://md.ggtea.org/@Clworld)

## [manx.social](https://manx.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=manx.social&view=local)
Social platform for the Isle of Man
Ever find that local discussion is lost in the vastness of Twitter? Or you're only reaching those that follow you on Facebook? That is where manx.social comes in - a truly public platform for the Isle of Man.
manx.social lets you get your message across to the island or just tune-in to what's currently happening island-wide.

Also connect with others around the world through the federated network and other instances of Mastodon.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>
Site rules
In order for this website to be able to function, there are some rules that you will have to follow while using it.
Be friendly.

The internet is a network that connects people using computers. The other endpoint is a human being with an inner life just as complex as your own. Act accordingly.
Consider the reach of the posts you make. Tag content that you expect others might not want to see.
Harassment and bullying of any kind are not tolerated here. Do not engage with a user if they do not want you to. Do not ask other users to, either.

Obey the law.

Specifically, UK (server location) and Isle of Man (owner location) law.
No illegal file sharing, no illegal pornography, no publication of personal protected information, you know the drill.

Spam is not allowed.

Bots that interact with a user without a users explicit request are not allowed.
Automated or excessive advertising is not allowed.

Be aware of the nature of the network.

This website is part of a network of similar websites. Other websites may have different rules.
The local administration has little control over users of other websites. You can, however, block and mute them - same as local users.
In egregious cases, remote users or entire groups of users may be blocked from interacting with users of this website.

Admin decisions are final.

The interpretation of these rules is up to the administration and an admins decision overrides the rules.
“Technically I did not violate any rule” is an extremely flimsy excuse for behaving badly.
The rules may be changed or amended when necessary.

These goal of these rules is to ensure a safe and welcoming environment.

Rule enforcement is guided by this goal.
Any enforcement action will generally be kept between those involved.
Try to self-moderate, but do not hesitate to involve an admin when necessary.
There are presently two people with administrative access to the website, @admin, @sati.
You can report rule violations via e-mail.



Mobile Apps
Apps are available for various platforms. We recommend Tusky for Android & Amaroq for iOS. More apps are available here.
 
</details>

Email: [admin@manx.social](mailto:admin@manx.social)

Admin: [@admin@manx.social](https://manx.social/@admin)

Lolicon, immoral and indecent child pics are strictly prohibited

Gory, bloody and violent pictures only in Content Warning.
Don't be a troll, Don't be a bully.
Don't be a jerk, please.
You can report every post you judge offensive.



Any user not respecting these rules may get silenced or suspended.
Bot accounts can be silenced if there are too much complains about them.

## [scholar.social](https://scholar.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=scholar.social&view=local)
A Mastodon instance for academics
"The Mastodon profile that you're not embarrassed to put on the last slide of a presentation at a conference"
Read more ...

<details><summary>(more)</summary>This is a general-purpose federated Mastodon instance. You may use it as a personal account, but the focus is on academics. This is supposed to be "the Mastodon profile that you're not embarrassed to put on the last slide of a presentation at a conference." :P
Real names and credentials are recommended for networking purposes but are absolutely not required.
Do

Brag about your publications
Share references and resources
Network with other academics
Add CW's (content warnings) to your posts liberally: label strong language, rants, spoilers of TV shows, etc. We're academics! We love meta-data!
Recruit participants for academic surveys—formal, IRB-approved ones or even informal ones (just make sure to CW them and don't get too obnoxious about it)

Don't

Post anything that could be described as "spam"
Racism, sexism, homophobia, transphobia, etc.
Impersonate other people
Harass other people

In more detail
Many thanks to mastodon.social, from whom I took these policies.
The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of scholar.social; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:

The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:

    
Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence


The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:

    
Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism


The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:

    
Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism


Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:

    
Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
      Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.



These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

## [bunyip.space](https://bunyip.space/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=bunyip.space&view=local)
Bunyip Space is a Mastodon instance for inclusive and diverse community discussion and social sharing with respect and tolerance. All are welcome.

See here for more information on why you should join, read about our community standards, and why we are called Bunyip Space.


<details><summary>(more)</summary>WHY JOIN THIS INSTANCE?

This instance of Mastodon is targeted at users of any age who wish to engage in safe, mature and stimulating discussion in a welcoming online space. We're happy to have a laugh, but abuse, disrespect, and intolerance are not welcome.

You can register here and follow and interact with users on any other instance in the Fediverse. This Mastadon instance does not intend to block any other instances, so users are free to see whatever they choose from the Fediverse, but we will be strict about preserving our own local timeline as a safe, welcoming and inclusive community.

We recognise the challenge in balancing free speech and protection from extreme and inappropriate language, and we expect that these guidelines and our practice in enforcing them over time will evolve over time, with consultation and communication

We hope to build a quality community, and will consider charging for membership and/or providing other joining restrictions in future to support this.  If we do introduce payments, existing members will be grandfathered in. 

For now, this instance is being run on a volunteer basis, and donations are welcome at https://paypal.me/spickup

WHAT IS A BUNYIP?

The bunyip is a large mythical creature from Australian Aboriginal mythology, said to lurk in swamps, billabongs, creeks, riverbeds, and waterholes. We choose this name as the founder is Australian, although currently living in the UK.
</details>

Email: [sp@bunyip.space](mailto:sp@bunyip.space)

Admin: Not Available

## [hamtter.net](https://hamtter.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=hamtter.net&view=local)

hamtter.netへようこそ。
アマチュア無線家のためのMastodonインスタンスです。
※フリーライセンスラジオやBCL/SWLは扱いません。
登録時のユーザー名は必ずご自身に割り当てられているアマチュア無線のコールサインを半角英数大文字で指定してください。
 例) JA1QRZ 7K4QTH 等
アマチュア無線を楽しんでいることの確認のため、登録用メールアドレスは文末のいずれかのドメイン名のみ受け付けます。
本登録に必要な電子メールが送信されますので、事前に正しく転送されるか確認後に登録作業を行って下さい。
@jarl.com @arrl.net

Internet Explorerは使えません。
他のブラウザを使って下さい。

For Amateur Radio Operator.
Notice:NO CB Radio or BCL/SWL.
Username or screen name Must set your Amateur Radio Callsign(Upper Case). 
 example) W0QRZ KA1QTH etc.
Valid mail address,below domains ONLY.
@jarl.com @arrl.net

Mastdon NOT SUPPORT Internet Explorer.

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Username or screen name Must set your Amateur Radio Callsign(Upper Case).

NO WARRANTY AS-IS.
このインスタンスは極力安定稼働へ努力をいたしますが、個人で運営しているため、動作は無保証、あるがままです。

他インスタンスからリモートフォローをしてきたユーザは必ずしもアマチュア無線家とは限りません。
迷惑だと感じた場合はブロックを推奨します。

参加することによる金銭的な損失、個人情報などの毀損については一切関知しません。

## [nomofomo.social](https://nomofomo.social/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=nomofomo.social&view=local)
This is a work in progress so be patient and be cool

If you want to support this server or continuing development, bitcoin is always appreciated.
1F69UCFCL24xNcRzCeRFMNmGLuaPi1z8yn

<details><summary>(more)</summary>The following guidelines are not a legal document, and final interpretation is up to the administration of nomofomo.social; they are here to provide you with an insight into our content moderation policies:


The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline:

Excessive advertising
Uncurated news bots posting from third-party news sources
Untagged pornography and sexually explicit content
Untagged gore and extremely graphic violence


The following types of content will be removed from the public timeline, and may result in account suspension and revocation of access to the service:

Racism or advocation of racism
Sexism or advocation of sexism
Discrimination against gender and sexual minorities, or advocation thereof
Xenophobic and/or violent nationalism


The following types of content are explicitly disallowed and will result in revocation of access to the service:

Sexual depictions of children
Content illegal in Germany and/or France, such as holocaust denial or Nazi symbolism
Conduct promoting the ideology of National Socialism

Any conduct intended to stalk or harass other users, or to impede other users from utilizing the service, or to degrade the performance of the service, or to harass other users, or to incite other users to perform any of the aforementioned actions, is also disallowed, and subject to punishment up to and including revocation of access to the service. This includes, but is not limited to, the following behaviors:


Continuing to engage in conversation with a user that has specifically has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist may be considered harassment, regardless of platform-specific privacy tools employed.
Aggregating, posting, and/or disseminating a person's demographic, personal, or private data without express permission (informally called doxing or dropping dox) may be considered harassment.
Inciting users to engage another user in continued interaction or discussion after a user has requested for said engagement with that user to cease and desist (informally called brigading or dogpiling) may be considered harassment.
These provisions notwithstanding, the administration of the service reserves the right to revoke any user's access permissions, at any time, for any reason, except as limited by law.
</details>

Email: [info@nomofomo.social](mailto:info@nomofomo.social)

## [torontomusic.cloud](https://torontomusic.cloud/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=torontomusic.cloud&view=local)
A social network for Toronto music folks: artists, bands, presenters, independent media, concertgoers, collaborators, DJs, producers, music sharers, venues, indie record labels, and whoever else wants to join. It's a Mastodon network, and accounts here can follow accounts on any other Mastodon network.
Mastodon is a new open-source social network that's starting to become popular as a Twitter alternative, especially in Japan and France. Twitter is kinda dying these days, so this trend will probably continue. On Masto, you get 500 characters for status updates, there are no ads, and no algorithms. It's still a bit basic compared with established social networks, but it's brand-new. There's a community of volunteer developers working on it and it's getting better every day.

## [mstdn.glorificatio.org](https://mstdn.glorificatio.org/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=mstdn.glorificatio.org&view=local)
ヌルいけど パソコン大好き、テック系インスタンス。Hello Worldからどこまでも

<details><summary>(more)</summary>お知らせ

当インスタンスに登録された方へ送られる確認メールはmailgunというサービスを使っています。

なかには迷惑メール扱いされることもあるようです。
登録したはずなのにメールがこない場合は、
mstdn.glorificatio.orgからの受信を許可してください。

また、hotmailへにはメールが届かないようです。
gmailなどは届いているので、どうしても届かない場合は別のメールにしてみてください。

インスタンスについて

パソコン大好き。
インスタンス主のあたしがそれほどスキル無いので、
プログラマ非ガチ勢インスタンスにします。

キーワード

プログラミング
セキュリティ
Linux
ラズベリーパイ
関数型言語
マストドンインスタンスづくり
インフラエンジニア
工程管理
品質管理
愚痴



インスタンス主について

Linuxクラスタ、プログラマクラスタ、はてなブックマークユーザー的な感じ




インスタンスの環境について

ConoHaVPS メモリ1G コア2個
CentOS 7.3

docker上でマストドンを動かしています。



利用規約 もしくはお願い

個人で管理運営しているインスタンスです。
セキュリティには充分気をつけておりますが、
参加される場合は自己責任でお願いします。
(パスワード使い回しをしないなど)
当インスタンスで発生した損害については責任を負いかねます。

参加される方は、共同運営者のつもりで参加をおねがいします。
インスタンス主だけでは判断が難しい場合には参加者の方々に意見を聞くこともあります。
運営に関して意見がありましたらおっしゃってください。

法律は守ってください。
他人の権利を侵害しないでください。
なりすましはしないでください。
公序良俗に反する行為はおやめください。


</details>

## [rich.gop](https://rich.gop/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=rich.gop&view=local)
Rich.GOP is an open, privacy-conscious, decentralized social network, dedicated to honest,
 open, and civil political discourse.
This instance is funded and maintained by @Motoma
One of the incredibly important pieces of a decentralized social network is diversity of options. To that end I maintain a public Mastodon instance at https://rich.gop. This instance is free of ads, marketers, and stalkers.
I provide this service on a virtualized infrastructure that I own. I would like to improve that infrastructure, in the dimensions of availability, reliability, and speed. Users of a free and public tools shouldn't be beholden to a second-rate service. Here, I leverage my 13 years of professions distributed software development and hosting experience to deliver a first-class experience to my users.
If you would like to support me in my goal of delivering this quality service to the public, please consider supporting this site on Patreon: https://www.patreon.com/motoma

<details><summary>(more)</summary>Code of Conduct
Welcome to Rich.GOP! This Mastodon instance is here you with a friendly environment where you can converse, exchange and discuss ideas, politely debate political subjects, and converse about any other aspects of your lives. Communities are at their best when participants treat each other with respect and courtesy. Therefore, by signing up for an account, you are explicitly agreeing to conduct yourself in a civilized manner when using this instance.
As a user of this instance, you agree to uphold an environment that is radically inclusive with respect for all users of the instance.
As a user of this instance, you commit to making participation in this instance an oppression-free experience for everyone, regardless of level of experience, gender, gender identity and expression, sexual orientation, disability, personal appearance, body size, race, ethnicity, age, religion, nationality, or political affiliation.
By creating an account on this instance, you agree to fairly and consistently applying these principles to every aspect of using this instance. users who do not follow or enforce the Code of Conduct may be permanently banned.
Instances of abusive, harassing, or otherwise unacceptable behavior may be reported by contacting @Motoma or by using the report button. All reports will be reviewed and investigated and will result in a response that is deemed necessary and appropriate to the circumstances.
</details>

Email: [motoma@gmail.com](mailto:motoma@gmail.com)

Admin: [@Motoma@rich.gop](https://rich.gop/@Motoma)

## [pso2.club](https://pso2.club/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=pso2.club&view=local)
Mastodonの、PSO2非公式Instanceです。PSO2ユーザーだけのローカルTLがあったらいいなー、という声が聞こえた気がしたのでつくりました。
※PSO2および株式会社セガゲームスとは一切関係ありません

<details><summary>(more)</summary>利用について

試験サービスのため、予告なくサービスが停止したり、初期化する場合があります。(たぶんとまる)
法に抵触するような文章や画像、動画は投稿しないでください。
PSO2の画像や動画は、著作物利用ガイドラインに則って投稿してください。
危うい内容を投稿する場合はMastodonの機能を活用して、他のユーザーに配慮するよう心掛けましょう。
迷惑行為は禁止します。悪質な場合はBANされる場合があります。
投稿の内容およびその結果について、管理者は一切の責任を負いかねます。

運用について

サポートが必要な場合は、登録時のメールアドレスから、メールにてお問い合わせいただくか、Twitter(@pso2_club)までご連絡ください。
すべてのお問い合わせに対し、対応を保証するものではありません。
権利者からのお問い合わせに対しては迅速に対応します。

</details>

Email: [webmaster@pso2.club](mailto:webmaster@pso2.club)

Admin: [@info@pso2.club](https://pso2.club/@info)

## [don.h3z.jp](https://don.h3z.jp/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=don.h3z.jp&view=local)

a[target="_blank"] {
padding-right: 15px;
background: url("/media/img/ext-icon-mstdn.png") no-repeat center right;
}

 情報
  日本向けのMastodonインスタンスです。
 This is a Mastodon instance for Japan.
 Created: 2017/04/29 23:18 JST
 メール送信元アドレスは mstdn@h3z.jp です。
上記のアドレス宛てにメールを送信しても、/dev/null されます。
 その他の日本のインスタンスは、こちらをご参照下さい。
 現在のサーバーの稼働状況は、こちらをご参照下さい。
 IT系やサブカルで盛り上がっていったらなと思っています。
 サーバー移転により、再構築を行いました。ログイン出来ない場合は、再登録をお願い致します。
 ｢出会い系サイトへの誘導｣ は禁止とさせて頂きます。
 発見次第、問答無用で即アカウント停止となりますのでご注意下さい。
 ｢このインスタンスについて｣ は必読ですよ!!

<details><summary>(more)</summary> (自称) 世界一分かりやすい説明ページ
(今までこのページを超える内容のインスタンスを観たことが無い)

 このインスタンスでの話題
IT系｜インフラ廻り｜アニメやラノベ等のサブカルチャーetc…
管理者は2014/05/20より "趣味" でインフラエンジニアをやっております。上記の話題は管理者が好きなものを列挙していますが、別に縛りとかはありませんので、何をするのかは自由です。(ただし、ルールは守って下さい。)

 サーバーについて
 Web hosted by  (Tokyo)
 Storage hosted by  (asia-northeast1)
Server OS: CentOS 7
front-end: H2O
back-end: Mastodon + PostgreSQL 9.6 + Redis 3.2

 mstdn, PostgerSQL


vCPU
3
Core


RAM
2
GB


SSD
50
GB


 web, Redis


vCPU
2
Core


RAM
1
GB


SSD
50
GB


 web-01

 web-02

 mstdn-srv01

 mstdn-srv02

 PostgerSQL

 Redis



CloudflareやDockerは使用しておりません。
また、Mastodon実行サーバーとDBは別のサーバーで稼働しています。
セキュリティ対策のため、バックエンドのサーバー(DB, Redis)は外部からの通信を全て遮断しています。
メール送信に使用しているサーバーは、自前で構築したものを使用しています。
Mastodon実行サーバーが落ちていると、502若しくは503エラーページが表示されます。
現在ブロックしているインスタンスはありません。

 Webフォントに Koruri Font を採用しています。

 注意事項
 基本的にメンテナンスは深夜時間帯(01:00～05:00)に行います。
上記時間帯に502や503が表示されたら、メンテナンス作業中だと思って下さい。
 このインスタンスは実験的なインスタンスのため、作業ミス等によりデータが全て消失してしまう場合があります。
上記のことをご理解の上でご利用下さい。
 このインスタンスでは、Google Analyticsなどのアクセス解析や広告の掲載、そして個人情報の収集を一切行っておりませんので、安心してご利用下さい。
 サーバーは、Zabbixを使用して死活監視を行っております。

 ルール
 このサーバーは日本国内にありますので、日本の法令に反しない程度の利用をお願いします。
 このインスタンスでの禁止事項は、下記にまとめてあります。
例としましては、｢出会い系サイトへの誘導｣, ｢犯罪予告｣ 等です。
  なコンテンツは
テキストには｢Content Warning (内容に注意)｣タグを、
画像には｢NSFW (仕事中閲覧注意)｣タグを付けて下さい。
✅ ←このマークは、管理者が承認した方のみの利用とします。利用したい方は、目的を添えてご連絡下さい。
 上記のルールを守っていれさえすれば、何をしても結構です。
(ただし、他人の迷惑にならない程度に)

 アカウントについて
 Mastodon の仕様によりアカウントの削除は出来ません。
 アカウントの停止は、停止を希望するアカウントから管理者宛にご連絡下さい。

 禁止事項
 違反者は発見次第、問答無用で即アカウント停止となりますのでご注意下さい。

日本国の法令に違反する行為
第三者が保有する著作権、商標権その他の権利を侵害する行為、又はそのおそれのある行為
第三者が保有する財産又はプライバシーを侵害する行為、又は侵害するおそれのある行為
第三者に不利益若しくは損害等を与える行為、又はそのおそれのある行為
第三者を不当に差別し若しくは誹謗中傷･侮辱し、第三者への差別を助長し、若しくはその名誉若しくは信用を毀損する行為
第三者の個人情報の売買若しくは譲受に当たる行為、又はそのおそれのある行為
公序良俗に反する行為、若しくはそれを助長する行為、又はそれらのおそれのある行為
事実に反する、又はそのおそれのある情報を提供する行為
第三者が入力した情報を改竄する行為
会員以外の第三者になりすまして会員登録する行為、又は本サービスを利用する行為、又は、情報を送信、受信又は表示する行為
会員ID等を不正に使用する行為、又は、不正目的をもって使用する行為
コンピューターウイルス等有害なプログラムを本サービスを通じて、又は本サービス及び会員登録に関連して使用する行為、又は、提供する行為
本サービス運営を妨げる行為、又は、そのおそれのある行為
本サービスの信用･名誉等を傷つける行為、又はそのおそれのある行為
出会い系サイトに対するリンクを表示又は送信する行為
わいせつ、児童ポルノ若しくは児童虐待に相当する画像、映像、音声若しくは文書等を送信又は表示する行為、又はこれらを収録した媒体を販売する行為、又はその送信、表示、販売を想起させる広告を表示又は送信する行為
未承認医薬品等の広告を行う行為
無限連鎖講(ネズミ講)を開設し、又はこれを勧誘する行為
人の殺害現場の画像等の残虐な情報、動物を殺傷･虐待する画像等の情報、その他社会通念上第三者に著しく嫌悪感を抱かせる情報を送信する行為
人を自殺に誘引又は勧誘する行為、又は第三者に危害の及ぶおそれの高い自殺の手段等を紹介するなどの行為
その行為が上記のいずれかに該当することを知りつつ、その行為を助長する態様又は目的で当該情報が掲載等されたウェブサイトに対するリンクを設置する行為
上記に定めるもののほか、文字、画像、音声その他の方法により、性的な好奇心を煽る情報を掲載する行為、第三者にそれを行わせる行為、又はそれに類似する行為
その他、管理者が不適切と判断する行為


 連絡先
 Mastodon (main): @admin@don.h3z.jp
 Mastodon (sub): @h3zjp@admins.mstdn.social
 Twitter: h3zjp
 また、メールフォームからでも連絡を受け付けています。

 寄付について
 いつでも歓迎です。

## [shadowverse-mstdn.jp](https://shadowverse-mstdn.jp/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=shadowverse-mstdn.jp&view=local)

メンテナンスの一貫でデータベース再構築の作業を行った際にバックアップの適用で不備が発生してしまい、大変恐縮なのですが記録データを消失してしまいました。
改めてサーバーを万全な状態で再構築致しましたので、お手数おかけしますが、ご利用されていた皆様は再度ユーザー登録をお願いいたします。私の不手際のせいで、大変申し訳ありませんでした。

## [imastodon.net](https://imastodon.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=imastodon.net&view=local)
アイマス + マストドン =アイマストドン
アイマスは人生、という皆様のためのサーバです。
アイドルマスターと冠されたものなら範囲に制限はありません。
765、ディアリースターズ、シンデレラガールズ、ミリオンライブ、SideM、ゼノグラシア、KR、その他未だ見知らぬあらゆるアイマスまで。


<details><summary>(more)</summary>メンテナンス予定
現在予定されているメンテナンスはありません
本サーバについて
過負荷等に伴う利用困難について
本サーバは主に私の懐事情の問題からAWS最安のオレゴンリージョン、かつ非常に小さなインスタンスで動作しています。
過負荷に陥ることも多々あると思われますが、何卒ご了承ください。
新規登録について
新規登録の可否はサーバの負荷状況を見ながら随時変更します。
スパム等の判断基準について
本サーバにおいてはスパム等の判断基準を公開しません。
投稿内容は外部からも閲覧することが可能ですので、胸を張れるような使い方をするように努めてください。
登録確認メールが来ない、アカウントを削除したい場合

Twitter: @fusagiko　のDM
mstdn.jp: @fusagiko　のDM
メール: fusagikoあっとまーくimastodon.net
のいずれかへ登録したメールアドレスと共にお問い合わせください。

登録確認等の自動メールはnotify@imastodon.netより届きますので、受信トレイ等に見当たらない場合には検索してみてください。


アカウント削除はメールによるお問合せのみ対応します。
また、アカウントを削除した場合投稿内容はすべて削除されますが、アカウントそのもの、つまり「登録していた」という事実は残りますのでその点ご了承ください。

皆様へお願い
本サーバは単独の個人が構築ならびに運用を行っていますので、本サーバについて他の法人、団体へのお問合せはおやめください。
</details>

Email: [fusagikoあっとまーくimastodon.net](mailto:fusagikoあっとまーくimastodon.net)

Admin: [@fusagiko@imastodon.net](https://imastodon.net/@fusagiko)

## [sns.gdgd.jp.net](https://sns.gdgd.jp.net/about/more) [(preview)](http://www.unmung.com/mastoview?url=sns.gdgd.jp.net&view=local)
ますとどんです。

ぐだぐだと運用します。
このインスタンスについてに書かれているやくそくを守って利用してください

<details><summary>(more)</summary>やくそく
インスタンスについて

日本に設置されています。日本の法律を守ってください
短時間での大量投稿（バルス）はサーバの負荷になるのでやめてください
無差別ブースト・無差別フォロー・無差別ファボもサーバの負荷になるのでやめてください
ストレージの容量も有限なので大きなファイルは外部サービスを活用してください
メンテナンスのためにサービスが止まることがあります
事故によってデータが消えることがあります
管理者が継続不能と判断した場合このインスタンスは予告なく終了します
やくそくを読んでませんでした、は通用しません

アカウントについて

データのエクスポートを時々してください
警察や裁判所の依頼があった場合情報提供をします
アカウントの停止をしたい場合はDMを送ってください。
アカウントの停止をしてもアカウントが使えなくなるだけで情報は残ります
アカウントの削除は行いません

通報について

必ず第三者から見て正当な理由がある場合のみ通報してください
通報の際はコメント欄に状況を詳しく書いてください
SILENCEかSUSPENDかは管理者が決めます
自分がブロックするだけじゃ済まなさそうな場合は積極的に通報してください

ボットについて

ボットを運用するときは必ずUnlistedで発言させてください
Publicで発言しているボットはSILENCEします

さいごに
みんなへいわにぐだぐだしよう


サーバちゃんについて
FUJITSU PRIMERGY TX1310 M1というサーバです
ますとどん以外にも動かしているものがあるので
処理能力をフル活用することはできないです

CPU: Celeron G1820(2.70GHz)
RAM: 4GB→8GB（すごーい！）

ひとこと
ぐだぐだと特にこだわりなく進行します。
ある程度のユーザーを抱えたので速度維持を第一目標とします
</details>

Email: [admin@gdgd.jp.net](mailto:admin@gdgd.jp.net)

Admin: [@lin@sns.gdgd.jp.net](https://sns.gdgd.jp.net/@lin)
